    OnInsert=BEGIN
               // Start PA032225
               IF ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnInsert,ExitPointSetupG.Type::Pre,'') THEN
                 EXIT;
               // Stop PA032225

               // Start PA038448.67906
               IF Type <> Type::" " THEN
                 TESTFIELD("No.");
               // Stop PA038448.67906
               // Start PA033019
               CheckUserRights(ModificationTypeG::Insert);
               // Stop PA033019
               LOCKTABLE;
               ServHdrG.GET("Document Type","Document No.");
               StatusCheckFunction(FALSE);
               // Start EU.0195242
               "Order Date" := ServHdrG."Order Date";
               IF (Type = Type::" ") AND ("Bill-to Customer No." = '') THEN BEGIN
                 ServHdrG."No." := '';
                 VALIDATE("Bill-to Customer No.", ServHdrG."Bill-to Customer No.");
                 ServHdrG.GET("Document Type","Document No.");
               END;
               // Start PA034249
               IF NOT SkipSrvLineCustUpdateG THEN
                 SrvCustSplitMgmtG.UpdServLineCust_ServLine(ServHdrG, Rec, FALSE, SkipSrvCustUpdateG, FALSE, FALSE);
               // Stop EU.0195242
               // Stop PA034249
               IF (Type <> Type::" ") AND ("No." > '') AND "Value Increasing Measure" THEN BEGIN
                 CLEAR(ServMgmtG);
                 ServMgmtG.ServOptionMatching(Rec,TRUE,TRUE);
               END;
               // Start EU.0195242
               // Stop EU.0195242
               PresentRecG.GETTABLE(Rec);
               WarrMgmtG.InsertFunction(PresentRecG, ServHdrG."Make Code");
               IF VehServContrG.ValidContrOfServCustFind(ServHdrG.VIN, ServHdrG."Document Type", ServHdrG."No.", ServHdrG."Completion Date") THEN
                 ServContrMgtG.FindingsInsert(PresentRecG, VehServContrG."Serv. Contract Cust. No.");
               // Start PA032225
               // Start PA033478
               // Start PA035208
               VALIDATE("Last Changed");
               // Stop PA035208

               // Stop PA033478
               ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnInsert,ExitPointSetupG.Type::Post,'');
               // Stop PA032225
             END;

    OnModify=VAR
               ExRecordL@3245300 : Record 5025625;
             BEGIN
               // Start PA032225
               IF ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnModify,ExitPointSetupG.Type::Pre,'') THEN
                 EXIT;
               // Stop PA032225

               // Start PA038448.67906
               IF Type <> Type::" " THEN
                 TESTFIELD("No.");
               // Stop PA038448.67906
               // Start PA033019
               CheckUserRights(ModificationTypeG::Modify);
               // Stop PA033019

               StatusCheckFunction(FALSE);
               // Stop PA036765
               // Start EU.0032453
               IF NOT ExRecordL.GET("Document Type", "Document No.", "Line No.") THEN
                 ExRecordL.INIT;
               ShoppingCartMgtG.WriteServiceLineQuantityModificationLostSaleData(
                 Rec, (Quantity - ExRecordL.Quantity), (Amount - ExRecordL.Amount), ("Amount Including VAT" - ExRecordL."Amount Including VAT"));
               // Stop EU.0032453
               // Stop PA036765.29110
               // Start PA034249
               IF NOT SkipSrvLineCustUpdateG THEN BEGIN
                 GetServHeader();

               END;

               IF (Type = Type::" ") AND ("Bill-to Customer No." = '') THEN BEGIN
                 ServHdrG.GET("Document Type","Document No.");
                 VALIDATE("Bill-to Customer No.", ServHdrG."Bill-to Customer No.");
               END;
               // Start PA034057
               // Stop PA034057
               IF (Type <> Type::" ") AND ("No." > '') THEN BEGIN
                 CLEAR(ServMgmtG);
                 ServMgmtG.ServOptionMatching(Rec,FALSE,FALSE);
               END;
               // Start PA034057
               // Start PA034134
               UserSessionUnitG.SetServLineModified(TRUE);
               // Stop PA034134
               // Start PA036950
               IF UserSessionUnitG.TimeManLicensePermissionCheck(FALSE) AND ("Resource No." <> '') THEN BEGIN
               // Update Service Resource Assignment
                 IF ServResourceMgntG.Check4ServResPortionsUpdate(xRec,Rec) THEN
                   ServResourceMgntG.UpdServResPortion_ServLine(Rec);
               // Stop PA034057
               END;
               // Stop PA036950

               PresentRecG.GETTABLE(Rec);
               PreviousRecG.GETTABLE(xRec);
               WarrMgmtG.ModifyFunctionForFindings(PreviousRecG, PresentRecG, ServHdrG."Make Code", '');
               IF VehServContrG.ValidContrOfServCustFind(ServHdrG.VIN, ServHdrG."Document Type", ServHdrG."No.", ServHdrG."Completion Date") THEN

               // Start PA032225
               // Start PA033478
               // Start PA035208
               VALIDATE("Last Changed");
               // Stop PA035208
               // Start PA042666.86931
               // Start EU.0052165
               IF NOT GetServiceJob() THEN
               // Stop EU.0052165
                 ServJobG.INIT;
               IF ServJobG."Includes Fixed Price" THEN

               // Stop PA042666.86931
               // Start EU.0095631

               FindStatus(FALSE);
               // Stop EU.0095631

               // Stop PA033478
               ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnModify,ExitPointSetupG.Type::Post,'');
               // Stop PA032225
             END;

                  ArchServHdrG."Reason for Archiving"::Post,
                  ArchServHdrG."Reason for Archiving"::"Delete Completed Document"])
               THEN
               // Stop PA035942
               // Stop PA034523.18878
                 StatusCheckFunction(FALSE);

               // Stop EU.0210554.213486

               // Stop PA034057

               // Stop EU.0210554.211799

               // Stop EU.0195242
               // Start EU.0154107.154767

               // Stop EU.0154107.154767

               PresentRecG.GETTABLE(Rec);
               WarrMgmtG.DeleteFunctionForFindings(PresentRecG, ServHdrG."Make Code", 'Table');

               // Start PA036188

                 SetAppointmentLine(Rec, xRec, ActionG::Delete);
               // Stop EU.0117766
               // Stop PA036188
               // Start EU.0098776
               ServiceLineTempL := Rec;
               ServiceLineTempL.Quantity := ServiceLineTempL."Outstanding Quantity";
               OutstandingAmtWithoutTaxesL := CalcOriginalAmount(ServiceLineTempL);

               // Start EU.0104306
               IF Quantity <> "Quantity Invoiced" THEN

                 // Stop EU.0104306
               // Stop PA042968
               // Start PA032225
               // Start PA034291.I002269
               // Stop PA034291.I002269
               // Start EU.0036239
               // Start EU.0188843.192508

    { 15  ;   ;Quantity            ;Decimal       ;OnValidate=VAR
                                                                ItemBinL@1109400001 : Record 5028749;
                                                                ItemL@1109400002 : Record 27;
                                                                CustL@1002 : Record 18;
                                                                UserLocationL@1109400000 : Record 5028664;
                                                                OldServLineL@1109400007 : Record 5025625;
                                                                ServLineCustL@1000 : Record 5025639;
                                                                ExServLineCustTempL@1001 : TEMPORARY Record 5025639;
                                                                ServLineCustSplitUpL@1004 : Record 5045370;
                                                                CodedPartValueL@1109400003 : Record 5205352;
                                                                RecRefL@1109400004 : RecordRef;
                                                                VehicleToDeliverCheckL@1117700000 : Codeunit 5028661;
                                                                UnitPriceOldL@1109400006 : Decimal;
                                                                FixedPriceToDeleteL@1119418000 : Boolean;
                                                                RestoreOldJobNoL@1055600 : Boolean;
                                                                TransactionStartedHereL@10430600 : Boolean;
                                                                CustomnerSplitHasChangedL@1003 : Boolean;
                                                              BEGIN
                                                                // Start PA038850
                                                                IF ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnValidate, ExitPointSetupG.Type::Pre, FIELDNAME(Quantity)) THEN
                                                                  EXIT;
                                                                // Stop PA038850

                                                                // Start PA042806
                                                                OldServLineL := Rec;
                                                                // Stop PA042806
                                                                // Start PA036765.29110
                                                                StatusCheckFunction(TRUE);
                                                                // Stop PA036765.29110
                                                                // Start PA045326
                                                                IF Quantity <> xRec.Quantity THEN
                                                                  IF ("Document Type" = xRec."Document Type") AND
                                                                     ("Document No." = xRec."Document No.") AND
                                                                     ("Line No." = xRec."Line No.")
                                                                  THEN
                                                                    CheckAttachedToServiceOrder(FIELDCAPTION(Quantity));
                                                                // Stop PA045326
                                                                // Start EU.0104306
                                                                "Quantity (Base)" := CalcBaseQty(Quantity);
                                                                "Qty. (Hour)" := CalcHoursQty(Quantity);
                                                                IF (Quantity * "Quantity Shipped" < 0) OR (ABS(Quantity) < ABS("Quantity Shipped")) THEN
                                                                  FIELDERROR(Quantity,STRSUBSTNO(C_INC013,FIELDCAPTION("Quantity Shipped")));
                                                                IF ("Quantity (Base)" * "Qty. Shipped (Base)" < 0) OR (ABS("Quantity (Base)") < ABS("Qty. Shipped (Base)")) THEN
                                                                  FIELDERROR("Quantity (Base)",STRSUBSTNO(C_INC013,FIELDCAPTION("Qty. Shipped (Base)")));
                                                                IF ("Qty. (Hour)" * "Qty. Shipped (Hour)" < 0) OR (ABS("Qty. (Hour)") < ABS("Qty. Shipped (Hour)")) THEN
                                                                  FIELDERROR("Qty. (Hour)",STRSUBSTNO(C_INC013,FIELDCAPTION("Qty. Shipped (Hour)")));
                                                                InitOutstanding();
                                                                InitQtyToShip();
                                                                IF ABS("Outstanding Qty. (Base)") < ABS("Reserved Qty. (Base)") THEN
                                                                  ERROR(C_INC014,FIELDCAPTION("Reserved Qty. (Base)"));
                                                                // Stop EU.0104306
                                                                // Start PA033019
                                                                IF CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO(Quantity) THEN BEGIN
                                                                  CheckUserRights(ModificationTypeG::Modify);
                                                                // Stop PA033019
                                                                // Start PA042806
                                                                // Start PA040497
                                                                // Start EU.0104306
                                                                  IF "Service Job No." > 0 THEN BEGIN
                                                                // Stop PA040497
                                                                    IF NOT CheckSplittCalculation(FIELDNO(Quantity),TRUE) THEN
                                                                // Start EU.0034979
                                                                      RestoreOldJobNoL := TRUE;
                                                                // Stop EU.0034979
                                                                // Start EU.0128664.129214
                                                                    ServLineCustInvValidation();
                                                                    // Check, if one of the Split Customers is not added in the Job Customer Split setup and has Invoiced quantity.
                                                                    ServLineCustL.RESET;
                                                                    ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Document Type", "Document Type");
                                                                    ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Document No.", "Document No.");
                                                                    ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Document Line No.", "Line No.");
                                                                    ServLineCustL.SETFILTER("Quantity Invoiced", '<>0');
                                                                    IF ServLineCustL.FINDSET THEN
                                                                      REPEAT
                                                                        RestoreOldJobNoL := TRUE;
                                                                        IF NOT ServLineCustSplitUpL.GET("Document Type", "Document No.", "Service Job No.", ServLineCustL."Bill-to Customer No.") THEN
                                                                          ERROR(C_INC_LineSplitInvocePosedAlready, "Line No.",
                                                                            STRSUBSTNO('%1 %2', ServLineCustL."Bill-to Customer No.", ServLineCustL."Bill-to Name"),
                                                                            STRSUBSTNO('%1=%2', ServLineCustL.FIELDCAPTION("Quantity Invoiced"), ServLineCustL."Quantity Invoiced"));
                                                                      UNTIL ServLineCustL.NEXT = 0;
                                                                  END;
                                                                // Stop EU.0128664.129214
                                                                // Stop EU.0104306
                                                                // Stop PA042806
                                                                // Stop PA033463
                                                                  IsDepositPosition();
                                                                // Start PA033463
                                                                END;
                                                                // Stop PA033463

                                                                //If the quantity changes and the line belongs to a package, check if a line lock has been defined for the package
                                                                // Then the quantity cannot be changed (anymore)
                                                                IF ("Package No." > '') AND (Quantity <> xRec.Quantity) THEN BEGIN
                                                                  CheckPackageLock(FIELDCAPTION(Quantity));
                                                                  FixedPriceToDeleteL := TRUE;
                                                                END;
                                                                IF NOT ServLine2G.GET("Document Type","Document No.","Line No.") THEN
                                                                  CLEAR(ServLine2G);
                                                                IF Quantity <> ServLine2G.Quantity THEN BEGIN
                                                                  IF Type = Type::"Ext. Service" THEN BEGIN

                                                                      END;
                                                                    END;

                                                                  ServLineCustL.RESET;
                                                                  ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Document Type", "Document Type");
                                                                  ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Document No.", "Document No.");
                                                                  ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Document Line No.", "Line No.");
                                                                  IF ServLineCustL.FINDSET THEN

                                                                      ExServLineCustTempL.INSERT;

                                                                // Start PA044674

                                                                // Stop PA044674
                                                                END;
                                                                // Stop EU.0104306

                                                                  DeleteFixedPrice();
                                                                CheckServOptionStatus(Rec,CurrFieldNo,FIELDNO(Quantity));

                                                                    VALIDATE(Amount,"Fixed Price");

                                                                      (UnitPriceOldL * Quantity) - (UnitPriceOldL * Quantity * "Cust./Item Disc. %" / 100) - "Fixed Price";
                                                                    "Line Discount %" :=
                                                                      ("Line Discount Amount" * 100) / ((UnitPriceOldL * Quantity) - (UnitPriceOldL * Quantity * "Cust./Item Disc. %") / 100);

                                                                  END;

                                                                // Start PA032600
                                                                // Stop PA032600
                                                                  END;
                                                                END;

                                                                // Start EU.0104306

                                                                // Stop EU.0104306
                                                                // Stop PA040732
                                                                // Start PA032450

                                                                // Stop PA032450

                                                                    IF ServLineCustL.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
                                                                      REPEAT
                                                                        IF NOT ExServLineCustTempL.GET(ServLineCustL.RECORDID) THEN
                                                                          CustomnerSplitHasChangedL := TRUE
                                                                        ELSE BEGIN

                                                                          ServLineCustL."Amount Invoiced" := ExServLineCustTempL."Amount Invoiced";
                                                                          ServLineCustL."Amount Including VAT Invoiced" := ExServLineCustTempL."Amount Including VAT Invoiced";

                                                                          CustomnerSplitHasChangedL := CustomnerSplitHasChangedL OR (ServLineCustL."Consider Price Calculation" AND (ServLineCustL."Line Discount %" <> ExServLineCustTempL."Line Discount %"));

                                                                      UNTIL ServLineCustL.NEXT = 0;
                                                                      IF CustomnerSplitHasChangedL THEN
                                                                        MESSAGE(C_INC_CustomerSplitHasChanged, "Service Job No.")

                                                                    END;
                                                                  END;

                                                                RunOrderLineRounding(TransactionStartedHereL, xRec);
                                                                // Stop EU.0104306

                                                                // Start PA038850
                                                                ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnValidate, ExitPointSetupG.Type::Post,FIELDNAME(Quantity));
                                                                // Stop PA038850

                                                                ELSE

                                                                IF ("Qty. to Invoice" * Quantity < 0) OR (ABS("Qty. to Invoice") > ABS(MaxQtyToInvoice)) THEN
                                                                  ERROR(C_INC015,MaxQtyToInvoice);
                                                                IF ("Qty. to Invoice (Base)" * "Quantity (Base)" < 0) OR (ABS("Qty. to Invoice (Base)") > ABS(MaxQtyToInvoiceBase)) THEN
                                                                  ERROR(C_INC016,MaxQtyToInvoiceBase);

                                                                   (ServOptionL.GET("Document Type","Document No.","Service Job No.","Option Code")) AND
                                                                   (NOT ServOptionL.Post)
                                                                THEN

    { 18  ;   ;Qty. to Ship        ;Decimal       ;OnValidate=VAR
                                                                ServLineL@1109400000 : Record 5025625;

                                                                ResQtyOnStockL@36900 : Decimal;
                                                              BEGIN
                                                                // Start PA036842
                                                                StatusCheckFunction(TRUE);
                                                                // Stop PA036842
                                                                IF (CurrFieldNo <> 0) AND ("Qty. to Ship" <> 0) THEN
                                                                  IF NOT (Type IN [Type::"G/L Account", Type::Item, Type::Labor, Type::"Ext. Service"]) THEN
                                                                    TESTFIELD("Qty. to Ship", 0);

                                                                  IF ("Qty. to Ship" <> xRec."Qty. to Ship") AND ("Qty. to Ship" <> "Outstanding Quantity") THEN
                                                                    ERROR(C_INC045);

                                                                // Start EU.0045397.45399

                                                                // Stop EU.0032451

                                                                  IF CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO("Qty. to Ship") THEN BEGIN
                                                                    IF ResQtyOnStockL < "Qty. to Ship" THEN BEGIN

                                                                        ERROR(C_INC_ResItemNotOnInventory, "No.")
                                                                      ELSE

                                                                    END;
                                                                // Start EU.0017374
                                                                  END ELSE BEGIN

                                                                  END;
                                                                // Stop EU.0017374
                                                                END;
                                                                // Stop EU.0000369
                                                                IF "Qty. to Ship" = "Outstanding Quantity" THEN
                                                                  InitQtyToShip
                                                                ELSE BEGIN
                                                                  "Qty. to Ship (Base)" := CalcBaseQty("Qty. to Ship");
                                                                  InitQtyToInv();
                                                                END;
                                                                IF ("Qty. to Ship" * Quantity < 0) OR
                                                                   (ABS("Qty. to Ship") > ABS("Outstanding Quantity")) OR
                                                                   (Quantity * "Outstanding Quantity" < 0)
                                                                THEN
                                                                  ERROR(C_INC017,"Outstanding Quantity");
                                                                IF ("Qty. to Ship (Base)" * "Quantity (Base)" < 0) OR
                                                                   (ABS("Qty. to Ship (Base)") > ABS("Outstanding Qty. (Base)")) OR
                                                                   ("Quantity (Base)" * "Outstanding Qty. (Base)" < 0)
                                                                THEN
                                                                  ERROR(C_INC018,"Outstanding Qty. (Base)");

                                                                IF (CurrFieldNo <> 0) AND
                                                                   ("Document Type" = "Document Type"::Order) AND
                                                                   (Type = Type::Item) AND ("No." > '') AND
                                                                // Start EU.0090125
                                                                // Start EU.0091263
                                                                   ("Qty. to Ship" > 0) AND ("Outstanding Quantity" > 0) AND GUIALLOWED AND
                                                                // Stop EU.0091263
                                                                   ("Qty. to Ship" <> ResQtyOnStockL)
                                                                // Stop EU.0090125

                                                                  VehicleToDeliverCheckG.CheckServLine(Rec);

                                                                      ERROR(C_INC068,ItemBinL."Location Code" );

                                                                      VALIDATE("Location Code",ServLineL."Location Code");
                                                                    IF "Bin Code" <> ServLineL."Bin Code" THEN
                                                                      VALIDATE("Bin Code",ServLineL."Bin Code");
                                                                    "Open Autom. Stock Info. Page" := FALSE;
                                                                    UserSessionUnitG.SetServiceLine(Rec);
                                                                  END;
                                                                END;
                                                                // Start PA032800
                                                                CheckNegativeStock;
                                                                // Stop PA032800
                                                                // Start PA042806
                                                                // Start PA044975
                                                                // Start EU.0017374
                                                                IF CurrFieldNo <> 0 THEN
                                                                  UpdateFieldInAttachedLines(FIELDNO("Qty. to Ship"));
                                                                // Stop PA044975
                                                                // Stop PA042806
                                                                UpdateQtytoInv();
                                                                ShipPropMgtG.CreateAutomaticLine(Rec, FirstReservationDateL, ResQtyOnStockL);
                                                                // Stop EU.0017374
                                                              END;

    { 29  ;   ;Amount              ;Decimal       ;OnValidate=VAR
                                                                TransactionStartedHereL@10430600 : Boolean;
                                                              BEGIN
                                                                // Start PA037116
                                                                IF NOT CollectionCodeunitG.NegativeQtyCheck(Quantity,Amount,SymbolTextG) THEN
                                                                  ERROR(C_INC_NegativeQuantity,FIELDCAPTION(Amount),xRec.Amount,Amount,SymbolTextG,FIELDCAPTION(Quantity));
                                                                // Stop PA037116
                                                                // Start PA036842
                                                                StatusCheckFunction(TRUE);
                                                                // Stop PA036842
                                                                TESTFIELD(Type);
                                                                // Start PA040480
                                                                // Start EU.0104306
                                                                IF Amount <> 0 THEN BEGIN
                                                                  TESTFIELD(Quantity);
                                                                  TESTFIELD("Unit Price");
                                                                END;
                                                                // Stop PA040480
                                                                // Start EU.0200720.199667
                                                                IF CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO(Amount) THEN
                                                                // Start EU.0210554.211581
                                                                  IF Amount <> xRec.Amount THEN BEGIN
                                                                    CheckServiceInvoiceExists();
                                                                    UserSalesPriceChangePermG.ServiceLinePriceChangeBlocked(Rec, FALSE);
                                                                  END;
                                                                // Stop EU.0210554.211581
                                                                // Stop EU.0200720.199667
                                                                // Start PA032600
                                                                // Stop PA032600
                                                                // Stop EU.0104306
                                                                // By a change of the amount and package link of the line, check if the package contains a line lock
                                                                // Then, the amount may not be changed (any longer)
                                                                IF ("Package No." > '') AND (Amount <> xRec.Amount) THEN BEGIN
                                                                  CheckPackageLock(FIELDCAPTION(Amount));
                                                                  DeleteFixedPrice();
                                                                END;
                                                                // Start PA036413.26607
                                                                IF ("Fixed Price" <> 0) AND (CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO(Amount)) AND (Amount <> xRec.Amount) THEN BEGIN
                                                                  IF NOT CONFIRM(C_INC025,FALSE) THEN BEGIN
                                                                    Amount := xRec.Amount;
                                                                    EXIT;
                                                                  END;
                                                                  "Fixed Price" := 0;
                                                                END;
                                                                // Stop PA036413.26607
                                                                IF ("No Charge") AND (CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO(Amount)) AND (Amount <> xRec.Amount) THEN
                                                                  IF NOT CONFIRM(C_INC026,FALSE) THEN BEGIN
                                                                    Amount := xRec.Amount;
                                                                    EXIT;
                                                                  END;
                                                                // Start EU.0104306
                                                                TransactionStartedHereL := SetProcessTriggeredFromField(FIELDNO(Amount));
                                                                // Stop EU.0104306

                                                                GetServHeader();
                                                                // Start PA034053.I000514
                                                                Amount := ROUND(Amount,CurrencyG."Amount Rounding Precision");

                                                                // Start PA036544
                                                                IF NOT ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnValidate,ExitPointSetupG.Type::"Condition 1",FIELDNAME(Amount)) THEN
                                                                // Stop PA036544
                                                                  CASE "VAT Calculation Type" OF
                                                                    "VAT Calculation Type"::"Normal VAT",
                                                                    "VAT Calculation Type"::"Reverse Charge VAT":
                                                                      BEGIN
                                                                // Start PA033352
                                                                        "VAT Base Amount" := ROUND(Amount * (1 - ServHdrG."VAT Base Discount %" / 100),CurrencyG."Amount Rounding Precision");
                                                                        "Amount Including VAT" := ROUND(Amount + "VAT Base Amount" * "VAT %" / 100,CurrencyG."Amount Rounding Precision");
                                                                // Stop PA033352
                                                                      END;
                                                                    "VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax":
                                                                      BEGIN
                                                                        IF (Amount = 0) OR (Amount <= (Quantity * "Unit Cost")) THEN
                                                                          "VAT Base Amount" := 0
                                                                        ELSE
                                                                // Start PA033352
                                                                          "VAT Base Amount" := ROUND((Amount - (Quantity * "Unit Cost")) *
                                                                            (1 - ServHdrG."VAT Base Discount %" / 100),CurrencyG."Amount Rounding Precision");
                                                                        "Amount Including VAT" := ROUND(Amount + "VAT Base Amount" * "VAT %" / 100,CurrencyG."Amount Rounding Precision");
                                                                // Stop PA033352
                                                                      END;
                                                                    "VAT Calculation Type"::"Exch. Parts Tax":
                                                                      BEGIN
                                                                // Start PA042968
                                                                        OriginalAmountG := CalcOriginalAmount(Rec);
                                                                // Stop PA042968
                                                                // Start PA033352
                                                                        "VAT Base Amount" := ROUND(Amount * (1 - ServHdrG."VAT Base Discount %" / 100),CurrencyG."Amount Rounding Precision");
                                                                        "Exch. Parts Tax Base" := ROUND(OriginalAmountG * "Exch. Parts Tax %" / 100,CurrencyG."Amount Rounding Precision");
                                                                        "Exch. Parts Tax Amount" := ROUND("Exch. Parts Tax Base" * "Exch. Parts VAT %" / 100,CurrencyG."Amount Rounding Precision");
                                                                        "Amount Including VAT" := ROUND(Amount + "VAT Base Amount" * "VAT %" / 100 +
                                                                          "Exch. Parts Tax Amount",CurrencyG."Amount Rounding Precision");
                                                                // Stop PA033352
                                                                      END;
                                                                    "VAT Calculation Type"::"Full VAT":
                                                                      IF Amount <> 0 THEN
                                                                        FIELDERROR(Amount,STRSUBSTNO(C_INC046,FIELDCAPTION("VAT Calculation Type"),"VAT Calculation Type"));
                                                                    "VAT Calculation Type"::"Sales Tax":
                                                                      BEGIN
                                                                        ServHdrG.TESTFIELD("VAT Base Discount %",0);
                                                                        "VAT Base Amount" := ROUND(Amount,CurrencyG."Amount Rounding Precision");

                                                                // Start PA036544
                                                                        ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnValidate,ExitPointSetupG.Type::"Inside 1",FIELDNAME(Amount));
                                                                // Stop PA036544

                                                                        "Amount Including VAT" := Amount +
                                                                // Start EU.0104321
                                                                          CalcSalesTaxG.CalculateTax(
                                                                            "Tax Area Code", "Tax Group Code", "Tax Liable", ServHdrG."Posting Date",
                                                                            "VAT Base Amount", Quantity, ServHdrG."Currency Factor");
                                                                // Stop EU.0104321
                                                                        IF "VAT Base Amount" <> 0 THEN
                                                                          "VAT %" := ROUND(100 * ("Amount Including VAT" - "VAT Base Amount") / "VAT Base Amount",0.00001)
                                                                        ELSE BEGIN
                                                                          "VAT %" := 0;
                                                                        END;
                                                                // Start EU.0104321
                                                                        "Amount Including VAT" := ROUND("Amount Including VAT", CurrencyG."Amount Rounding Precision");
                                                                // Stop EU.0104321
                                                                      END;
                                                                  END;

                                                                // Start PA036544
                                                                ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnValidate,ExitPointSetupG.Type::"Inside 2",FIELDNAME(Amount));
                                                                // Stop PA036544

                                                                // Start PA042968
                                                                OriginalAmountG := CalcOriginalAmount(Rec);
                                                                // Start PA041789
                                                                "Line Discount Amount" := OriginalAmountG - Amount;
                                                                // Start EU.0138596
                                                                VALIDATE("Autom. Rounding Disc. %", 0);
                                                                // Stop EU.0138596
                                                                IF OriginalAmountG <> 0 THEN
                                                                  "Line Discount %" := ROUND("Line Discount Amount" / OriginalAmountG * 100,0.00001)
                                                                // Stop PA042968
                                                                ELSE
                                                                  "Line Discount %" := 0;
                                                                // Stop PA041789
                                                                // Stop PA034053.I000514
                                                                // Start EU.0104306
                                                                // Stop EU.0104306
                                                                InitOutstandingAmount();

                                                                CheckDiscount(FIELDCAPTION("Line Discount %"));
                                                                // Start EU.0104306
                                                                // Stop EU.0104306
                                                                // Start PA043220
                                                                IF NOT RecordIsTemporalG THEN
                                                                  VehiclePriceCalcG.ServPriceCalcChange(Rec,ServHdrG);
                                                                // Stop PA043220

                                                                // Start EU.0104306
                                                                RunOrderLineRounding(TransactionStartedHereL, xRec);
                                                                // Stop EU.0104306

                                                                // Start PA036544
                                                                ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnValidate,ExitPointSetupG.Type::Post,FIELDNAME(Amount));
                                                                // Stop PA036544
                                                              END;

                                                   CaptionML=ENU=Amount;
                                                   BlankZero=Yes;
                                                   Description=PA040837;
                                                   AutoFormatType=1;
                                                   AutoFormatExpr="Currency Code" }

                                                                 ELSE IF (Type=CONST(Labor)) "Unit of Measure".Code WHERE (Code=FIELD(Unit of Measure Code))
                                                                 ELSE "Unit of Measure";

                                                                IF CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO("Unit of Measure Code") THEN
                                                                  IF ("Additional Item" <> "Additional Item"::" ") AND ("Quantity Multiplier" <> 0) THEN
                                                                    ERROR(C_INC041,FIELDCAPTION("Unit of Measure Code"));
                                                                IF (Type = Type::Labor) AND ("No." > '') AND (CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO("Unit of Measure Code")) THEN BEGIN

    { 5025352;;Service Job No.     ;Integer       ;TableRelation="Service Job Line"."Line No." WHERE (Document Type=FIELD(Document Type),

                                                   OnValidate=BEGIN
                                                                // Start PA036544

                                                                  EXIT;
                                                                // Stop PA036544

                                                                // Stop PA036842

                                                                // Stop PA042806
                                                                IF "Service Job No." <> 0 THEN BEGIN
                                                                  IF CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO("Service Job No.") THEN
                                                                    "Service Job No." := ServJobG.JobNoSearch("Document Type","Document No.","Service Job No.");

                                                                // Stop EU.0052165

                                                                // Stop PA043750.95994

                                                                      IF "Bill-to Customer No." <> ServJobG."Bill-to Customer No." THEN

                                                                // Stop PA043822
                                                                  ServiceJobNoOnValidate(CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO("Service Job No."));

    { 5025362;;Package No.         ;Code20        ;TableRelation="Service Package Line"."Package No." WHERE (Document Type=FIELD(Document Type),
                                                                                                             Document No.=FIELD(Document No.));
                                                   OnValidate=VAR
                                                                MakeL@1109400005 : Record 12;
                                                                ServPkgLineL@1109400001 : Record 5025635;
                                                                PackageL@1109400003 : Record 5025610;
                                                                TextL@1109400000 : Text[260];
                                                              BEGIN
                                                                // Start PA036842
                                                                StatusCheckFunction(TRUE);
                                                                // Stop PA036842
                                                                // Start EU.0052165
                                                                // EU.0188843.192865
                                                                IF (CurrFieldNo > 0) AND (("Package No." <> xRec."Package No.") OR ("Package Version No." = 0)) THEN BEGIN
                                                                // EU.0188843.192865
                                                                  IF ServPkgLineG.GET("Document Type","Document No.",xRec."Package No.",xRec."Package Version No.") THEN
                                                                    IF ServPkgLineG."Line Lock" THEN
                                                                      ERROR(C_INC065,FIELDCAPTION("Package No."), xRec."Package No.");
                                                                  GetServHeader();
                                                                  IF "Package No." = '' THEN BEGIN
                                                                    // Package no. was removed from current line so reset a Package Warranty Bill-to Customer back to the regular Order Bill to.
                                                                    "Package Version No." := 0;
                                                                    IF ServPkgLineL.GET("Document Type", "Document No.", xRec."Package No.", xRec."Package Version No.") THEN
                                                                      IF MakeL.GET(ServPkgLineL."Make Code") THEN
                                                                        IF "Bill-to Customer No." = MakeL."Factory Warranty Customer" THEN
                                                                          IF "Service Job No." = 0 THEN BEGIN
                                                                            IF "Bill-to Customer No." <> ServHdrG."Bill-to Customer No." THEN
                                                                              VALIDATE("Bill-to Customer No.", ServHdrG."Bill-to Customer No.");
                                                                          END ELSE
                                                                            IF GetServiceJob() THEN
                                                                              IF "Bill-to Customer No." <> ServJobG."Bill-to Customer No." THEN
                                                                                VALIDATE("Bill-to Customer No.", ServJobG."Bill-to Customer No.");
                                                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                                                    CheckPackageLock(FIELDCAPTION("Package No."));
                                                                    IF xRec."Package No." > '' THEN
                                                                      "Package Version No." := 0;
                                                                    ServPkgLineL.RESET;
                                                                    ServPkgLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
                                                                    ServPkgLineL.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
                                                                    ServPkgLineL.SETRANGE("Package No.","Package No.");
                                                                    ServPkgLineL.SETRANGE("Package Version No.", "Package Version No.");
                                                                    IF ServPkgLineL.ISEMPTY THEN
                                                                      "Package Version No." := 0;
                                                                    ServPkgLineL.SETRANGE("Package Version No.");
                                                                    IF "Package Version No." = 0 THEN
                                                                      IF ServPkgLineL.COUNT > 1 THEN BEGIN
                                                                        TextL := "Package No.";
                                                                        IF NOT PackageNoOnLookup(TextL,"Package Version No.") THEN
                                                                          ERROR('');
                                                                        "Package No." := TextL;
                                                                      END ELSE
                                                                        IF ServPkgLineL.FINDFIRST THEN
                                                                          "Package Version No." := ServPkgLineL."Package Version No.";
                                                                    VALIDATE("Package Version No.");
                                                                // Start EU.0051613
                                                                // Stop EU.0052165
                                                                    ServPkgLineL.GET("Document Type","Document No.", "Package No.", "Package Version No.");
                                                                    PackageL.GET(ServPkgLineL."Make Code", ServPkgLineL."Package No.");
                                                                    IF PackageL."Warranty Package" THEN BEGIN
                                                                      MakeL.GET(PackageL."Make Code");
                                                                      IF ("Bill-to Customer No." <> MakeL."Factory Warranty Customer") THEN BEGIN
                                                                        IF GUIALLOWED THEN
                                                                          IF NOT CanModifyCustSplit(MakeL."Factory Warranty Customer") THEN
                                                                            IF NOT CONFIRM(C_INC_PackageChangesBillToCust, TRUE, PackageL.TABLECAPTION) THEN
                                                                              ERROR('');
                                                                        VALIDATE("Bill-to Customer No.", MakeL."Factory Warranty Customer");
                                                                      END;
                                                                    END;
                                                                // Start EU.0052165
                                                                  END;
                                                                // Stop EU.0052165
                                                                END;
                                                              END;

                                                   CaptionML=ENU=Package No.;
                                                   AutoFormatExpr='JMD' }

                                                                "Manual VAT Amount" := ("VAT Amount" <> "Calculated VAT Amount");

    { 5045212;;Serv. Contract Type ;Code20        ;OnValidate=VAR
                                                                VehServContractL@1109400000 : Record 5061005;
                                                                PresentRecL@1117700000 : RecordRef;
                                                                ServContractMgmtL@1117700001 : Codeunit 5061000;
                                                                UnitPriceOldL@17722600 : Decimal;
                                                              BEGIN
                                                                // Start PA036842
                                                                StatusCheckFunction(TRUE);
                                                                // Stop PA036842
                                                                IF CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO("Serv. Contract Type") THEN
                                                                  IF ("Serv. Contract Type" <> xRec."Serv. Contract Type") AND ("Service Job No." <> 0) THEN
                                                                // Start EU.0052165
                                                                    ERROR(C_INC_FieldChangeCanBeDoneInTheJobOnly,
                                                                      TABLECAPTION,
                                                                      STRSUBSTNO('%1 %2',Type, "No."),
                                                                      FIELDCAPTION("Service Job No."),
                                                                      "Service Job No.",
                                                                      FIELDCAPTION("Serv. Contract Type"));
                                                                // Stop EU.0052165

                                                                IF "Serv. Contract Type" > '' THEN BEGIN
                                                                  GetServHeader;
                                                                  VehServContractL.RESET;
                                                                  VehServContractL.SETRANGE(VIN, ServHdrG.VIN);
                                                                  VehServContractL.SETRANGE("Serv. Contract Cust. No.", "Bill-to Customer No.");
                                                                  VehServContractL.SETFILTER("Beginning of Contract", '=%1|<=%2' , 0D, "Order Date");
                                                                  VehServContractL.SETFILTER("Expiration of Contract", '=%1|>=%2' , 0D, "Order Date");
                                                                  IF VehicleG.GET(ServHdrG.VIN) THEN BEGIN
                                                                    VehServContractL.SETFILTER("Max. Mileage", '=%1|>=%2' , 0, VehicleG.Mileage);
                                                                    VehServContractL.SETFILTER("Distance Kilometer", '=%1|>=%2' , 0, VehicleG.Mileage);
                                                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                                                    VehServContractL.SETFILTER("Max. Mileage", '=%1|>=%2' , 0, ServHdrG.Mileage);
                                                                    VehServContractL.SETFILTER("Distance Kilometer", '=%1|>=%2' , 0, ServHdrG.Mileage);
                                                                  END;
                                                                // Start EU.0064128
                                                                  IF VehServContractL.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
                                                                    VehServContractL.GET(ServHdrG.VIN, "Bill-to Customer No.", "Serv. Contract Type");
                                                                    MESSAGE(C_INC072, "Serv. Contract Type", ServHdrG.VIN, "Bill-to Customer No.");
                                                                  END;
                                                                // Stop EU.0064128
                                                                END;

                                                                // Delete Findings No.
                                                                IF ("Serv. Contract Type" <> xRec."Serv. Contract Type") AND (xRec."Serv. Contract Type" > '') THEN BEGIN
                                                                  PresentRecL.GETTABLE(xRec);
                                                                // Start PA032651
                                                                  ServContractMgmtL.FindingNosDelete(
                                                                    PresentRecL,
                                                                    FORMAT(DATABASE::"Service Line"),
                                                                    xRec."Bill-to Customer No.");
                                                                // Stop PA032651
                                                                END;
                                                                // Start PA034531.19042
                                                                IF ("Serv. Contract Type" <> xRec."Serv. Contract Type") THEN BEGIN
                                                                  IF Type IN [Type::Item,Type::Labor] THEN BEGIN
                                                                    UpdateUnitPrice();
                                                                    SalesPriceCalculation(TRUE);
                                                                // Start EU.0177226.178565
                                                                    CheckLaborPrice();
                                                                    IF ServPostingGroupG.GET("Service Posting Group") THEN BEGIN
                                                                      IF (Type = Type::Labor) AND ("Fixed Price" <> 0) AND (Quantity <> 0) THEN BEGIN
                                                                        UnitPriceOldL := "Unit Price";
                                                                        VALIDATE(Amount,"Fixed Price");
                                                                        "Line Discount Amount" :=
                                                                          (UnitPriceOldL * Quantity) - (UnitPriceOldL * Quantity * "Cust./Item Disc. %" / 100) - "Fixed Price";
                                                                        "Line Discount %" :=
                                                                          ("Line Discount Amount" * 100) / ((UnitPriceOldL * Quantity) - (UnitPriceOldL * Quantity * "Cust./Item Disc. %") / 100);
                                                                        Amount := "Fixed Price";
                                                                      END;
                                                                    END;
                                                                // Stop EU.0177226.178565
                                                                  END;
                                                                END;
                                                                // Stop PA034531.19042
                                                              END;

                                                   OnLookup=VAR
                                                              VehServContractL@1109400000 : Record 5061005;
                                                            BEGIN
                                                              GetServHeader;
                                                              VehServContractL.RESET;
                                                              VehServContractL.SETRANGE(VIN, ServHdrG.VIN);
                                                              VehServContractL.SETRANGE("Serv. Contract Cust. No.", "Bill-to Customer No.");
                                                              VehServContractL.SETFILTER("Beginning of Contract", '=%1|<=%2' , 0D, "Order Date");
                                                              VehServContractL.SETFILTER("Expiration of Contract", '=%1|>=%2' , 0D, "Order Date");
                                                              IF VehicleG.GET(ServHdrG.VIN) THEN BEGIN
                                                                VehServContractL.SETFILTER("Max. Mileage", '=%1|>=%2' , 0, VehicleG.Mileage);
                                                                VehServContractL.SETFILTER("Distance Kilometer", '=%1|>=%2' , 0, VehicleG.Mileage);
                                                              END ELSE BEGIN
                                                                VehServContractL.SETFILTER("Max. Mileage", '=%1|>=%2' , 0, ServHdrG.Mileage);
                                                                VehServContractL.SETFILTER("Distance Kilometer", '=%1|>=%2' , 0, ServHdrG.Mileage);
                                                              END;
                                                              // Start EU.0064128
                                                              IF NOT VehServContractL.FINDFIRST THEN
                                                                MESSAGE(C_INC073, ServHdrG.VIN, "Bill-to Customer No.");
                                                              IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(0, VehServContractL) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN
                                                                VALIDATE("Serv. Contract Type", VehServContractL."Contract Type");
                                                              // Start PA039250
                                                              StatusCheckFunction(FALSE);
                                                              // Stop PA039250
                                                              // Stop EU.0064128
                                                            END;

                                                   CaptionML=ENU=Serv. Contract Type;
                                                   Description=EU.0123449 }

                                                                // Start PA036842

                                                                // Start PA034057

                                                                    END ELSE BEGIN
                                                                      VALIDATE("Unit Cost (LCY)", 0);
                                                                    END;
                                                                  END;

                                                                END;

                                                                UpdateFieldInAttachedLines(FIELDNO("Resource No."));

    LOCAL PROCEDURE ExitPointCall@5025380(MakeCoddeP@1109400003 : Code[20];TriggerP@1109400002 : Integer;TypeP@1109400001 : Integer;ExitPointIDP@1109400000 : Text[50];VAR EPRecRefP@1109400005 : RecordRef) : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      EXIT(ExitPointUnitG.RunExitPoint(
        ExitPointSetupG."Object Type"::Table,
        DATABASE::"Service Line",
        MakeCoddeP, TriggerP, TypeP, ExitPointIDP, EPRecRefP, EPRecRef2G, ExitPointParamG));
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE ExitPoint@5025450(TriggerP@1119452001 : Integer;TypeP@1119432000 : Integer;ExitPointIDP@1119432001 : Text[50]) ReturnR : Boolean;
    VAR
      EPRecRefL@1109400004 : RecordRef;
    BEGIN
      // @ This local function works as ExitPoint wrapper function. It will control the ExitPointCheck function call.
      // @ It passes thru all the handshake parameter values.
      // @ It takes care to provide the processing records as RecordReference to the ExitPointCheck function.
      // @ When possible a Make Code is also identified and passed to the called ExitPointCheck function.

      // Start PA036544
      EPRecRefL.GETTABLE(Rec);
      EPRecRef2G.GETTABLE(xRec);
      ExitPointParamG."Called CurrFieldNo" := CurrFieldNo;
      ReturnR := ExitPointCall("Make Code", TriggerP, TypeP, ExitPointIDP, EPRecRefL);
      EPRecRefL.SETTABLE(Rec);
      CLEAR(EPRecRef2G);
      // Stop PA036544
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE ServiceLineExitPoint@1101342644(VAR ServLineP@1101342643 : Record 5025625;TriggerP@1109400002 : Integer;TypeP@1109400001 : Integer;ExitPointIDP@1109400000 : Text[50]) ReturnR : Boolean;
    VAR
      EPRecRefL@1109400004 : RecordRef;
    BEGIN
      // @ This local function works as ExitPoint wrapper function. It will control the ExitPointCheck function call.
      // @ It passes thru all the handshake parameter values.
      // @ It takes care to provide the processing records as RecordReference to the ExitPointCheck function.
      // @ When possible a Make Code is also identified and passed to the called ExitPointCheck function.

      EPRecRefL.GETTABLE(ServLineP);
      ReturnR := ExitPointCall(ServLineP."Make Code", TriggerP, TypeP, ExitPointIDP, EPRecRefL);
      EPRecRefL.SETTABLE(ServLineP);
      CLEAR(EPRecRef2G);
    END;
