    PROCEDURE InitOutstanding@16();
    BEGIN
      "Qty. Shipped (Hour)" := CalcHoursQty("Quantity Shipped");
      "Qty. Invoiced (Hour)" := CalcHoursQty("Quantity Invoiced");
      "Outstanding Quantity" := Quantity - "Quantity Shipped";
      "Outstanding Qty. (Base)" := "Quantity (Base)" - "Qty. Shipped (Base)";
      "Outstanding Qty. (Hour)" := "Qty. (Hour)" - "Qty. Shipped (Hour)";
      // Start PA033978.I000905
      IF Type IN [Type::Item,Type::Labor,Type::"G/L Account"] THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA033978.I000905
        "Qty. Shipped Not Invoiced" := "Quantity Shipped" - "Quantity Invoiced";
        "Qty. Shipped Not Invd. (Base)" := "Qty. Shipped (Base)" - "Qty. Invoiced (Base)";
        "Qty. Rcd. Not Invoiced (Hour)" := "Qty. Shipped (Hour)" - "Qty. Invoiced (Hour)";
      END ELSE BEGIN
        "Qty. Shipped Not Invoiced" := 0;
        "Qty. Shipped Not Invd. (Base)" := 0;
        "Qty. Rcd. Not Invoiced (Hour)" := 0;
      END;
      InitOutstandingAmount();
      IF CurrFieldNo = 0 THEN
      // Start EU.0036239
        FindStatus(FALSE);
      // Stop EU.0036239
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE InitOutstandingAmount@17();
    BEGIN
      IF Quantity = 0 THEN BEGIN
        "Outstanding Amount" := 0;
        "Outstanding Amount (LCY)" := 0;
        "Shipped Not Invoiced" := 0;
        "Shipped Not Invoiced (LCY)" := 0;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        GetServHeader();
        VALIDATE("Outstanding Amount", ROUND("Amount Including VAT" * "Outstanding Quantity" / Quantity,
          CurrencyG."Amount Rounding Precision"));
        VALIDATE("Shipped Not Invoiced", ROUND("Amount Including VAT" * "Qty. Shipped Not Invoiced" / Quantity,
          CurrencyG."Amount Rounding Precision"));
      END;

      // Start EU.0109895.110101
      // Stop EU.0109895.110101
    END;

    PROCEDURE InitQtyToShip@15();
    BEGIN
      IF (Type IN [Type::"G/L Account", Type::Item, Type::Labor, Type::"Ext. Service"]) AND
         (NOT ("Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::Quote,"Document Type"::Scheduling]))
      THEN BEGIN
        "Qty. to Ship" := "Outstanding Quantity";
        "Qty. to Ship (Base)" := "Outstanding Qty. (Base)";
      END ELSE BEGIN
        "Qty. to Ship" := 0;
        "Qty. to Ship (Base)" := 0;
      END;
      InitQtyToInv();
    END;

    PROCEDURE InitQtyToInv@13();
    BEGIN
      "Qty. to Invoice" := MaxQtyToInvoice;
      "Qty. to Invoice (Base)" := MaxQtyToInvoiceBase;
      IF CurrFieldNo = 0 THEN
      // Start EU.0036239
        FindStatus(FALSE);
      // Stop EU.0036239
    END;

    PROCEDURE MaxQtyToInvoice@18() : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      IF Type IN [Type::"Ext. Service"] THEN
        EXIT(Quantity - "Quantity Invoiced");
      EXIT("Quantity Shipped" + "Qty. to Ship" - "Quantity Invoiced");
    END;

    PROCEDURE MaxQtyToInvoiceBase@19() : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      IF Type IN [Type::"Ext. Service"] THEN
        EXIT("Quantity (Base)" - "Qty. Invoiced (Base)");
      EXIT("Qty. Shipped (Base)" + "Qty. to Ship (Base)" - "Qty. Invoiced (Base)");
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalcBaseQty@14(QtyP@1109400000 : Decimal) : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      TESTFIELD("Qty. per Unit of Measure");
      EXIT(ROUND(QtyP * "Qty. per Unit of Measure", 0.00001));
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalcHoursQty@28(QtyP@1109400000 : Decimal) : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      TESTFIELD("Qty. per Hour");
      EXIT(ROUND(QtyP / "Qty. per Hour", 0.00001));
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE SelectItemEntry@8(CurrentFieldNoP@1109400000 : Integer);
    BEGIN
      ItemLedgEntryG.RESET;
      TESTFIELD(Type,Type::Item);
      ItemLedgEntryG.SETCURRENTKEY("Item No.","Variant Code",Open);
      ItemLedgEntryG.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
      IF Quantity <> 0 THEN
        ItemLedgEntryG.SETRANGE(Positive,Quantity > 0);
      CASE CurrentFieldNoP OF
        FIELDNO("Appl.-to Item Entry"):
          BEGIN
            ItemLedgEntryG.SETRANGE(Positive, TRUE);
            ItemLedgEntryG.SETRANGE(Open, TRUE);
            IF ItemLedgEntryG.GET("Appl.-to Item Entry") THEN
              ;
          END;
        FIELDNO("Appl.-from Item Entry"):
          BEGIN
            ItemLedgEntryG.SETRANGE(Positive, FALSE);
            IF ItemLedgEntryG.GET("Appl.-from Item Entry") THEN
              ;
          END;
        FIELDNO("Serial No."):
          BEGIN
            ItemLedgEntryG.SETRANGE(Positive, Quantity > 0);
          END;
      END;
      IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(PAGE::"Item Ledger Entries",ItemLedgEntryG) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
        CASE CurrentFieldNoP OF
          FIELDNO("Appl.-to Item Entry"):
            BEGIN
              VALIDATE("Appl.-to Item Entry", ItemLedgEntryG."Entry No.");
            END;
          FIELDNO("Appl.-from Item Entry"):
            BEGIN
              VALIDATE("Appl.-from Item Entry", ItemLedgEntryG."Entry No.");
            END;
          FIELDNO("Serial No."):
            BEGIN
              VALIDATE("Appl.-to Item Entry", ItemLedgEntryG."Entry No.");
            END;
        END;
        IF Reserve <> Reserve::Always THEN
          CheckItemAvailable();
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE SetServHeader@24(ServHdrP@1109400000 : Record 5025624);
    BEGIN
      ServHdrG := ServHdrP;
      // Start EU.0082249
      CurrencyG.Initialize(ServHdrG."Currency Code");
      IF ServHdrG."Currency Code" <> '' THEN
        CurrencyG.TESTFIELD("Amount Rounding Precision");
      // Stop EU.0082249
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetServHeader@1();
    BEGIN
      TESTFIELD("Document No.");
      IF ("Document Type" <> ServHdrG."Document Type") OR ("Document No." <> ServHdrG."No.") THEN BEGIN
        ServHdrG.GET("Document Type","Document No.");
      // Start EU.0082249
        CurrencyG.Initialize(ServHdrG."Currency Code");
      // Start EU.0210554.171367
        LocalCurrencyG.InitRoundingPrecision();
      // Stop EU.0210554.171367
        IF ServHdrG."Currency Code" <> '' THEN
      // Stop EU.0082249
          CurrencyG.TESTFIELD("Amount Rounding Precision");
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetVatBusPostingGroup@1055603(GenBusPostingGrpP@1055600 : Code[10];GenVatBusPostingGrpP@1055604 : Code[10];BillToCustomerNoP@1055602 : Code[20]) : Code[10];
    VAR
      CustL@1055601 : Record 18;
      GenBusPostingGroupL@1055603 : Record 250;
    BEGIN
      // @ The function will detect if a "Gen. Bus. Posting Group" must be changed to the "Bus. Posting Group/Own Sales"
      // Start EU.0044639
      IF GenBusPostingGrpP > '' THEN
        IF CustL.GET(BillToCustomerNoP) AND
           CustL."EU Business Customer" AND
           (GenBusPostingGrpP <> CustL."Gen. Bus. Posting Group") AND
           GenBusPostingGroupL.ValidateVatBusPostingGroup(GenBusPostingGroupL, GenBusPostingGrpP) AND
           (GenBusPostingGroupL."Def. EU VAT Bus. Posting Group" > '')
        THEN
          EXIT(GenBusPostingGroupL."Def. EU VAT Bus. Posting Group");

      IF GenVatBusPostingGrpP = '' THEN
        CASE TRUE OF
      // Start EU.0052165
          ("Service Job No." > 0) AND GetServiceJob() AND ("Bill-to Customer No." = ServJobG."Bill-to Customer No."):
      // Stop EU.0052165
            GenVatBusPostingGrpP := ServJobG."VAT Bus. Posting Group";
          ServCustG.GET("Document Type", "Document No.", BillToCustomerNoP):
            GenVatBusPostingGrpP := ServCustG."Default VAT Bus. Posting Group";
          ServHdrG.GET("Document Type", "Document No.") AND (ServHdrG."VAT Bus. Posting Group" > ''):
            GenVatBusPostingGrpP := ServHdrG."VAT Bus. Posting Group";
          BillToCustomerNoP = '':
            BEGIN
      // Start EU.0104306
              ServSetupGet();
      // Stop EU.0104306
              ServSetupG.TESTFIELD("Def. Cust. No. Service Inquiry");
              CustL.GET(ServSetupG."Def. Cust. No. Service Inquiry");
              GenVatBusPostingGrpP := CustL."VAT Bus. Posting Group";
            END;
          ELSE BEGIN
            CustL.GET(BillToCustomerNoP);
            GenVatBusPostingGrpP := CustL."VAT Bus. Posting Group";
          END;
        END;
      EXIT(GenVatBusPostingGrpP);
      // Stop EU.0044639
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetItem@9();
    BEGIN
      TESTFIELD("No.");
      IF "No." <> ItemG."No." THEN
      // Start PA032651
        IF NOT ItemG.GET("No.") THEN BEGIN
          ItemG.SETCURRENTKEY("Manufacturer No.");
          ItemG.SETRANGE("Manufacturer No.","No.");
          ItemG.FINDFIRST();
          "No." := ItemG."No.";
        END;
      // Stop PA032651
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetSalesSetup@10430601();
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0104306
      IF SalesSetupG."Primary Key" = 'OK' THEN
        EXIT;
      SalesSetupG.GET();
      SalesSetupG."Primary Key" := 'OK';
      // Stop EU.0104306
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE UpdateUnitPrice@2();
    VAR
      GLSetupL@1109400000 : Record 98;
      PkgVersionL@1117900002 : Record 5025615;
      ServPkgL@1117900001 : Record 5025635;
      PkgUnitL@1117900003 : Codeunit 5025621;
      SetFixPriceL@1117900000 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // Start PA036544
      IF ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::"Function",ExitPointSetupG.Type::Pre,'UpdateUnitPrice') THEN
        EXIT;
      // Stop PA036544

      TESTFIELD("Qty. per Unit of Measure");
      GetServHeader();
      PriceInCurrencyG := FALSE;
      ItemPriceInclVATG := FALSE;
      // Start PA034249
      // Stop PA034249
      CASE Type OF
        Type::Item:
          BEGIN
      // Start PA034249
            IF "No." > '' THEN
              GetItem();
      // Stop PA034249
            ItemPriceG.INIT;
            ItemPriceG."Item No." := "No.";
      // Start PA034249
            GetServCustomer();
            ItemPriceG."Price Group Code" := ServCustG."Item Sales Price Group";
      // Stop PA034249
            ItemPriceG."Currency Code" := ServHdrG."Currency Code";
            ItemPriceG."Unit of Measure Code" := "Unit of Measure Code";
            IF "Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::Quote,"Document Type"::Order,"Document Type"::Scheduling] THEN
              ItemPriceG."Starting Date" := WORKDATE
            ELSE
              ItemPriceG."Starting Date" := ServHdrG."Posting Date";
            ItemPriceG."Location Code" := "Location Code";
            ItemFindUnitPriceG.RUN(ItemPriceG);
      // Start PA041789.82600
      // Start PA041789
            "Unit Price" := ItemPriceG."Unit Price";
      // Stop PA041789
      // Stop PA041789.82600
            ItemG."VAT Bus. Posting Gr. (Price)" := ItemPriceG."VAT Bus. Posting Gr. (Price)";
            "Allow Quantity Disc." := ItemPriceG."Allow Quantity Disc.";
            "Allow Discount" := ItemPriceG."Allow Discount";
            IF ItemPriceG."Allow Cust./Item Disc." THEN BEGIN
              IF CustItemDiscG.GET(ServHdrG."Cust./Item Disc. Gr.",ItemG."Cust./Item Disc. Gr.") THEN
                "Cust./Item Disc. %" := CustItemDiscG."Discount %";
            END ELSE
              "Cust./Item Disc. %" := 0;
      // Start PA032651
            "Quantity Disc. %" := 0;
      // Stop PA032651
            PriceInCurrencyG := ItemPriceG."Currency Code" > '';
            ItemPriceInclVATG := ItemPriceG."Price Includes VAT";
          END;
        Type::Labor:
          BEGIN
            ChrgGrpSalPriceG.INIT;
            ChrgGrpSalPriceG."Charging Group No." := "No.";
      // Start PA034249
            GetServCustomer();
      // Stop PA034249
            ChrgGrpSalPriceG."Labor Price Group" := ServCustG."Labor Price Group";

      // Start PA036544
            ExitPointParamG.INIT;
            ExitPointParamG."Code 1" := ChrgGrpSalPriceG."Labor Price Group";
            EPRecRef2G.GETTABLE(ServCustG);
            ServiceLineExitPoint(Rec, ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::"Function",ExitPointSetupG.Type::"Inside 1",'UpdateUnitPrice');
            ChrgGrpSalPriceG."Labor Price Group" := ExitPointParamG."Code 1";
      // Stop PA036544

            ChrgGrpSalPriceG."Labor Charging Code" := ServHdrG."Labor Charging Code";
            ChrgGrpSalPriceG."Data Make Code" := "Data Make Code";
            GetChrgGrpValSalPriceG.Code(ChrgGrpSalPriceG,ServHdrG."Order Date","Location Code",ServHdrG."Currency Code");
      // Start EU.0106909.115086
            OnInside1UpdateUnitPriceEvent(ChrgGrpSalPriceG, ServHdrG, Rec);
      // Stop EU.0106909.115086
            SetFixPriceL := TRUE;
            IF "Package No." > '' THEN BEGIN
              IF ServPkgL.GET("Document Type","Document No.","Package No.","Package Version No.") THEN BEGIN
                SetFixPriceL := ServPkgL."Unit Price" = 0;
              END ELSE
                IF PkgVersionL.GET("Data Make Code","Package No.","Package Version No.") THEN BEGIN
                  SetFixPriceL := NOT PkgUnitL.IsFixedPricePackage(PkgVersionL,ServHdrG."Location Code",
                    ServHdrG."Currency Code",ServHdrG."Order Date");
                END;
            END;
            IF SetFixPriceL THEN
              "Fixed Price" := ChrgGrpSalPriceG."Fixed Price";
            "Unit Price" := ChrgGrpSalPriceG."Unit Price (Hour)";
            "No Charge" := ChrgGrpSalPriceG."No Charge";
      // Start EU.0091116
      // Stop EU.0091116
      // Start PA040732.60765
            IF "Fixed Price" <> 0 THEN
              "Cust./Item Disc. %" := 0
            ELSE
              "Cust./Item Disc. %" := ChrgGrpSalPriceG."Discount %";
      // Stop PA040732.60765
            IF "Qty. per Hour" <> 0 THEN BEGIN
      // Start PA040295
              "Unit Price" := ROUND(("Unit Price" / "Qty. per Hour"),CurrencyG."Unit-Amount Rounding Precision");
      // Stop PA040295
            END;
      // Start PA032600
      // Stop PA032600
          END;
      END;

      // Start EU.0091116
      // Check if ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY should be performed
      IF (ServHdrG."Currency Code" > '') THEN BEGIN
        IF Type <> Type::Labor THEN BEGIN
          IF NOT PriceInCurrencyG THEN BEGIN
            ServHdrG.TESTFIELD("Currency Factor");
            "Unit Price" := CurrencyExchRateG.ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(GetDate,ServHdrG."Currency Code", "Unit Price",ServHdrG."Currency Factor");
            "Fixed Price" := CurrencyExchRateG.ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(GetDate,ServHdrG."Currency Code", "Fixed Price",ServHdrG."Currency Factor");
          END;
        END ELSE BEGIN // For Labor we need to consider Unit Price and Fixed Price separately
          IF NOT GetChrgGrpValSalPriceG.IsUnitPriceInCurrency() THEN BEGIN
            ServHdrG.TESTFIELD("Currency Factor");
            "Unit Price" := CurrencyExchRateG.ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(GetDate,ServHdrG."Currency Code", "Unit Price",ServHdrG."Currency Factor");
          END;
          IF NOT GetChrgGrpValSalPriceG.IsFixedPriceInCurrency() THEN BEGIN
            ServHdrG.TESTFIELD("Currency Factor");
            "Fixed Price" := CurrencyExchRateG.ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(GetDate,ServHdrG."Currency Code", "Fixed Price",ServHdrG."Currency Factor");
          END;
        END;
      END;
      // Stop EU.0091116

      IF ItemPriceG."Unit of Measure Code" = '' THEN
        "Unit Price" := "Unit Price" * "Qty. per Unit of Measure";

      IF ItemPriceInclVATG THEN BEGIN
        IF NOT VATPostingSetupG.GET(ItemG."VAT Bus. Posting Gr. (Price)",ItemG."VAT Prod. Posting Group") THEN
          VATPostingSetupG.INIT;
        CASE VATPostingSetupG."VAT Calculation Type" OF
          VATPostingSetupG."VAT Calculation Type"::"Reverse Charge VAT":
            VATPostingSetupG."VAT %" := 0;
          VATPostingSetupG."VAT Calculation Type"::"Sales Tax":
            ERROR(C_INC023, VATPostingSetupG.FIELDCAPTION("VAT Calculation Type"), VATPostingSetupG."VAT Calculation Type");
        END;
        CASE "VAT Calculation Type" OF
          "VAT Calculation Type"::"Normal VAT",
            "VAT Calculation Type"::"Full VAT",
          "VAT Calculation Type"::"Sales Tax":
            BEGIN
              IF ServHdrG."Prices Including VAT" THEN BEGIN
                IF "VAT Bus. Posting Group" <> ItemG."VAT Bus. Posting Gr. (Price)" THEN
                  "Unit Price" := "Unit Price" * (100 + "VAT %") / (100 + VATPostingSetupG."VAT %");
              END ELSE
                "Unit Price" := "Unit Price" / (1 + VATPostingSetupG."VAT %" / 100);
            END;
          "VAT Calculation Type"::"Reverse Charge VAT":
            "Unit Price" := "Unit Price" / (1 + VATPostingSetupG."VAT %" / 100);
        END;
      END ELSE
        IF ServHdrG."Prices Including VAT" THEN
          "Unit Price" := "Unit Price" * (1 + "VAT %" / 100);
      CurrencyG.TESTFIELD("Unit-Amount Rounding Precision");
      "Unit Price" := ROUND("Unit Price",CurrencyG."Unit-Amount Rounding Precision");

      // Start PA036544
      ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::"Function",ExitPointSetupG.Type::Post,'UpdateUnitPrice');
      // Stop PA036544
    END;

    PROCEDURE UpdateAmounts@3();
    BEGIN
      // Start PA036544
      IF ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::"Function",ExitPointSetupG.Type::Pre,'UpdateAmounts') THEN
        EXIT;
      // Stop PA036544

      TESTFIELD(Type);
      GetServHeader();
      // Start EU.0088907
      // Start EU.0132795
      OriginalAmountG := CalcOriginalAmountUnrounded(Quantity, "Unit Price", ServHdrG."Prices Including VAT", "VAT Calculation Type", "VAT %");
      // Stop EU.0132795
      // Stop EU.0088907
      // Start PA033352
      IF ServHdrG."Currency Code" = '' THEN
      // Start PA036224
        CurrencyG.InitRoundingPrecision();
      // Stop PA036224
      // Stop PA033352
      CASE "VAT Calculation Type" OF
        "VAT Calculation Type"::"Normal VAT",
        "VAT Calculation Type"::"Reverse Charge VAT":
          BEGIN
            IF "Fixed Price" <> 0 THEN
              Amount := "Fixed Price"
            ELSE
      // Start PA033352
      // Start PA034053.I000514
      // Start PA042968
      // Start EU.0138596
              Amount := ROUND(OriginalAmountG - "Line Discount Amount" + "Autom. Rounding Disc. Amount",CurrencyG."Amount Rounding Precision");
      // Stop EU.0138596
      // Stop PA042968
      // Stop PA034053.I000514
      // Start EU.0143914.144069
            IF ("Line Discount %" = 100) OR "No Charge" THEN
              Amount := 0;
      // Stop EU.0143914.144069
            "VAT Base Amount" := ROUND(Amount * (1 - ServHdrG."VAT Base Discount %" / 100),CurrencyG."Amount Rounding Precision");
            "Amount Including VAT" := ROUND(Amount + "VAT Base Amount" * "VAT %" / 100,CurrencyG."Amount Rounding Precision");
      // Stop PA033352
          END;
        "VAT Calculation Type"::"Full VAT":
          BEGIN
            Amount := 0;
            "VAT Base Amount" := 0;
      // Start PA042968
            "Amount Including VAT" := ROUND(OriginalAmountG);
      // Stop PA042968
          END;
        "VAT Calculation Type"::"Sales Tax":
          BEGIN
      // Start PA036544
            ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::"Function",ExitPointSetupG.Type::"Inside 1",'UpdateAmounts');
      // Stop PA036544
            IF "Fixed Price" <> 0 THEN
              Amount := "Fixed Price"
            ELSE
      // Start PA033352
      // Start PA042968
      // Start EU.0138596
              Amount := ROUND(OriginalAmountG - "Line Discount Amount" + "Autom. Rounding Disc. Amount",CurrencyG."Amount Rounding Precision");
      // Stop EU.0138596
      // Stop PA042968
            "VAT Base Amount" := ROUND(Amount,CurrencyG."Amount Rounding Precision");
      // Stop PA033352
      // Start PA034053.I000514
           "Amount Including VAT" :=
              Amount +
      // Start EU.0104321
              CalcSalesTaxG.CalculateTax(
                "Tax Area Code", "Tax Group Code", "Tax Liable", ServHdrG."Posting Date",
                "VAT Base Amount", Quantity, ServHdrG."Currency Factor");
      // Stop EU.0104321
            IF "VAT Base Amount" <> 0 THEN
              "VAT %" := ROUND(100 * ("Amount Including VAT" - "VAT Base Amount") / "VAT Base Amount",0.00001)
            ELSE
              "VAT %" := 0;
      // Start EU.0104321
            "Amount Including VAT" := ROUND("Amount Including VAT", CurrencyG."Amount Rounding Precision");
      // Stop EU.0104321
          END;
      // Stop PA034053.I000514
        "VAT Calculation Type"::"Exch. Parts Tax":
          BEGIN
      // Start PA033352
      // Start PA042968
      // Start EU.0138596
            Amount := ROUND(OriginalAmountG - "Line Discount Amount" + "Autom. Rounding Disc. Amount",CurrencyG."Amount Rounding Precision");
      // Stop EU.0138596
            "VAT Base Amount" := ROUND(Amount * (1 - ServHdrG."VAT Base Discount %" / 100),CurrencyG."Amount Rounding Precision");
            "Exch. Parts Tax Base" := ROUND(OriginalAmountG * "Exch. Parts Tax %" / 100,CurrencyG."Amount Rounding Precision");
      // Stop PA042968
            "Exch. Parts Tax Amount" := ROUND("Exch. Parts Tax Base" * "Exch. Parts VAT %" / 100,CurrencyG."Amount Rounding Precision");
            "Amount Including VAT" := ROUND(Amount + "VAT Base Amount" * "VAT %" / 100 +
              "Exch. Parts Tax Amount",CurrencyG."Amount Rounding Precision");
      // Stop PA033352
          END;
      END;
      // Start EU.0104306
      // Stop EU.0104306
      InitOutstandingAmount();

      // Start PA036544
      ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::"Function",ExitPointSetupG.Type::Post,'UpdateAmounts');
      // Stop PA036544
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE SetProcessTriggeredFromField@10430602(FromFieldNoP@10430600 : Integer) TransactionStartDetected : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0104306
      IF ProcessTriggeredFromFieldG <> 0 THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      ProcessTriggeredFromFieldG := FromFieldNoP;
      EXIT(TRUE);
      // Stop EU.0104306
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE RunOrderLineRounding@10430603(TransactionStartDetectedP@10430601 : Boolean;ExRecP@10430600 : Record 5025625);
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0104306
      IF TransactionStartDetectedP THEN BEGIN
        IF NOT SkipUpdateVATAmountRoundingG THEN BEGIN
          IF (ExRecP.Amount = 0) OR (ExRecP."Amount Including VAT" = 0) THEN
            IF NOT ExRecP.GET(RECORDID) THEN
              ;
          IF UpdateVATAmountRounding(FALSE) THEN
            IF (Amount <> ExRecP.Amount) OR ("Amount Including VAT" <> ExRecP."Amount Including VAT") THEN
              InitOutstandingAmount();
          IF (Amount <> ExRecP.Amount) OR
             ("Amount Including VAT" <> ExRecP."Amount Including VAT") OR
             ("Line Discount %" <> ExRecP."Line Discount %") OR
             ("Line Discount Amount" <> ExRecP."Line Discount Amount")
          THEN
            UpdateSplittCalculation();
        END;
        ProcessTriggeredFromFieldG := 0;
      END;
      // Stop EU.0104306
    END;

    PROCEDURE RoundOneLine@10430605();
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0104306
      RunOrderLineRounding(TRUE, Rec);
      // Stop EU.0104306
    END;

    PROCEDURE SetSkipUpdateVATAmountRounding@10430604(SetParamP@10430600 : Boolean) OldSetParamR : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0104306
      OldSetParamR := SkipUpdateVATAmountRoundingG;
      SkipUpdateVATAmountRoundingG := SetParamP;
      EXIT(OldSetParamR);
      // Stop EU.0104306
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE UpdateVATAmountRounding@1000000001(SkipCurrentLineP@1000000000 : Boolean) CurrLineAdjustedR : Boolean;
    VAR
      ExRecL@1000 : Record 5025625;
    BEGIN
      // @ New function to detect cent rounding difference coming from the 2 decimals "VAT Amount" calculation of the "Amount" and the "Amount including VAT"
      // @ In case there are some the difference it added to the current "Amount including VAT"
      // Start EU.0104306
      IF ("Unit Price" = 0) OR ("VAT %" = 0) OR (Quantity = 0) THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      GetServHeader();
      IF ServHdrG."Prices Including VAT" THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      GeneralLedgerSetupG.GetRec();
      IF "Virtual Record" OR (GeneralLedgerSetupG."Service VAT Rounding Adjustm." = GeneralLedgerSetupG."Service VAT Rounding Adjustm."::"Directly when modify a Line") THEN
        IF RecordIsTemporalG OR ISTEMPORARY THEN
          TempTableUpdateLineVATAmountRounding()
        ELSE BEGIN
          ExRecL := Rec;
          UpdateLineVATAmountRounding(SkipCurrentLineP);
          EXIT((Amount <> ExRecL.Amount) OR ("Amount Including VAT" <> ExRecL."Amount Including VAT") OR ("Line Discount %" <> ExRecL."Line Discount %"));
      END;
      EXIT(FALSE);
      // Stop EU.0104306
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE TempTableUpdateLineVATAmountRounding@1109400041();
    VAR
      ServHdrL@1001 : Record 5025624;
      VATAmountLineTempL@1109400003 : TEMPORARY Record 290;
      TotalAmountRoundedL@1109400001 : Decimal;
      TotalAmountL@1002 : Decimal;
      TotalDifferenceL@1109400000 : Decimal;
      OriginalAmountL@1000 : Decimal;
      NewLineDiscountAmountL@10430600 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      // @ New function to detect cent rounding difference coming from the 2 decimals "VAT Amount" calculation of the "Amount" and the "Amount including VAT"
      // @ In case there are some the difference it added to the current "Amount including VAT"
      // @ This function should be used when the source table is defined as temporary table (RecordIsTemporalG is active)
      // Start PA041187.90442
      IF ("Unit Price" = 0) OR ("VAT %" = 0) THEN
        EXIT;
      // Start EU.0104306
      // Stop EU.0104306
      IF ServHdrG."Prices Including VAT" THEN
        EXIT;

      // Add the unrounded "Amount Including VAT" for the currentl line
      VATAmountLineTempL.INIT;
      VATAmountLineTempL."VAT Identifier" := FORMAT("VAT %");
      // Start EU.0104306
      ServHdrL := ServHdrG;
      IF "Service Job No." <> 0 THEN
        IF GeneralLedgerSetupG.EnhancedVATCalculationLogicActive() THEN BEGIN
          IF (ServJobG."Document Type" <> "Document Type") OR (ServJobG."Document No." <> "Document No.") OR (ServJobG."Line No." <> "Service Job No.") THEN
            ServJobG.GET("Document Type", "Document No.", "Service Job No.");
          CASE TRUE OF
            ServJobG."Fixed Price" <> 0:
              ServHdrL."VAT Calculation Logic" := ServHdrL."VAT Calculation Logic"::"Amount + VAT";
            ServJobG."Fixed Price Incl. VAT" <> 0:
              ServHdrL."VAT Calculation Logic" := ServHdrL."VAT Calculation Logic"::"Amount incl. VAT";
          END;
        END;
      IF NOT GeneralLedgerSetupG.EnhancedVATCalculationLogicInDocActive(ServHdrL."VAT Calculation Logic") THEN BEGIN
        VATAmountLineTempL."Amount Including VAT" := CalcVATAmountUnrounded(Rec);
        TotalAmountL := "Amount Including VAT";
      END ELSE BEGIN
        VATAmountLineTempL."Line Amount" := CalcAmountUnrounded(Rec);
        TotalAmountL := Amount;
      END;
      VATAmountLineTempL.InsertLine();
      // Stop EU.0104306

      ServLineTempG.RESET;
      ServLineTempG.SETRANGE("Document Type", "Document Type");
      ServLineTempG.SETRANGE("Document No.", "Document No.");
      ServLineTempG.SETFILTER("Line No.", '<>%1', "Line No.");
      // Start EU.0104306
      ServLineTempG.SETFILTER(Type, '<>%1', Type::" ");
      ServLineTempG.SETFILTER("Unit Price", '<>0');
      ServLineTempG.SETFILTER("VAT %", '<>0');
      ServLineTempG.SETFILTER(Quantity, '<>0');
      // Start EU.0132795
      ServLineTempG.SETFILTER("Line Discount %", '<>100');
      // Stop EU.0132795
      // Stop EU.0104306
      ServLineTempG.SETRANGE("Bill-to Customer No.", "Bill-to Customer No.");
      IF ServLineTempG.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          VATAmountLineTempL.INIT;
          VATAmountLineTempL."VAT Identifier" := FORMAT(ServLineTempG."VAT %");
      // Start EU.0104306
          IF NOT GeneralLedgerSetupG.EnhancedVATCalculationLogicInDocActive(ServHdrL."VAT Calculation Logic") THEN BEGIN
            VATAmountLineTempL."Amount Including VAT" := CalcVATAmountUnrounded(ServLineTempG);
            TotalAmountL := TotalAmountL + ServLineTempG."Amount Including VAT";
          END ELSE BEGIN
            VATAmountLineTempL."Line Amount" := CalcAmountUnrounded(ServLineTempG);
            TotalAmountL := TotalAmountL + ServLineTempG.Amount;
          END;
          VATAmountLineTempL.InsertLine();
        UNTIL ServLineTempG.NEXT = 0;

      // Add the rounded total "Amount Including VAT" for each detected VAT %
      IF VATAmountLineTempL.FINDSET THEN
        IF NOT GeneralLedgerSetupG.EnhancedVATCalculationLogicInDocActive(ServHdrL."VAT Calculation Logic") THEN BEGIN
          REPEAT
            TotalAmountRoundedL := TotalAmountRoundedL + ROUND(VATAmountLineTempL."Amount Including VAT", CurrencyG."Amount Rounding Precision", CurrencyG.VATRoundingDirection);
          UNTIL VATAmountLineTempL.NEXT = 0;
          TotalDifferenceL := ROUND(TotalAmountRoundedL - TotalAmountL, CurrencyG."Amount Rounding Precision", CurrencyG.VATRoundingDirection);
          "Amount Including VAT" := "Amount Including VAT" + TotalDifferenceL;
        END ELSE BEGIN
          REPEAT
            TotalAmountRoundedL := TotalAmountRoundedL + ROUND(VATAmountLineTempL."Line Amount", CurrencyG."Amount Rounding Precision");
          UNTIL VATAmountLineTempL.NEXT = 0;
          TotalDifferenceL := ROUND(TotalAmountRoundedL - TotalAmountL, CurrencyG."Amount Rounding Precision");
          Amount := Amount + TotalDifferenceL;
          OriginalAmountL := CalcOriginalAmount(Rec);
          NewLineDiscountAmountL := OriginalAmountL - Amount;
          IF NewLineDiscountAmountL <> "Line Discount Amount" THEN BEGIN
            "Line Discount Amount" := NewLineDiscountAmountL;
            IF OriginalAmountL <> 0 THEN
              "Line Discount %" := ROUND("Line Discount Amount" / OriginalAmountL * 100, 0.00001)
            ELSE
              "Line Discount %" := 0;
          END ELSE
            IF "Line Discount Amount" = 0 THEN
              "Line Discount %" := 0;
        END;
      // Stop EU.0104306
      // Stop PA041187.90442
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE UpdateLineVATAmountRounding@1109400040(SkipCurrentLineP@1000000000 : Boolean);
    VAR
      RecL@10430600 : Record 5025625;
    BEGIN
      // @ New function to detect cent rounding difference coming from the 2 decimals "VAT Amount" calculation of the "Amount" and the "Amount including VAT"
      // @ In case there are some the difference it added to the current "Amount including VAT"
      // Start PA042968
      // Add the unrounded "Amount Including VAT" for the other lines
      // Start EU.0104306
      RecL.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
      RecL.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
      RecL.SETFILTER(Type, '<>%1', Type::" ");
      RecL.SETFILTER(Quantity, '<>0');
      RecL.SETFILTER("Unit Price", '<>0');
      // Start EU.0132795
      RecL.SETFILTER("Line Discount %", '<>100');
      // Stop EU.0132795
      RecL.SETRANGE("VAT %","VAT %");
      RecL.SETRANGE("Bill-to Customer No.","Bill-to Customer No.");
      RecL.SETRANGE("VAT Calculation Type", "VAT Calculation Type");
      RecL.SETRANGE("VAT Identifier", "VAT Identifier");
      IF "VAT Calculation Type" = "VAT Calculation Type"::"Exch. Parts Tax" THEN BEGIN
        AdjustRoundingRestOneVAT(Rec, RecL, FIELDNO("Exch. Parts Tax Base"), SkipCurrentLineP);
        AdjustRoundingRestOneVAT(Rec, RecL, FIELDNO("Exch. Parts Tax Amount"), SkipCurrentLineP);
      END;
      IF NOT GeneralLedgerSetupG.EnhancedVATCalculationLogicInDocActive(ServHdrG."VAT Calculation Logic") THEN BEGIN
        AdjustRoundingRestOneVAT(Rec, RecL, FIELDNO("Amount Including VAT"), SkipCurrentLineP);
      END ELSE BEGIN
        RecL.SETRANGE("Fixed Price", 0);
        RecL.SETRANGE("Has Fixed Price", FALSE);
        AdjustRoundingRestOneVAT(Rec, RecL, FIELDNO(Amount), SkipCurrentLineP);
      END;
      // Stop EU.0104306
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE AdjustRoundingRestOneVAT@1000000004(VAR CurLineP@1000000006 : Record 5025625;VAR LineP@1000000005 : Record 5025625;AdjustmentFieldIDP@1000000004 : Integer;SkipCurrentLineP@1000000000 : Boolean);
    VAR
      LastLineL@13279500 : Record 5025625;
      ExLineL@10430600 : Record 5025625;
      CurrencyL@1001 : Record 4;
      TotalAmountUnroundedL@1109400001 : Decimal;
      TotalAmountL@1002 : Decimal;
      CurrLineProcessedL@10430601 : Boolean;
      UseTotalAmountsL@13279501 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // @ New function to detect cent rounding difference coming from the 2 decimals "VAT Amount" calculation of the "Amount" and the "Amount including VAT"
      // @ In case there are some the difference it added to the current "Amount including VAT"
      // Start PA042968
      // Add the unrounded "Amount Including VAT" for the other lines
      // Start EU.0104306
      CurrencyL := CurrencyG;
      IF AdjustmentFieldIDP = FIELDNO(Amount) THEN
        CASE CurrencyG.VATRoundingDirection OF
          '>':
            CurrencyL."VAT Rounding Type" := CurrencyL."VAT Rounding Type"::Down;
          '<':
            CurrencyL."VAT Rounding Type" := CurrencyL."VAT Rounding Type"::Up;
        END;

      // Start EU.0132795
      IF LineP.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        UseTotalAmountsL :=
           (CurLineP."VAT Calculation Type" IN [CurLineP."VAT Calculation Type"::"Normal VAT", CurLineP."VAT Calculation Type"::"Reverse Charge VAT"]) AND
           (AdjustmentFieldIDP IN [FIELDNO("Amount Including VAT"), FIELDNO(Amount)]);
      // Stop EU.0132795
        REPEAT
          ExLineL := LineP;
          IF LineP."Line No." = CurLineP."Line No." THEN BEGIN
      // Start EU.0138596
            CurrLineProcessedL := TRUE;
      // Stop EU.0138596
            IF NOT SkipCurrentLineP THEN
      // Start EU.0132795
              AdjustVATRoundingRestOneLine(CurLineP, AdjustmentFieldIDP, CurrencyL, TotalAmountUnroundedL, TotalAmountL, UseTotalAmountsL);
          END ELSE BEGIN
            AdjustVATRoundingRestOneLine(LineP, AdjustmentFieldIDP, CurrencyL, TotalAmountUnroundedL, TotalAmountL, UseTotalAmountsL);
      // Stop EU.0132795
            IF (LineP.Amount <> ExLineL.Amount) OR
               (LineP."Amount Including VAT" <> ExLineL."Amount Including VAT") OR
               (LineP."Line Discount %" <> ExLineL."Line Discount %") OR
      // Start EU.0138596
               (LineP."Autom. Rounding Disc. %" <> ExLineL."Autom. Rounding Disc. %") OR
      // Stop EU.0138596
               (LineP."Exch. Parts Tax Base" <> ExLineL."Exch. Parts Tax Base") OR
               (LineP."Exch. Parts Tax Amount" <> ExLineL."Exch. Parts Tax Amount")
            THEN BEGIN
              IF LineP."Line No." <> CurLineP."Line No." THEN
                LineP.UpdateLineSplittCalculation(FALSE);
              LineP.MODIFY;
            END;
          END;
      // Start EU.0138596
      // Stop EU.0138596
        UNTIL LineP.NEXT = 0;
        IF NOT CurrLineProcessedL THEN
          IF NOT SkipCurrentLineP THEN
      // Start EU.0132795
      // Start EU.0138596
            IF CurLineP."Line No." <> 0 THEN
      // Stop EU.0138596
              AdjustVATRoundingRestOneLine(CurLineP, AdjustmentFieldIDP, CurrencyL, TotalAmountUnroundedL, TotalAmountL, UseTotalAmountsL)
      END;
      // Stop EU.0132795
      // Stop EU.0104306
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE AdjustVATRoundingRestOneLine@10430600(VAR LineP@1000000005 : Record 5025625;AdjustmentFieldIDP@1000000004 : Integer;CurrencyP@10430601 : Record 4;VAR TotalAmountUnroundedP@10430603 : Decimal;VAR TotalAmountP@10430602 : Decimal;UseTotalAmountsP@13279501 : Boolean);
    VAR
      DummyLineL@13279502 : Record 5025625;
    BEGIN
      // @ New function to detect cent rounding difference in one line
      // @ UseTotalAmountsP = indicator which controls if the rounding rest is calculated over summed up single line values or the sum on all lines.
      // @                    True = All lines are summed up and then the VAT is calculated to - or out of it.
      // @                    False = In each line the VAT is calculated to - or of the Amount and then the values are summed up to totals.
      // @                            This method must be used for all lines which are not "VAT Calculation Type"::"Normal VAT" or "Reverse Charge VAT".
      // @                    Each way sound identical but there can be a small rounding happen when we don't use the "True" way.
      // Start EU.0104306
      CASE AdjustmentFieldIDP OF
        FIELDNO("Exch. Parts Tax Base"):
          BEGIN
      // Start EU.0132795
            TotalAmountUnroundedP += CalcOriginalAmount(LineP) * LineP."Exch. Parts Tax %" / 100;
            LineP."Exch. Parts Tax Base" := ROUND(TotalAmountUnroundedP, CurrencyP."Amount Rounding Precision", CurrencyP.VATRoundingDirection) - TotalAmountP;
            TotalAmountP += LineP."Exch. Parts Tax Base";
      // Stop EU.0132795
          END;
        FIELDNO("Exch. Parts Tax Amount"):
          BEGIN
      // Start EU.0132795
            TotalAmountUnroundedP += LineP."Exch. Parts Tax Base" * LineP."Exch. Parts VAT %" / 100;
            LineP."Exch. Parts Tax Amount" := ROUND(TotalAmountUnroundedP, CurrencyP."Amount Rounding Precision", CurrencyP.VATRoundingDirection) - TotalAmountP;
            TotalAmountP += LineP."Exch. Parts Tax Amount";
      // Stop EU.0132795
          END;
        FIELDNO("Amount Including VAT"):
          BEGIN
      // Start EU.0132795
            IF UseTotalAmountsP THEN BEGIN
              TotalAmountUnroundedP += LineP.Amount;
              DummyLineL := LineP;
              DummyLineL.Amount := TotalAmountUnroundedP;
              DummyLineL."Amount Including VAT" := DummyLineL.CalcVATAmountUnrounded(DummyLineL);
            END ELSE BEGIN
              TotalAmountUnroundedP += CalcVATAmountUnrounded(LineP);
              DummyLineL."Amount Including VAT" := TotalAmountUnroundedP;
            END;
            LineP."Amount Including VAT" := ROUND(DummyLineL."Amount Including VAT", CurrencyP."Amount Rounding Precision", CurrencyP.VATRoundingDirection) - TotalAmountP;
            TotalAmountP += LineP."Amount Including VAT";
      // Stop EU.0132795
          END;
        FIELDNO(Amount):
          BEGIN
      // Start EU.0132795
            IF UseTotalAmountsP THEN BEGIN
              TotalAmountUnroundedP += LineP."Amount Including VAT";
              DummyLineL := LineP;
              DummyLineL."Amount Including VAT" := TotalAmountUnroundedP;
              DummyLineL.Amount := DummyLineL.CalcAmountUnrounded(DummyLineL);
            END ELSE BEGIN
              TotalAmountUnroundedP += CalcVATAmountUnrounded(LineP);
              DummyLineL.Amount := TotalAmountUnroundedP;
            END;
            LineP.Amount := ROUND(DummyLineL.Amount, CurrencyP."Amount Rounding Precision", CurrencyP.VATRoundingDirection) - TotalAmountP;
            TotalAmountP += LineP.Amount;
            GetServHeader();
            // Calc new Line Discount
            CalcLineDiscount(
              LineP.Amount,
              LineP."Line Discount Amount",
              LineP."Line Discount %",
      // Start EU.0138596
              LineP."Autom. Rounding Disc. Amount",
              LineP."Autom. Rounding Disc. %",
      // Stop EU.0138596
              CurrencyP."Amount Rounding Precision",
              CalcOriginalAmountUnrounded(LineP.Quantity, LineP."Unit Price", ServHdrG."Prices Including VAT", LineP."VAT Calculation Type", LineP."VAT %"));
      // Stop EU.0132795
          END;
      END;
      // Stop EU.0104306
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalcLineDiscount@12971300(AmountP@1000000005 : Decimal;VAR LineDiscountAmountP@12971303 : Decimal;VAR LineDiscountP@12971302 : Decimal;VAR RoundingDiscountAmountP@1385961 : Decimal;VAR RoundingDiscountP@1385960 : Decimal;AmountRoundingPrecisionP@12971300 : Decimal;OriginalAmountP@12971301 : Decimal);
    BEGIN
      // @ Function to calculate the Line Discount % and the Discount Amount
      // Start EU.0132795
      OriginalAmountP := ROUND(OriginalAmountP, AmountRoundingPrecisionP);
      // Start EU.0138596
      IF OriginalAmountP = 0 THEN BEGIN
        LineDiscountP := 0;
        LineDiscountAmountP := 0;
        RoundingDiscountP := 0;
        RoundingDiscountAmountP := 0;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        LineDiscountP := LineDiscountP - RoundingDiscountP;
        RoundingDiscountAmountP := OriginalAmountP - AmountP - (LineDiscountAmountP - RoundingDiscountAmountP);
        IF OriginalAmountP <> 0 THEN
          RoundingDiscountP := ROUND(RoundingDiscountAmountP / OriginalAmountP * 100, 0.00001)
        ELSE
          RoundingDiscountP := 0;
        LineDiscountP := LineDiscountP + RoundingDiscountP;
        LineDiscountAmountP := ROUND(OriginalAmountP * LineDiscountP / 100, AmountRoundingPrecisionP);
      END;
      // Stop EU.0138596
      // Stop EU.0132795
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalcVATAmountUnrounded@1109400039(VAR ServLineP@1109400001 : Record 5025625) : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      // @ New function to calculate "Amount including VAT" out of the Amount with high precision
      // Start PA040295
      CASE ServLineP."VAT Calculation Type" OF
        "VAT Calculation Type"::"Normal VAT",
      // Start PA040962
        "VAT Calculation Type"::"Reverse Charge VAT":
          EXIT(ServLineP.Amount + ServLineP.Amount * ServLineP."VAT %" / 100);
        "VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax":
          EXIT(ServLineP.Amount + ServLineP."VAT Base Amount" * ServLineP."VAT %" / 100);
      // Stop PA040962
        "VAT Calculation Type"::"Exch. Parts Tax":
      // Start PA042968
          EXIT(ServLineP.Amount + ServLineP."VAT Base Amount" * ServLineP."VAT %" / 100 + ServLineP."Exch. Parts Tax Amount");
      // Stop PA042968
        "VAT Calculation Type"::"Sales Tax":
      // Start PA040837
          BEGIN
            GetServHeader();
            EXIT(ServLineP.Amount + CalcSalesTaxG.CalculateTax(
              ServLineP."Tax Area Code",
              ServLineP."Tax Group Code",
              ServLineP."Tax Liable",
              ServHdrG."Posting Date",
              ServLineP."VAT Base Amount",
              ServLineP.Quantity,
              ServHdrG."Currency Factor"));
          END;
      // Stop PA040837
        "VAT Calculation Type"::"Full VAT":
          EXIT(ServLineP."Amount Including VAT");
      END;
      // Stop PA040295
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalcAmountUnrounded@10329508(VAR RecP@1109400001 : Record 5025625) : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      // @ New function to calculate Amount out of the "Amount including VAT" with high precision
      // Start EU.0104306
      CASE RecP."VAT Calculation Type" OF
        "VAT Calculation Type"::"Normal VAT",
        "VAT Calculation Type"::"Reverse Charge VAT":
          EXIT(RecP."Amount Including VAT" / (1 + RecP."VAT %" / 100));
        "VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax":
          EXIT(RecP."VAT Base Amount" * RecP.Quantity * RecP."Unit Cost");
        "VAT Calculation Type"::"Exch. Parts Tax":
          BEGIN
            GetServHeader();
            EXIT((RecP."Amount Including VAT" - RecP."Exch. Parts Tax Amount") / (1 + (1 - ServHdrG."VAT Base Discount %" / 100) * RecP."VAT %" / 100));
          END;
        "VAT Calculation Type"::"Sales Tax":
          BEGIN
            GetServHeader();
            EXIT(CalcSalesTaxG.ReverseCalculateTax(
              RecP."Tax Area Code",
              RecP."Tax Group Code",
              RecP."Tax Liable",
              ServHdrG."Posting Date",
              RecP."Amount Including VAT",
              RecP.Quantity,
              ServHdrG."Currency Factor"));
          END;
        "VAT Calculation Type"::"Full VAT":
          EXIT(0);
      // Stop EU.0104306
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalcOriginalAmount@6(LineP@1000000000 : Record 5025625) : Decimal;
    VAR
      OriginalAmountL@1000000001 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      // Start PA042968
      GetServHeader();
      // Start EU.0132795
      OriginalAmountL := CalcOriginalAmountUnrounded(LineP.Quantity, LineP."Unit Price", ServHdrG."Prices Including VAT", LineP."VAT Calculation Type", LineP."VAT %");
      // Stop EU.0132795
      EXIT(ROUND(OriginalAmountL, CurrencyG."Amount Rounding Precision"));
      // Stop PA042968
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalcOriginalAmountUnrounded@1000000000(QuantityP@12971301 : Decimal;UnitPriceP@12971302 : Decimal;PricesIncludingVATP@12971300 : Boolean;VATCalculationTypeP@12971304 : Option;VatPercentP@12971303 : Decimal) OriginalAmountR : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      // @ Function calculate the Original Amount using the Quantity, Unit Price and the VAT%
      // Start PA042968
      // Start EU.0132795
      OriginalAmountR := QuantityP * UnitPriceP;
      IF PricesIncludingVATP THEN
        CASE VATCalculationTypeP OF
      // Stop EU.0132795
          "VAT Calculation Type"::"Normal VAT",
          "VAT Calculation Type"::"Reverse Charge VAT",
          "VAT Calculation Type"::"Sales Tax":
      // Start EU.0132795
            OriginalAmountR := QuantityP * UnitPriceP / (1 + VatPercentP / 100);
        END;
      // Stop EU.0132795
      // Stop PA042968
    END;

    END;

    PROCEDURE Signed@20(ValP@1109400000 : Decimal) : Decimal;

    PROCEDURE ItemAvailability@12(AvailabilityTypeP@1109400000 : 'Date,Variant,Location,Bin');
    BEGIN
      TESTFIELD(Type,Type::Item);
      TESTFIELD("No.");
      ItemG.RESET;
      ItemG.GET("No.");
      ItemG.SETRANGE("No.","No.");
      ItemG.SETRANGE("Date Filter",0D,"Order Date");
      CASE AvailabilityTypeP OF
        AvailabilityTypeP::Date:
          BEGIN
            ItemG.SETRANGE("Variant Filter","Variant Code");
            ItemG.SETRANGE("Location Filter","Location Code");
            ItemG.SETRANGE("Bin Filter","Bin Code");
            CLEAR(ItemAvailByDateG);
            ItemAvailByDateG.LOOKUPMODE(TRUE);
            ItemAvailByDateG.SETRECORD(ItemG);
            ItemAvailByDateG.SETTABLEVIEW(ItemG);
            IF ItemAvailByDateG.RUNMODAL = ACTION::LookupOK THEN
              IF "Order Date" <> ItemAvailByDateG.GetLastDate THEN
                IF CONFIRM(C_INC006,TRUE,
                   FIELDCAPTION("Order Date"),
                   "Order Date",
                   ItemAvailByDateG.GetLastDate)
                THEN
                  VALIDATE("Order Date",ItemAvailByDateG.GetLastDate);
          END;
        AvailabilityTypeP::Variant:
          BEGIN
            ItemG.SETRANGE("Location Filter","Location Code");
            ItemG.SETRANGE("Bin Filter","Bin Code");
            CLEAR(ItemAvailByVarG);
            ItemAvailByVarG.LOOKUPMODE(TRUE);
            ItemAvailByVarG.SETRECORD(ItemG);
            ItemAvailByVarG.SETTABLEVIEW(ItemG);
            IF ItemAvailByVarG.RUNMODAL = ACTION::LookupOK THEN
              IF "Variant Code" <> ItemAvailByVarG.GetLastVariant THEN
                IF CONFIRM(C_INC006,TRUE,
                   FIELDCAPTION("Variant Code"),
                   "Variant Code",
                   ItemAvailByVarG.GetLastVariant)
                THEN
                  VALIDATE("Variant Code",ItemAvailByVarG.GetLastVariant);
          END;
        AvailabilityTypeP::Location:
          BEGIN
            ItemG.SETRANGE("Variant Filter","Variant Code");
            ItemG.SETRANGE("Bin Filter","Bin Code");
            CLEAR(ItemAvailByLocationG);
            ItemAvailByLocationG.LOOKUPMODE(TRUE);
            ItemAvailByLocationG.SETRECORD(ItemG);
            ItemAvailByLocationG.SETTABLEVIEW(ItemG);
            IF ItemAvailByLocationG.RUNMODAL = ACTION::LookupOK THEN
              IF ("Location Code" <> ItemAvailByLocationG.GetLastLocation()) AND (ItemAvailByLocationG.GetLastLocation() > '') THEN
                IF CONFIRM(C_INC006,TRUE,
                   FIELDCAPTION("Location Code"),
                   "Location Code",
                   ItemAvailByLocationG.GetLastLocation())
                THEN
                  VALIDATE("Location Code",ItemAvailByLocationG.GetLastLocation);
          END;
        AvailabilityTypeP::Bin:
          BEGIN
            ItemG.SETRANGE("Variant Filter","Variant Code");
            ItemG.SETRANGE("Location Filter","Location Code");
            CLEAR(ItemAvailByBinG);
            ItemAvailByBinG.LOOKUPMODE(TRUE);
            ItemAvailByBinG.SETRECORD(ItemG);
            ItemAvailByBinG.SETTABLEVIEW(ItemG);
            IF ItemAvailByBinG.RUNMODAL = ACTION::LookupOK THEN
              IF NOT (ItemAvailByBinG.GetLastBin IN ['',"Bin Code"]) THEN
                IF CONFIRM(C_INC006,TRUE,
                   FIELDCAPTION("Bin Code"),
                   "Bin Code",ItemAvailByBinG.GetLastBin)
                THEN
                  VALIDATE("Bin Code",ItemAvailByBinG.GetLastBin);
          END;
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CheckDiscount@33(FieldCaptionP@1109400000 : Text);
    BEGIN
      // Start PA040837
      IF CurrFieldNo <> 0 THEN
        IF NOT "Allow Discount" THEN
          IF ("Line Discount %" <> 0) OR ("Quantity Disc. %" <> 0) THEN
      // Start PA042806
            ERROR(C_INC004,FieldCaptionP);
      // Stop PA042806
      // Stop PA040837
    END;

    PROCEDURE SalesPriceCalculation@25(DeficeCalcRecP@1109400000 : Boolean);
    BEGIN
      IF (Type = Type::" ") OR ("No." = '') OR ("Line No." = 0) OR (Quantity = 0) THEN
        EXIT;
      ServMgmtG.DeleteServCalc(Rec);
      IF Type IN [Type::Item,Type::Labor] THEN BEGIN
        IF Type = Type::Item THEN
          GetItem();
        UpdateUnitPrice();
        BlockedG := FALSE;
        IF ServPkgLineG.GET("Document Type","Document No.","Package No.","Package Version No.") THEN
          BlockedG := ServPkgLineG."Line Lock";
        VALIDATE("Quantity Disc. %");
      END;
      IF Type = Type::"Ext. Service" THEN
        LoadExtServicePrice("Unit Price");
      GetServHeader();
      CurrFieldNoSavG := CurrFieldNo;
      // Start PA034249
      GetServCustomer();
      VehiclePriceCalcG.ServPriceCalculation(Rec,ServHdrG,ServCustG,ItemG,ItemPriceG."Allow Price Calculation",DeficeCalcRecP);
      // Update of SrvCustSplitUp removed from ServPriceCalculation, but needed if amount changed!
      IF NOT SkipSrvLineCustUpdateG THEN
      // Start EU.0104306
      // Start EU.0169755.170219
        SrvCustSplitMgmtG.UpdServLineCusFromServLine(ServHdrG, Rec, CurrFieldNo, FALSE, SkipSrvCustUpdateG, FALSE, "Service Job No." <> xRec."Service Job No.");
      // Stop EU.0169755.170219
      // Stop EU.0104306
      // Stop PA034249
      CurrFieldNo := CurrFieldNoSavG;
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetNextLineNo@10() : Integer;
    VAR
      LastServLineL@1109400000 : Record 5025625;
    BEGIN
      LastServLineL.LOCKTABLE;
      LastServLineL.RESET;
      LastServLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
      LastServLineL.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
      IF NOT LastServLineL.FINDLAST THEN
        CLEAR(LastServLineL);
      EXIT(LastServLineL."Line No." + 10000);
    END;

    PROCEDURE NoOnLookup@23(VAR TextP@1109400000 : Text[250];VAR MakeCodeP@1109400001 : Code[20]) ChangedR : Boolean;
    VAR
      LabMasterL@1109400002 : Record 5025601;
      ItemL@1109400003 : Record 27;
      ServMakeL@1109400005 : Record 5028685;
    BEGIN
      ChangedR := FALSE;
      ServHdrG.GET("Document Type", "Document No.");
      CASE Type OF
        Type::" ":
          BEGIN
            IF NOT StandardTextG.GET(TextP) THEN
              CLEAR(StandardTextG);
            IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(0, StandardTextG) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
              ChangedR := TRUE;
              TextP := StandardTextG.Code;
            END;
          END;
        Type::"G/L Account":
          BEGIN
            IF NOT GLAccG.GET(TextP) THEN
              CLEAR(GLAccG);
      // Start PA035497
            CLEAR(PageGLAccsListG);
            PageGLAccsListG.Def(UserGLAccG.Area::"Service Sales");
      // Start PA036549.32893
            PageGLAccsListG.SETRECORD(GLAccG);
      // Start PA036549.32893
            PageGLAccsListG.LOOKUPMODE(TRUE);
            IF PageGLAccsListG.RUNMODAL = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
              PageGLAccsListG.GETRECORD(GLAccG);
              ChangedR := TRUE;
              TextP := GLAccG."No.";
            END;
      // Stop PA035497
          END;
        Type::Item:
          BEGIN
            IF ItemL.GET(TextP) THEN
              ;
            ItemL.SETCURRENTKEY("Item Type", "Make Code", "No.");
            ServMakeL.GetServiceMakeFilter(ServHdrG."Make Code");
            ServMakeL.COPYFILTER("Service Make Code", ItemL."Make Code");
            IF ItemL.LookupWithMaster() THEN BEGIN
              ChangedR := TRUE;
              TextP := ItemL."No.";
              MakeCodeP := ItemL."Make Code";
            END;
          END;
        Type::Labor:
          BEGIN
            IF LabMasterL.GET("Data Make Code", TextP) THEN
              ;
            ServMakeL.GetServiceMakeFilter(ServHdrG."Make Code");
            ServMakeL.COPYFILTER("Service Make Code", LabMasterL."Make Code");
            IF LabMasterL.LookupWithMaster(ServHdrG."Make Code", ServHdrG."Labor Type", ServHdrG."Prod. Year") THEN BEGIN
              ChangedR := TRUE;
              TextP := LabMasterL."No.";
              MakeCodeP := LabMasterL."Make Code";
            END;
          END;
        Type::"Ext. Service":
          BEGIN
            IF NOT ExtServG.GET(TextP) THEN
              CLEAR(ExtServG);
            IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(0, ExtServG) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
              ChangedR := TRUE;
              TextP := ExtServG."No.";
            END;
          END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE NoOnAssistEdit@38() : Boolean;
    VAR
      LaborMasterL@1109400000 : Record 5029104;
      ItemMasterL@1109400001 : Record 5029101;
      ServMakeL@1109400002 : Record 5028685;
      MakeL@1109400003 : Record 12;
      LaborTimeMasterL@1109400005 : Record 5029105;
    BEGIN
      CASE Type OF
        Type::Item:
          BEGIN
            GetServHeader();
            ServMakeL.GetServiceMakeFilter(ServHdrG."Make Code");
            ServMakeL.COPYFILTER("Service Make Code", ItemMasterL."Make Code");
            IF ItemMasterL.GET("No.", "Data Make Code") THEN
              ;
            IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(0, ItemMasterL) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
      // Start PA032651
              "Data Make Code" := ItemMasterL."Make Code";
              VALIDATE("No.", ItemMasterCheckG.CheckMasterRecord(ItemMasterL));
      // Stop PA032651
      // Start PA032651
              EXIT(TRUE);
      // Stop PA032651
            END;
          END;
        Type::Labor:
          BEGIN
            GetServHeader();
            ServMakeL.GetServiceMakeFilter(ServHdrG."Make Code");
            IF NOT MakeL.GET(ServHdrG."Make Code") THEN
              MakeL.INIT;
            IF NOT MakeL."Lab. Select: Respect Lab. Type" THEN BEGIN
              ServMakeL.COPYFILTER("Service Make Code", LaborMasterL."Make Code");
              IF LaborMasterL.GET("Data Make Code", "No.") THEN
                ;
              IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(0, LaborMasterL) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
                ItemMasterCheckG.CheckLabor(LaborMasterL);
                "Data Make Code" := LaborMasterL."Make Code";
                VALIDATE("No.", LaborMasterL."No.");
      // Start PA032651
                EXIT(TRUE);
      // Stop PA032651
              END;
            END ELSE BEGIN
              LaborTimeMasterL.SETRANGE("Labor Type",ServHdrG."Labor Type");
              ServMakeL.COPYFILTER("Service Make Code", LaborTimeMasterL."Make Code");
              IF ServHdrG."Prod. Year" <> 0D THEN
                LaborTimeMasterL.SETFILTER("Prod. Year from", '<=%1|%2', ServHdrG."Prod. Year", 0D);
              LaborTimeMasterL."Make Code" := "Data Make Code";
              LaborTimeMasterL."Labor No." := "No.";
              LaborTimeMasterL."Labor Type" := ServHdrG."Labor Type";
              LaborTimeMasterL."Prod. Year from" := ServHdrG."Prod. Year";
              IF LaborTimeMasterL.FIND('=>') THEN
                ;
              IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(PAGE::"Labor Std Time Master List",LaborTimeMasterL) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
                LaborMasterL.GET(LaborTimeMasterL."Make Code",LaborTimeMasterL."Labor No.");
                ItemMasterCheckG.CheckLabor(LaborMasterL);
                "Data Make Code" := LaborMasterL."Make Code";
                VALIDATE("No.", LaborMasterL."No.");
      // Start PA032651
                EXIT(TRUE);
      // Stop PA032651
              END;
            END;
          END;
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CheckAttachedToServiceOrder@44(FieldCaptionP@1109400000 : Text);
    BEGIN
      PurchLineG.RESET;
      PurchLineG.SETCURRENTKEY("Document Type","Service Order No.","Service Order Line No.");
      PurchLineG.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
      PurchLineG.SETRANGE("Service Order No.","Document No.");
      PurchLineG.SETRANGE("Service Order Line No.","Line No.");
      IF PurchLineG.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
      // Start PA042806
        IF FieldCaptionP > '' THEN
          ERROR(C_INC001,FieldCaptionP,"Document Type",PurchLineG."Document Type",PurchLineG."Document No.")
      // Stop PA042806
        ELSE
          ERROR(C_INC002,"Document Type",PurchLineG."Document Type",PurchLineG."Document No.");
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckMaster@27();
    VAR
      SearchMakeL@1109400000 : Code[20];
    BEGIN
      ServHdrG.GET("Document Type","Document No.");
      SearchMakeL := ServHdrG."Make Code";
      IF Type <> Type::" " THEN
        TESTFIELD("No.");
      CASE Type OF
        Type::Item:
          BEGIN
      // Start EU.0195242.197191
            "No." := ItemG.ItemSearch("No.", SearchMakeL, 3, CurrFieldNo);
      // Stop EU.0195242.197191
            IF ItemG.GET("No.") THEN
              "Data Make Code" := ItemG."Make Code";
      // Start PA033958
      // Start PA044817
      // Stop PA044817
      // Stop PA033958
          END;
        Type::Labor:
          BEGIN
            "No." := LabG.LaborSearch("No.", SearchMakeL);
            IF LabG.GET(SearchMakeL,"No.") THEN
              "Data Make Code" := SearchMakeL;
          END;
        Type::"Ext. Service":
          "No." := ExtServG.ExtServiceSearch("No.");
        Type::"G/L Account":
          "No." := UserGLAccG.FindGLAccount("No.",UserGLAccG.Area::"Service Sales",USERID);
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetDepartment@26();
    VAR
      LocationL@1109400000 : Record 14;
      ServDeptL@1109400001 : Record 5028668;
      LaborL@1109400002 : Record 5025601;
      GLAccL@1109400003 : Record 15;
    BEGIN
      // Start PA036544
      IF ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::"Function",ExitPointSetupG.Type::Pre,'GetDepartment') THEN
        EXIT;
      // Stop PA036544

      // Start PA036002.26254
      "Department Code" := '';
      // Stop PA036002.26254
      GetServHeader();
      IF (Type <> Type::" ") AND ("Location Code" > '') THEN BEGIN
        LocationL.GET("Location Code");
        ServDeptL.SETRANGE("Location Code","Location Code");
        CASE Type OF
          Type::Item:
            ServDeptL.SETRANGE("Line Type",ServDeptL."Line Type"::Item);
          Type::"G/L Account":
      // Start PA036002.26254
            BEGIN
              IF GLAccL.GET("No.") THEN BEGIN
                IF GLAccL."Global Dimension 1 Code" <> '' THEN
                  "Department Code" := GLAccL."Global Dimension 1 Code";
              END;
      // Stop PA036002.26254
              ServDeptL.SETRANGE("Line Type",ServDeptL."Line Type"::"G/L Account");
      // Start PA036002.26254
            END;
      // Stop PA036002.26254
          Type::Labor:
            ServDeptL.SETRANGE("Line Type",ServDeptL."Line Type"::Labor);
          Type::"Ext. Service":
            ServDeptL.SETRANGE("Line Type",ServDeptL."Line Type"::"Ext. Service");
        END;
      // Start PA043459
        IF Type = Type::Labor THEN BEGIN
          ServDeptL.SETRANGE("Charging Group No.",'');
          IF (LaborL.GET("Data Make Code","No.")) AND (LaborL."Charging Group" > '') THEN BEGIN
            ServDeptL.SETRANGE("Charging Group No.",LaborL."Charging Group");
            IF ServDeptL.ISEMPTY THEN
              ServDeptL.SETRANGE("Charging Group No.",'');
          END;
        END;
      // Stop PA043459
      // Start PA036002.26254
        IF "Department Code" = '' THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA036002.26254
          IF ServDeptL.FINDFIRST AND (ServDeptL."Department Code" > '') THEN
            "Department Code" := ServDeptL."Department Code"
          ELSE
            IF LocationL."Department Code" > '' THEN
              "Department Code" := LocationL."Department Code"
            ELSE
              "Department Code" := ServHdrG."Department Code";
      // Start PA036002.26254
        END;
      // Stop PA036002.26254
      END ELSE BEGIN
        "Department Code" := ServHdrG."Department Code";
      END;

      // Start PA036544
      ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::"Function",ExitPointSetupG.Type::Post,'GetDepartment');
      // Stop PA036544
    END;

    PROCEDURE DeleteFixedPrice@32();
    VAR
      RecL@10430600 : Record 5025625;
    BEGIN
      // If an entry is made, then the package fixed price has to be deleted from the service package line
      IF CurrFieldNo > 0 THEN BEGIN
        IF ServPkgLineG.GET("Document Type","Document No.","Package No.","Package Version No.") THEN BEGIN
      // Start PA032589
      // The following Modify had been commented by PA031288. However we need this modify here because OnValidate "Unit Price"
      // will modify all lines if the user confirms to re-calculate the sales prices of a package. Thus all lines will be modified.
      // Without this modify here all changes so fare would be lost and the user would get the error "Antoher user has changed..."
          MODIFY;
      // Stop PA032589
      // Start EU.0104306
          RecL.SETRANGE("Document Type", "Document Type");
          RecL.SETRANGE("Document No.", "Document No.");
          RecL.SETRANGE("Package No.", "Package No.");
          RecL.SETRANGE("Package Version No.", "Package Version No.");
          RecL.MODIFYALL("Has Fixed Price", FALSE);
      // Stop EU.0104306
          ServPkgLineG.VALIDATE("Unit Price",0);
      // Start EU.0161230.160507
          ServPkgLineG.VALIDATE("Unit Price Incl. VAT", 0);
      // Stop EU.0161230.160507
          ServPkgLineG.MODIFY;
      // Start EU.0104306
          GET(RECORDID);
      // Stop EU.0104306
        END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetServCustomer@4();
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0143914.143790
      IF "Bill-to Customer No." = '' THEN
        IF GetServiceJob() AND (ServJobG."Bill-to Customer No." > '') THEN
          "Bill-to Customer No." := ServJobG."Bill-to Customer No."
        ELSE
          "Bill-to Customer No." := ServHdrG."Bill-to Customer No.";
      // Stop EU.0143914.143790
      // Start PA034249
      IF (ServCustG."Document Type" <> "Document Type") OR (ServCustG."Document No." <> "Document No.") OR
         (ServCustG."Bill-to Customer No." <> "Bill-to Customer No.")
      THEN BEGIN
      // Start PA035937
        IF NOT ServCustG.GET("Document Type","Document No.","Bill-to Customer No.") THEN
          CLEAR(ServCustG);
      // Stop PA035937
      END;
      // Stop PA034249
    END;

      // Start PA034249

    END;

    PROCEDURE ShowReservationEntries@35(PageRunModalP@1109400000 : Boolean);
    BEGIN
      TESTFIELD(Type,Type::Item);
      TESTFIELD("No.");
      IF Signed("Quantity (Base)") < 0 THEN BEGIN
        ReservMgtG.InitFilterAndSortingLookupFor(ReservEntryG,TRUE);
        ReservMgtG.ServFilterReservFor(ReservEntryG,Rec);
      END ELSE BEGIN
        ReservMgtG.InitFilterAndSortingLookupFrom(ReservEntryG,TRUE);
        ReservMgtG.ServFilterReservFrom(ReservEntryG,Rec);
      END;
      IF PageRunModalP THEN
        PAGE.RUNMODAL(PAGE::"Reservation Entries",ReservEntryG)
      ELSE
        PAGE.RUN(PAGE::"Reservation Entries",ReservEntryG);
    END;

    PROCEDURE AutoReserve@5(ShowReservationPageP@1109400000 : Boolean);
    BEGIN
      TESTFIELD(Type,Type::Item);
      TESTFIELD("No.");
      ReservSetupG.GET;
      IF ((("Document Type" = "Document Type"::Quote) AND (ReservSetupG."Auto Service Quote")) OR
         (("Document Type" = "Document Type"::Order) AND (ReservSetupG."Auto Service Order")) OR
      // Start EU.0004860
         (("Document Type" = "Document Type"::Scheduling) AND (ReservSetupG."Auto Service Scheduling")) AND
      // Stop EU.0004860
         (ReservMgtG.ServReservQty(Rec,FALSE) > 0))
      THEN BEGIN
        ReservMgtG.ServSetReservFor(Rec);
        TESTFIELD("Order Date");
        ReservMgtG.AutoReserve(
          FullAutoReservationG,
          CALCDATE(ReservSetupG."Valid-to Formula","Order Date"),
          '',
          "Order Date");
        FIND;
        IF NOT FullAutoReservationG AND ShowReservationPageP THEN BEGIN
          COMMIT;
      // Start PA032651
          IF CONFIRM(C_INC_NoAutomaticReservation, TRUE, ItemG.TABLECAPTION, "No.", Description + ' ' + "Description 2") THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA032651
            ShowReservation();
            FIND;
          END;
        END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckItemAvailable@40();
    BEGIN
      IF (CurrFieldNo <> 0) AND (Type = Type::Item) AND ("No." > '') AND ("Outstanding Quantity" > 0) THEN BEGIN
        CurrFieldNoSavG := CurrFieldNo;
        VehicleAvailOnHandG.CalculateServLine(Rec);
        CurrFieldNo := CurrFieldNoSavG;
      // Start EU.0045397.45399
        CLEAR(ServHdrG);
      // Stop EU.0045397.45399
        GetServHeader();
        ServHdrG.UpdateStatus();
        ServHdrG.MODIFY;
        IF GetServiceJob() THEN BEGIN
          ServJobG.UpdateStatus();
          ServJobG.MODIFY;
        END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE IsNotStockVehicle@37() : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // Set "With Book No."

      IF NOT VehicleG.GET(ServHdrG.VIN) THEN
        CLEAR(VehicleG);
      IF VehicleG."Vehicle Status" IN [
         VehicleG."Vehicle Status"::"New Vehicle",
         VehicleG."Vehicle Status"::"Demo Vehicle",
         VehicleG."Vehicle Status"::"Used Vehicle"]
      THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      EXIT(TRUE);
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckLaborPrice@39();
    BEGIN
      IF Type <> Type::Labor THEN
        EXIT;
      IF Quantity <> 0 THEN
        LabG.GET("Data Make Code","No.");
      // Start EU.0094259.98863
      IF ("Fixed Price" <> 0) AND (Quantity <> 0) AND ("Unit Price" <> 0) THEN BEGIN
        VALIDATE(Amount,"Fixed Price");
        IF NOT SkipSrvLineCustUpdateG THEN
          SrvCustSplitMgmtG.UpdServLineCust_ServLine(ServHdrG, Rec, FALSE, SkipSrvCustUpdateG, FALSE, FALSE);
      // Stop EU.0094259.98863
      END;
      IF "No Charge" AND (Quantity <> 0) AND ("Unit Price" <> 0) THEN
        VALIDATE("Quantity Disc. %", 100);
    END;

    PROCEDURE InsertLineNoDistance@7(NoOfLinesNeededP@1109400000 : Integer;AbortOnErrorP@1109400001 : Boolean) StepValR : Integer;
    VAR
      ErrorTextL@1109400002 : Text[250];
    BEGIN
      ServLine2G.RESET;
      ServLine2G.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
      ServLine2G.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
      ServLine2G := Rec;
      IF ServLine2G.FIND('>') THEN BEGIN
        StepValR := (ServLine2G."Line No." - "Line No.") DIV (1 + NoOfLinesNeededP);
        IF StepValR = 0 THEN BEGIN
          ErrorTextL := STRSUBSTNO(C_INC019,
            TABLECAPTION,
            FIELDCAPTION("Document Type"),
            "Document Type",
            FIELDCAPTION("Document No."),
            "Document No.",
            "Line No.",
            ServLine2G."Line No.");
          IF AbortOnErrorP THEN
            ERROR(ErrorTextL)
          ELSE
            MESSAGE(ErrorTextL);
        END;
      END ELSE
        StepValR := 10000;
    END;

    PROCEDURE UpdateFieldInAttachedLines@46(UpdateFieldNoP@1109400001 : Integer);
    VAR
      ServLineL@1109400000 : Record 5025625;
      DepItemMakeSetupL@1101257463 : Record 5205395;
    BEGIN
      // @ This line will update a specific field value in all attached lines
      // Start PA044975
      IF "Line No." = 0 THEN
        EXIT;

      // Start EU.0078549
      IF UpdateFieldNoP IN [FIELDNO(Quantity), FIELDNO("Qty. to Ship"), FIELDNO("Qty. to Invoice"),FIELDNO("Service Job No."),
        FIELDNO("Resource No.")]
      THEN BEGIN
      // Stop EU.0078549
        ServLineL.RESET;
      // Stop PA044975
        ServLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
        ServLineL.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
      // Start PA043750.95994
        ServLineL.SETFILTER(Type, '<>%1', Type::" ");
      // Stop PA043750.95994
      // Start PA044975
        ServLineL.SETRANGE("Attached to Line No.", "Line No.");
      // Stop PA044975
      // Start PA042806
      // Start PA039241
      // Start EU.0078549
        IF ServLineL.FINDSET(TRUE) THEN
      // Stop EU.0078549
      // Stop PA039241
          REPEAT
            CASE UpdateFieldNoP OF
      // Start PA044975
              FIELDNO(Quantity), FIELDNO("Qty. to Ship"), FIELDNO("Qty. to Invoice"):
                BEGIN
                  IF Quantity = 0 THEN BEGIN
                    ServLineL.VALIDATE("Qty. to Ship", 0);
                    ServLineL.VALIDATE("Qty. to Invoice", 0);
                    IF ServLineL."Quantity Multiplier" = 0 THEN
                      ServLineL.VALIDATE(Quantity, ServLineL."Quantity Shipped")
                    ELSE
                      ServLineL.VALIDATE(Quantity, 0);
                  END ELSE
                    IF (ServLineL."Quantity Multiplier" <> 0) OR (ServLineL.Quantity = 0) THEN
                      ServLineL.VALIDATE(Quantity, AddtlItemG.CalcServiceQty(Quantity, ServLineL.Quantity, Rec, ServLineL));
      // Start PA033986
                  IF ServLineL."Quantity Multiplier" <> 0 THEN
                    IF ServLineL."Additional Item" <> ServLineL."Additional Item"::" " THEN
                      ServLineL.VALIDATE("Qty. to Ship", AddtlItemG.CalcServiceQty("Qty. to Ship", ServLineL."Qty. to Ship", Rec, ServLineL));
                  IF ServLineL."Quantity Multiplier" <> 0 THEN
                    IF ServLineL."Additional Item" <> ServLineL."Additional Item"::" " THEN
                      ServLineL.VALIDATE("Qty. to Invoice", AddtlItemG.CalcServiceQty("Qty. to Invoice", ServLineL."Qty. to Invoice", Rec, ServLineL));
      // Stop PA033986
      // Stop PA044975
                END;
              FIELDNO("Service Job No."):
                ServLineL.VALIDATE("Service Job No.", "Service Job No.");
              FIELDNO("Resource No."):
                ServLineL.VALIDATE("Resource No.", "Resource No.");
            END;
            ServLineL.MODIFY;
          UNTIL ServLineL.NEXT = 0;
      // Start EU.0078549
      END;
      // Stop EU.0078549

      // Start PA035101
      IF Type = Type::Item THEN
        DepItemMakeSetupL.CheckDepositServLine(Rec);
      // Stop PA042806
      // Stop PA035101
    END;

    PROCEDURE CreatedRelatedLines@41(VAR ServLineP@1109400000 : Record 5025625) DoPageUpdateR : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // @ Wrapper function for function CreatedRelatedLinesWithStepWidth.
      // @ It will use "0" as LineNoStepWidthP which will make the final additional line creation routine to look for a
      // @ decent step width by itself.
      // Start PA044975
      EXIT(CreatedRelatedLinesWithStepWidth(ServLineP, 0));
      // Stop PA044975
    END;

    PROCEDURE CreatedRelatedLinesWithStepWidth@1055602(VAR ServLineP@1109400000 : Record 5025625;LineNoStepWidthP@1055600 : Integer) DoPageUpdateR : Boolean;
    VAR
      StdTimeL@1109400001 : Codeunit 5025637;
      TransfExtTextL@1109400002 : Codeunit 5028653;
      AddItemFuncL@1109400003 : Codeunit 5028716;
    BEGIN
      // @ The function will call the appropriate function in codeunit "Additional Item - Functions"
      // @ It can consider a given Step Width for the Line number creation.
      // Start PA044975
      DoPageUpdateR := FALSE;
      // Start PA034249
      IF (ServLineP.Type = ServLineP.Type::Labor) AND (ServLineP."No." > '') THEN
        ServLineP.VALIDATE(Quantity, Quantity);
      // Stop PA034249
      CASE ServLineP.Type OF
        ServLineP.Type::Item:
          IF AddItemFuncL.CopyToService(ServLineP, LineNoStepWidthP, AddtlItemG.FIELDCAPTION("Consider in Service Sales")) THEN
            DoPageUpdateR := TRUE;
        Type::Labor:
          IF StdTimeL.ServicePaintAddtlLine(Rec) THEN
            DoPageUpdateR := TRUE;
      END;
      IF TransfExtTextL.ServCheckIfExtText(ServLineP, FALSE) THEN BEGIN
        TransfExtTextL.ServInsertExtText(ServLineP);
      END;
      IF TransfExtTextL.Update THEN
        DoPageUpdateR := TRUE;
      // Start PA034249
      ServMgmtG.BillToCustNo2AttachedLines(TRUE, ServLineP);
      // Stop PA034249
      // Stop PA044975
    END;

    PROCEDURE DeleteRelatedLines@42(WithConfirmationP@1109400000 : Boolean);
    VAR
      ServLineL@1109400001 : Record 5025625;
      RemoveLineRelationL@19524200 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      IF "Line No." <> 0 THEN BEGIN
      // Start EU.0078549
        ServLineL.SETCURRENTKEY("Document Type","Document No.","Attached to Line No.","Additional Item");
      // Stop EU.0078549

        ServLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type", "Document Type");
        ServLineL.SETRANGE("Document No.", "Document No.");
        ServLineL.SETRANGE("Attached to Line No.", "Line No.");
      // Start EU.0195242
        ServLineL.SETRANGE(Type, Type::Item);
        ServLineL.SETRANGE("Additional Item", ServLineL."Additional Item"::"Additional Item", ServLineL."Additional Item"::Deposit);
        IF WithConfirmationP AND (Type <> Type::Labor) THEN
          IF NOT ServLineL.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
            IF ServLineL.COUNT = 1 THEN
              RemoveLineRelationL := CONFIRM(C_INC022, TRUE)
            ELSE
              RemoveLineRelationL := CONFIRM(C_INC021, TRUE, ServLineL.COUNT);
            IF NOT RemoveLineRelationL THEN BEGIN
              ServLineL.MODIFYALL("Additional Item",ServLineL."Additional Item"::" ");
              ServLineL.MODIFYALL("Quantity Multiplier",0);
              ServLineL.MODIFYALL("Attached to Line No.",0);
            END;
          END;
      // Start EU.0210554.211799
        IF NOT (ArchReasonG IN [ArchServHdrG."Reason for Archiving"::Post,ArchServHdrG."Reason for Archiving"::"Delete Completed Document"]) THEN
      // Stop EU.0210554.211799
          TransferExtendedTextG.DeleteServLines(Rec);
        ServLineL.SETRANGE(Type);
        ServLineL.SETRANGE("Additional Item");
        IF Type <> Type::Labor THEN
          ServLineL.SETFILTER("Line No.",'<>%1', "Line No.");
      // Start PA041187.94021
        IF ServLineL.FINDSET(TRUE) THEN
      // Stop EU.0195242
          REPEAT
      // Start EU.0089938
      // Start EU.0101759.103252
            IF NOT DeletedFromHdrG THEN
      // Stop EU.0101759.103252
              IF (CurrFieldNo > 0) OR (UserSessionUnitG.GetKeyValueAsBoolean('IsCalledFromServOrdPage')) THEN BEGIN
                ServLineL.TESTFIELD("Quantity Shipped", 0);
      // Start EU.0119070.119481
                ServLineL.ServLineCustInvValidation();
      // Stop EU.0119070.119481
      // Start EU.0091608
              END;
      // Stop EU.0091608
      // Stop EU.0089938
            ServLineL.SetDeletedFromHeader(DeletedFromHdrG);
      // Start EU.0210554.209952
            IF RemoveLineRelationL THEN
      // Stop EU.0210554.209952
              ServLineL.DELETE(TRUE);
          UNTIL ServLineL.NEXT = 0;
      // Stop PA041187.94021
      // Start EU.0195242
      // Stop EU.0195242
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE LoadExtServicePrice@49(VAR ExtServPriceP@1109400000 : Decimal);
    VAR
      RecL@14166500 : Record 5025625;
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0141665.143178
      RecL := Rec;
      // Stop EU.0141665.143178
      ExtServG.GET("No.");
      ExtServPriceP := ExtServG."Unit Price";
      IF ServHdrG."Currency Code" > '' THEN BEGIN
        ServHdrG.TESTFIELD("Currency Factor");
      // Start EU.0082249
        CurrencyG.Initialize(ServHdrG."Currency Code");
      // Stop EU.0082249
        ExtServPriceP := CurrencyExchRateG.ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(GetDate,"Currency Code",ExtServPriceP, ServHdrG."Currency Factor");
      END;
      ExtServSalesPriceG.SETRANGE("Ext. Service No.","No.");
      ExtServSalesPriceG.SETFILTER("Location Code",'%1|%2',"Location Code",'');
      ExtServSalesPriceG.SETFILTER("Currency Code",'%1|%2',ServHdrG."Currency Code",'');
      ExtServSalesPriceG.SETRANGE("Valid-From Date",0D,ServHdrG."Order Date");
      ExtServSalesPriceG.SETFILTER("Valid-To Date",'=%1|>=%2',0D,ServHdrG."Order Date");
      IF ExtServSalesPriceG.FINDLAST THEN BEGIN
        ExtServPriceP := ExtServSalesPriceG."Unit Price";
        IF (ServHdrG."Currency Code" > '') AND (ExtServSalesPriceG."Currency Code" = '') THEN BEGIN
          ServHdrG.TESTFIELD("Currency Factor");
      // Start EU.0082249
          CurrencyG.Initialize(ServHdrG."Currency Code");
      // Stop EU.0082249
      // Start EU.0114873.116243
          ExtServPriceP := CurrencyExchRateG.ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(GetDate,"Currency Code", ExtServPriceP,ServHdrG."Currency Factor");
      // Stop EU.0114873.116243
        END;
      END;
      // Start EU.0141665.143178
      IF ExtServPriceP = 0 THEN
      // Start EU.0177226.179148
        IF RecL."Line Discount %" < 0 THEN
          ExtServPriceP := RecL."Unit Price" * 100 / (100 - RecL."Line Discount %")
        ELSE
          IF RecL."Line Discount %" <> 100 THEN
            ExtServPriceP := RecL."Unit Price";
      // Stop EU.0177226.179148
      // Stop EU.0141665.143178
    END;

    PROCEDURE LocationCodeAssist@5025384();
    VAR
      ItemLocationL@1109400000 : Record 5028700;
      UserLocationL@1109400001 : Record 5028664;
      LocationFilterL@1109400002 : Text[1024];
    BEGIN
      IF Type <> Type::Item THEN
        EXIT;
      UserLocationL.SETRANGE("User ID",USERID);
      IF UserLocationL.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          LocationFilterL := LocationFilterL + '|' + UserLocationL."Location Code";
        UNTIL UserLocationL.NEXT = 0;
        LocationFilterL := COPYSTR(LocationFilterL, 2);
        ItemLocationL.FILTERGROUP(2);
        ItemLocationL.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
        ItemLocationL.SETFILTER("Location Code",LocationFilterL);
        ItemLocationL.FILTERGROUP(0);
      // Start EU.0052165
        IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(0, ItemLocationL) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN
          IF "Location Code" <> ItemLocationL."Location Code" THEN
            VALIDATE("Location Code",ItemLocationL."Location Code");
      // Stop EU.0052165
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE BinCodeOnLookup@1109400096(VAR TextP@1109400000 : Text) : Boolean;
    VAR
      BinL@1109400003 : Record 5400;
      ItemBinL@1109400002 : Record 5028749;
    BEGIN
      // Start PA041146.68559
      TESTFIELD(Type, Type::Item);
      BinL.RESET;
      BinL.SETRANGE("Location Code","Location Code");
      IF BinL.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          ItemBinL.RESET;
          ItemBinL.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
          ItemBinL.SETRANGE("Location Code",BinL."Location Code");
          ItemBinL.SETRANGE("Bin Code",BinL.Code);
          IF ItemBinL.FINDFIRST THEN
            BinL.MARK(TRUE);
        UNTIL BinL.NEXT = 0;

      BinL.MARKEDONLY(TRUE);
      IF BinL.FINDFIRST THEN
        IF BinL.GET("Location Code", TextP) THEN
          ;
      IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(PAGE::Bins, BinL) <> ACTION::LookupOK THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      TextP := BinL.Code;
      EXIT(TRUE);
      // Stop PA041146.68559
    END;
