    PROCEDURE FindStatus@5025383(SkipLineNoCheckP@1055600 : Boolean);
    VAR
      ServLineL@1109400000 : Record 5025625;
      ServJobLineL@9012500 : Record 5025627;
      OldStatusCodeL@1109400002 : Code[20];
      NewStatusL@1109400003 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      // Start PA032877
      NewStatusL := FindStatus2();
      // Start EU.0078549
      IF "Line Document Status" <> NewStatusL THEN BEGIN
      // Stop EU.0078549
        "Line Document Status" := NewStatusL;
        IF ServLineL.GET("Document Type","Document No.","Line No.") THEN
          MODIFY;
      // Start EU.0078549
      END;
      // Stop EU.0078549
      // Start PA033478.I000257
      CLEAR(ServHdrG);
      // Stop PA033478.I000257
      GetServHeader();
      OldStatusCodeL := ServHdrG."Status Code";
      // Start EU.0036239
      IF SkipLineNoCheckP THEN
      // Start EU.0095631
        ServHdrG.UpdateDocStatus("Line No.")
      ELSE
        ServHdrG.UpdateStatus();
      // Stop EU.0095631
      // Stop EU.0036239
      IF OldStatusCodeL <> ServHdrG."Status Code" THEN
      // Start EU.0044141
        IF NOT DeletedFromHdrG THEN
          ServHdrG.MODIFY;
      // Stop EU.0044141
      // Start EU.0095631
      IF "Service Job No." <> xRec."Service Job No." THEN
        IF xRec."Service Job No." > 0 THEN
          IF ServJobLineL.GET("Document Type","Document No.",xRec."Service Job No.") THEN BEGIN
            OldStatusCodeL := ServJobLineL."Status Code";
            ServJobLineL.UpdateDocStatus("Line No.");
            IF OldStatusCodeL <> ServJobLineL."Status Code" THEN
              ServJobLineL.MODIFY;
          END;
      IF GetServiceJob() THEN BEGIN
        OldStatusCodeL := ServJobG."Status Code";
        IF SkipLineNoCheckP THEN
          ServJobG.UpdateDocStatus("Line No.")
        ELSE
          ServJobG.UpdateStatus();
      // Stop EU.0095631
        IF OldStatusCodeL <> ServJobG."Status Code" THEN
          ServJobG.MODIFY;
      END;
      // Stop PA032877
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE FindStatus2@5025382() : Integer;
    VAR
      ServLineCustL@19400600 : Record 5025639;
      ReserveQtyOnStockL@9012500 : Decimal;
      DummyDateL@9012501 : Date;
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0095631
      CASE TRUE OF
      // Start EU.0119070.119481
      // Start EU.0123449.125338
        "Quantity Invoiced" <> 0:
      // Stop EU.0123449.125338
      // Stop EU.0119070.119481
      // Start EU.0194006.198003
          BEGIN
            ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Document Type", "Document Type");
            ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Document No.", "Document No.");
            ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Document Line No.", "Line No.");
            ServLineCustL.SETFILTER("Quantity Invoiced", '<>%1', "Quantity Invoiced");
            IF ("Qty. Shipped Not Invoiced" = 0) AND ("Quantity Shipped" = Quantity) AND ServLineCustL.ISEMPTY THEN
              EXIT("Line Document Status"::"Completely Invoiced")
            ELSE
              EXIT("Line Document Status"::"Partly Invoiced");
          END;
      // Stop EU.0194006.198003
        "Quantity Shipped" <> 0:
          IF ("Quantity Shipped" = Quantity) THEN
            EXIT("Line Document Status"::"Completely Shipped")
          ELSE
            EXIT("Line Document Status"::"Partly Shipped");

        ELSE
          BEGIN
            IF ("Reserved Quantity" > 0) AND ("Outstanding Qty. (Base)" <> 0) THEN BEGIN
              ReserveQtyOnStockL := CalculateReserveQtyOnStock(DummyDateL);
              IF (ReserveQtyOnStockL <> 0) AND (ReserveQtyOnStockL = "Outstanding Qty. (Base)") THEN
                EXIT("Line Document Status"::"Fully Reserved on Inventory");
            END;
            IF "Qty. to Ship" > 0 THEN
              EXIT("Line Document Status"::"Ready for Shipment");
          END;
      END;
      EXIT("Line Document Status"::" ");
      // Stop EU.0095631
    END;

    PROCEDURE StatusCheckFunction@45(CurrCheckFieldNoP@1109400000 : Boolean);
    BEGIN
      IF CurrCheckFieldNoP AND (CurrFieldNo = 0) THEN
        EXIT;
      // Start EU.0104306
      IF CurrFieldNo > 0 THEN
        IF CurrFieldNo = LastStatusChechOnFieldNoG THEN
          EXIT
        ELSE
          LastStatusChechOnFieldNoG := CurrFieldNo;
      // Stop EU.0104306
      GetServHeader();
      ServHdrG.ApplyStatusFunction(FALSE);
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetServiceJob@47() : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      IF "Service Job No." = 0 THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      EXIT(ServJobG.GET("Document Type","Document No.","Service Job No."));
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE IsDepositPosition@5025370();
    BEGIN
      IF ("Attached to Line No." > 0) AND ("Quantity Multiplier" <> 0) THEN BEGIN
        ServLine2G.GET("Document Type", "Document No.", "Attached to Line No.");
        ERROR(C_INC039, ServLine2G.Type, ServLine2G."No.", ServLine2G.Description);
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE FormatType@52(TypeP@1109400000 : Integer) : Text[30];

    END;

    PROCEDURE FormatDocType@48(DocTypeP@1109400000 : Integer) : Text[30];

    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CalculateUnitCost@53(ItemLedgEntryP@1000 : Record 32) : Decimal;
    VAR
      ValueLedgEntryL@1001 : Record 5802;
      CalcAdjustedCostL@1002 : Decimal;
      ExpectedAdjustedCostL@1003 : Decimal;
      UnitCostL@1004 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      ValueLedgEntryL.RESET;
      ValueLedgEntryL.SETCURRENTKEY("Item Ledger Entry No.",Inventoriable,"Expected Cost");
      ValueLedgEntryL.SETRANGE("Item Ledger Entry No.",ItemLedgEntryP."Entry No.");
      ValueLedgEntryL.SETRANGE(Inventoriable,TRUE);
      IF ItemLedgEntryP."Completely Invoiced" THEN
        ValueLedgEntryL.SETRANGE("Expected Cost",FALSE);
      IF ValueLedgEntryL.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          IF ValueLedgEntryL."Expected Cost" THEN
            ExpectedAdjustedCostL := ExpectedAdjustedCostL + ValueLedgEntryL."Adjusted Cost"
          ELSE
            CalcAdjustedCostL := CalcAdjustedCostL + ValueLedgEntryL."Adjusted Cost";
        UNTIL ValueLedgEntryL.NEXT = 0;
      UnitCostL :=
        ((ExpectedAdjustedCostL / ItemLedgEntryP.Quantity *
        (ItemLedgEntryP.Quantity - ItemLedgEntryP."Invoiced Quantity")) + CalcAdjustedCostL) /
        ItemLedgEntryP.Quantity;
      // Start EU.0210554.171367
      EXIT(ABS(ROUND(UnitCostL * "Qty. per Unit of Measure", LocalCurrencyG."Unit-Amount Rounding Precision")));
      // Stop EU.0210554.171367
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE UpdateAssocEntry@54(ModifedFieldNoP@1109400000 : Integer) : Boolean;
    VAR
      ItemLedgEntryL@1109400001 : Record 32;
      ServLineL@1109400002 : Record 5025625;
      ServLedgEntryL@1109400003 : Record 5025620;
      ExtServLedgEntryL@1109400005 : Record 5025641;
      VehicleLedgEntryL@1109400006 : Record 5025405;
      LaborLedgEntryL@1109400007 : Record 5025603;
      SalesLineL@1109400008 : Record 37;
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0188843.190996
      IF UserSessionUnitG.GetKeyValueAsBoolean('SkipUpdateAssocEntry') THEN
        EXIT(TRUE);
      // Stop EU.0188843.190996
      IF NOT ServLineL.GET("Document Type","Document No.","Line No.") THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      // Start EU.0119070.119481
      IF ServLineCustInv() THEN
      // Stop EU.0119070.119481
        EXIT(FALSE);
      GetServHeader();
      PresentRecG.GETTABLE(Rec);
      PreviousRecG.GETTABLE(xRec);
      WarrMgmtG.ModifyFunctionForFindings(PreviousRecG, PresentRecG, ServHdrG."Make Code", '');
      IF VehServContrG.ValidContrOfServCustFind(ServHdrG.VIN, ServHdrG."Document Type", ServHdrG."No.", ServHdrG."Completion Date") THEN
        ServContrMgtG.FindingsModify(PreviousRecG, PresentRecG, VehServContrG."Serv. Contract Cust. No.", '');
      // Write changed dimension back to database!
      // Update associated sales invoice lines.

      // Start EU.0078549
      IF ModifedFieldNoP IN [FIELDNO("Service Posting Group"),FIELDNO("Gen. Prod. Posting Group"),FIELDNO("Department Code"),FIELDNO("Make Code"),
         FIELDNO("Gen. Bus. Posting Group"),FIELDNO("Bill-to Customer No.")]
      THEN BEGIN
      // Stop EU.0078549
        SalesLineL.SETCURRENTKEY("Service Type","Service Order No.","Service Order Line No.");
        SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Service Type",SalesLineL."Service Type"::"G/L Account",SalesLineL."Service Type"::"Ext. Service");
        SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Service Order No.","Document No.");
        SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Service Order Line No.","Line No.");
        SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type",SalesLineL."Document Type"::Invoice);
        SalesLineL.SETFILTER(Quantity,'<>0');
        IF SalesLineL.FINDSET(TRUE) THEN
          REPEAT
      // Start PA042806
            CASE ModifedFieldNoP OF
              FIELDNO("Service Posting Group"):
                SalesLineL.VALIDATE("Service Posting Group","Service Posting Group");
              FIELDNO("Gen. Prod. Posting Group"):
                SalesLineL.VALIDATE("Gen. Prod. Posting Group","Gen. Prod. Posting Group");
              FIELDNO("Department Code"):
      // Stop PA042806
      // Start PA035597
               SalesLineL.VALIDATE("Shortcut Dimension 1 Code","Department Code");
      // Stop PA035597
      // Start PA042806
             FIELDNO("Make Code"):
      // Stop PA042806
      // Start PA035597
               SalesLineL.VALIDATE("Shortcut Dimension 2 Code","Make Code");
      // Stop PA035597
      // Start PA042806
              FIELDNO("Gen. Bus. Posting Group"):
                ERROR(C_INC054,FIELDCAPTION("Bill-to Customer No."),SalesLineL."Document Type");
              FIELDNO("Bill-to Customer No."):
      // Stop PA042806
                ERROR(C_INC054,FIELDCAPTION("Bill-to Customer No."),SalesLineL."Document Type");
            END;
            SalesLineL.MODIFY;
          UNTIL SalesLineL.NEXT = 0;
      // Start EU.0078549
      END;
      // Stop EU.0078549

      // Update Service Ledger Entry
      ServLedgEntryL.SETCURRENTKEY("Order No.","Order Line No.");
      ServLedgEntryL.SETRANGE("Order No.","Document No.");
      ServLedgEntryL.SETRANGE("Order Line No.","Line No.");
      ServLedgEntryL.SETRANGE(Open,TRUE);
      IF ServLedgEntryL.FINDSET(TRUE) THEN
        REPEAT
      // Start PA042806
          CASE ModifedFieldNoP OF
            FIELDNO("Service Posting Group"):
      // Stop PA042806
              BEGIN
                IF CheckServLedgerEntryPosted2GL(ServLedgEntryL) THEN BEGIN
                  "Dimension Change" := TRUE;
                  EXIT;
                END;
                ServLedgEntryL.VALIDATE("Service Posting Group","Service Posting Group");
              END;
      // Start PA042806
            FIELDNO("Gen. Bus. Posting Group"):
      // Stop PA042806
              BEGIN
                IF CheckServLedgerEntryPosted2GL(ServLedgEntryL) THEN BEGIN
                  "Dimension Change" := TRUE;
                  EXIT;
                END ELSE
      // Start PA042806
                  IF NOT UpdateAssocValueEntry(ServLedgEntryL, ModifedFieldNoP) THEN
      // Stop PA042806
                    EXIT;
                ServLedgEntryL.VALIDATE("Gen. Bus. Posting Group", "Gen. Bus. Posting Group");
              END;
      // Start PA042806
            FIELDNO("Gen. Prod. Posting Group"):
      // Stop PA042806
              BEGIN
                IF CheckServLedgerEntryPosted2GL(ServLedgEntryL) THEN BEGIN
                  "Dimension Change" := TRUE;
                  EXIT;
                END ELSE
      // Start PA042806
                  IF NOT UpdateAssocValueEntry(ServLedgEntryL, ModifedFieldNoP) THEN
      // Stop PA042806
                    EXIT;
                ServLedgEntryL.VALIDATE("Gen. Prod. Posting Group", "Gen. Prod. Posting Group");
              END;
      // Start PA042806
            FIELDNO("Department Code"):
      // Stop PA042806
              BEGIN
                IF CheckServLedgerEntryPosted2GL(ServLedgEntryL) THEN BEGIN
                  "Dimension Change" := TRUE;
                  EXIT;
                END ELSE
      // Start PA042806
                  IF NOT UpdateAssocValueEntry(ServLedgEntryL, ModifedFieldNoP) THEN
      // Stop PA042806
                    EXIT;
                ServLedgEntryL.VALIDATE("Department Code","Department Code");
      // Start PA036002.26542
                ServLedgEntryL."Dimension Set ID" := DimMgtG.GetDimSetID(ServLedgEntryL."Dimension Set ID",ServLedgEntryL."Department Code",ServLedgEntryL."Make Code");
      // Stop PA036002.26542
              END;
      // Start PA042806
            FIELDNO("Make Code"):
      // Stop PA042806
              BEGIN
                IF CheckServLedgerEntryPosted2GL(ServLedgEntryL) THEN BEGIN
                  "Dimension Change" := TRUE;
                  EXIT;
                END ELSE
      // Start PA042806
                  IF NOT UpdateAssocValueEntry(ServLedgEntryL, ModifedFieldNoP) THEN
      // Stop PA042806
                    EXIT;
                ServLedgEntryL.VALIDATE("Make Code","Make Code");
      // Start PA036002.26542
                ServLedgEntryL."Dimension Set ID" := DimMgtG.GetDimSetID(ServLedgEntryL."Dimension Set ID",ServLedgEntryL."Department Code",ServLedgEntryL."Make Code");
      // Stop PA036002.26542
              END;
      // Start PA042806
            FIELDNO("Sales Department Code"):
      // Stop PA042806
              BEGIN
                IF CheckServLedgerEntryPosted2GL(ServLedgEntryL) THEN BEGIN
                  "Dimension Change" := TRUE;
                  EXIT;
                END;
                ServLedgEntryL.VALIDATE("Sales Department Code","Sales Department Code");
              END;
      // Start PA042806
            FIELDNO("Bill-to Customer No."):
      // Stop PA042806
              BEGIN
                IF CheckServLedgerEntryPosted2GL(ServLedgEntryL) THEN BEGIN
      // Start PA032589
                  IF ServMgmtG.CustomerChangeIntExternCheck("Bill-to Customer No.",ServLedgEntryL."Source No. (Payment)") THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA032589
                    "Dimension Change" := TRUE;
                    EXIT;
                  END;
                END ELSE
      // Start PA042806
                  IF NOT UpdateAssocValueEntry(ServLedgEntryL,ModifedFieldNoP) THEN
      // Stop PA042806
                    EXIT;
                ServLedgEntryL.VALIDATE("Source No. (Payment)","Bill-to Customer No.");
              END;
      // Start PA042806
            FIELDNO("Location Code"):
      // Stop PA042806
              BEGIN
                IF CheckServLedgerEntryPosted2GL(ServLedgEntryL) THEN BEGIN
      // Start PA032589
                  IF ServMgmtG.CustomerChangeIntExternCheck("Bill-to Customer No.", ServLedgEntryL."Source No. (Payment)") THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA032589
                    "Dimension Change" := TRUE;
                    EXIT;
                  END;
                END ELSE
      // Start PA042806
                  IF NOT UpdateAssocValueEntry(ServLedgEntryL,ModifedFieldNoP) THEN
      // Stop PA042806
                    EXIT;
                ServLedgEntryL.VALIDATE("Location Code","Location Code");
              END;
      // Start PA042806
            FIELDNO("Service Job No."):
              ServLedgEntryL.VALIDATE("Service Job No.","Service Job No.");
            FIELDNO("Option Code"):
              ServLedgEntryL.VALIDATE("Option Code","Option Code");
            FIELDNO("Value Increasing Measure"):
      // Stop PA042806
              ServLedgEntryL.VALIDATE("Value Increasing Measure","Value Increasing Measure");
          END;
          ServLedgEntryL.MODIFY;

          // Update vehicle ledger entries
          IF VehicleLedgEntryL.GET(ServLedgEntryL."Assoc. Vehicle Entry No.") THEN BEGIN
      // Start PA042806
            CASE ModifedFieldNoP OF
              FIELDNO("Gen. Bus. Posting Group"):
                VehicleLedgEntryL.VALIDATE("Gen. Bus. Posting Group","Gen. Bus. Posting Group");
              FIELDNO("Gen. Prod. Posting Group"):
                VehicleLedgEntryL.VALIDATE("Gen. Prod. Posting Group","Gen. Prod. Posting Group");
              FIELDNO("Department Code"):
      // Stop PA042806
      // Start PA035597
                BEGIN
                  VehicleLedgEntryL.VALIDATE("Department Code","Department Code");
      // Start PA036002.26542
                  VehicleLedgEntryL."Dimension Set ID" := DimMgtG.GetDimSetID(VehicleLedgEntryL."Dimension Set ID",VehicleLedgEntryL."Department Code",VehicleLedgEntryL."Make Code");
      // Stop PA036002.26542
                END;
      // Start PA042806
              FIELDNO("Make Code"):
      // Stop PA042806
                BEGIN
                  VehicleLedgEntryL.VALIDATE("Make Code","Make Code");
      // Start PA036002.26542
                  VehicleLedgEntryL."Dimension Set ID" := DimMgtG.GetDimSetID(VehicleLedgEntryL."Dimension Set ID",VehicleLedgEntryL."Department Code",VehicleLedgEntryL."Make Code");
      // Stop PA036002.26542
                END;
      // Stop PA035597
      // Start PA042806
              FIELDNO("Bill-to Customer No."):
                VehicleLedgEntryL.VALIDATE("Source No. (Payment)","Bill-to Customer No.");
              FIELDNO("Value Increasing Measure"):
      // Stop PA042806
                BEGIN
                  VehicleLedgEntryL.VALIDATE("Value Increasing Measure","Value Increasing Measure");
                END;
            END;
            VehicleLedgEntryL.MODIFY;
            // Update corresponding item ledger entry.
            IF ItemLedgEntryL.GET(VehicleLedgEntryL."Item Ledger Entry No.") THEN BEGIN
      // Start PA042806
              CASE ModifedFieldNoP OF
                FIELDNO("Department Code"):
      // Stop PA042806
      // Start PA035597
                  BEGIN
                    ItemLedgEntryL.VALIDATE("Global Dimension 1 Code","Department Code");
      // Start PA036002.26542
                    ItemLedgEntryL."Dimension Set ID" := DimMgtG.GetDimSetID(ItemLedgEntryL."Dimension Set ID",ItemLedgEntryL."Global Dimension 1 Code",ItemLedgEntryL."Global Dimension 2 Code");
      // Stop PA036002.26542
                  END;
      // Stop PA035597
      // Start PA042806
                FIELDNO("Make Code"):
      // Stop PA042806
      // Start PA035597
                  BEGIN
                    ItemLedgEntryL.VALIDATE("Global Dimension 2 Code","Make Code");
      // Start PA036002.26542
                    ItemLedgEntryL."Dimension Set ID" := DimMgtG.GetDimSetID(ItemLedgEntryL."Dimension Set ID",ItemLedgEntryL."Global Dimension 1 Code",ItemLedgEntryL."Global Dimension 2 Code");
      // Stop PA036002.26542
                  END;
      // Stop PA035597
      // Start PA042806
                FIELDNO("Bill-to Customer No."):
                  ItemLedgEntryL.VALIDATE("Source No. (Payment)","Bill-to Customer No.");
                FIELDNO("Location Code"):
                  ItemLedgEntryL.TESTFIELD("Location Code","Location Code");
                FIELDNO("Value Increasing Measure"):
      // Stop PA042806
                  ItemLedgEntryL.VALIDATE("Value Increasing Measure","Value Increasing Measure");
              END;
              ItemLedgEntryL.MODIFY;
            END;
          END;

          // Update Labor Ledger Entries
          IF ServLedgEntryL.Type = ServLedgEntryL.Type::Labor THEN
            IF LaborLedgEntryL.GET(ServLedgEntryL."Assoc. Entry") THEN BEGIN
      // Start PA042806
              CASE ModifedFieldNoP OF
                FIELDNO("Gen. Bus. Posting Group"):
                  LaborLedgEntryL.VALIDATE("Gen. Bus. Posting Group","Gen. Bus. Posting Group");
                FIELDNO("Gen. Prod. Posting Group"):
                  LaborLedgEntryL.VALIDATE("Gen. Prod. Posting Group","Gen. Prod. Posting Group");
                FIELDNO("Department Code"):
      // Stop PA042806
      // Start PA036002.26542
                  BEGIN
                    LaborLedgEntryL.VALIDATE("Department Code","Department Code");
                    LaborLedgEntryL."Dimension Set ID" := DimMgtG.GetDimSetID(LaborLedgEntryL."Dimension Set ID",LaborLedgEntryL."Department Code",LaborLedgEntryL."Make Code");
                  END;
      // Start PA042806
                FIELDNO("Make Code"):
      // Stop PA042806
                  BEGIN
                    LaborLedgEntryL.VALIDATE("Make Code","Make Code");
                    LaborLedgEntryL."Dimension Set ID" := DimMgtG.GetDimSetID(LaborLedgEntryL."Dimension Set ID",LaborLedgEntryL."Department Code",LaborLedgEntryL."Make Code");
                  END;
      // Stop PA036002.26542
      // Start PA042806
                FIELDNO("Bill-to Customer No."):
      // Stop PA042806
                  LaborLedgEntryL.VALIDATE("Bill-to Customer No.","Bill-to Customer No.");
              END;
              LaborLedgEntryL.MODIFY;
            END;

          // Update Ext. Service Ledger Entry
          IF ServLedgEntryL.Type = ServLedgEntryL.Type::"Ext. Service" THEN
            IF ExtServLedgEntryL.GET(ServLedgEntryL."Assoc. Entry") THEN BEGIN
      // Start PA042806
              CASE ModifedFieldNoP OF
                FIELDNO("Department Code"):
      // Stop PA042806
      // Start PA036002.26542
                  BEGIN
                    ExtServLedgEntryL.VALIDATE("Department Code","Department Code");
                    ExtServLedgEntryL."Dimension Set ID" := DimMgtG.GetDimSetID(ExtServLedgEntryL."Dimension Set ID",ExtServLedgEntryL."Department Code",ExtServLedgEntryL."Make Code");
                  END;
      // Start PA042806
                FIELDNO("Make Code"):
      // Stop PA042806
                  BEGIN
                    ExtServLedgEntryL.VALIDATE("Make Code","Make Code");
                    ExtServLedgEntryL."Dimension Set ID" := DimMgtG.GetDimSetID(ExtServLedgEntryL."Dimension Set ID",ExtServLedgEntryL."Department Code",ExtServLedgEntryL."Make Code");
                  END;
      // Stop PA036002.26542
      // Start PA042806
                FIELDNO("Bill-to Customer No."):
      // Stop PA042806
                  ExtServLedgEntryL.VALIDATE("Source No. (Payment)","Bill-to Customer No.");
              END;
              ExtServLedgEntryL.MODIFY;
            END;
        UNTIL ServLedgEntryL.NEXT = 0;
      EXIT(TRUE);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE UpdateAssocValueEntry@1109400012(VAR ServLedgEntryP@1109400002 : Record 5025620;ModifedFieldNoP@1109400000 : Integer) DirektChangeR : Boolean;
    VAR
      ValueEntryL@1109400004 : Record 5802;
    BEGIN
      IF ServLedgEntryP.Type <> ServLedgEntryP.Type::Item THEN
        EXIT(TRUE);
      // Update Value Ledger Entry
      ValueEntryL.SETCURRENTKEY("Item Ledger Entry No.");
      ValueEntryL.SETRANGE("Item Ledger Entry No.",ServLedgEntryP."Assoc. Entry");
      IF NOT ValueEntryL.FINDSET(TRUE) THEN
        EXIT(TRUE);
      DirektChangeR := FALSE;
      REPEAT
      // Start PA042806
        CASE ModifedFieldNoP OF
          FIELDNO("Gen. Bus. Posting Group"):
      // Stop PA042806
            BEGIN
              IF CheckValueLedgerEntryPosted2GL(ValueEntryL) THEN BEGIN
                "Dimension Change" := TRUE;
                EXIT;
              END;
              ValueEntryL.VALIDATE("Gen. Bus. Posting Group","Gen. Bus. Posting Group");
            END;
      // Start PA042806
          FIELDNO("Gen. Prod. Posting Group"):
      // Stop PA042806
            BEGIN
              IF CheckValueLedgerEntryPosted2GL(ValueEntryL) THEN BEGIN
                "Dimension Change" := TRUE;
                EXIT;
              END;
              ValueEntryL.VALIDATE("Gen. Prod. Posting Group","Gen. Prod. Posting Group");
            END;
      // Start PA042806
          FIELDNO("Department Code"):
      // Stop PA042806
            BEGIN
              IF CheckValueLedgerEntryPosted2GL(ValueEntryL) THEN BEGIN
                "Dimension Change" := TRUE;
                EXIT;
              END;
      // Start PA035597
              ValueEntryL.VALIDATE("Global Dimension 1 Code","Department Code");
      // Start PA036002.26542
              ValueEntryL."Dimension Set ID" := DimMgtG.GetDimSetID(ValueEntryL."Dimension Set ID",ValueEntryL."Global Dimension 1 Code",ValueEntryL."Global Dimension 2 Code");
      // Stop PA036002.26542
      // Stop PA035597
            END;
      // Start PA042806
          FIELDNO("Make Code"):
      // Stop PA042806
            BEGIN
              IF CheckValueLedgerEntryPosted2GL(ValueEntryL) THEN BEGIN
                "Dimension Change" := TRUE;
                EXIT;
              END;
      // Start PA035597
              ValueEntryL.VALIDATE("Global Dimension 2 Code","Make Code");
      // Start PA036002.26542
              ValueEntryL."Dimension Set ID" := DimMgtG.GetDimSetID(ValueEntryL."Dimension Set ID",ValueEntryL."Global Dimension 1 Code",ValueEntryL."Global Dimension 2 Code");
      // Stop PA036002.26542
      // Stop PA035597
            END;
      // Start PA042806
          FIELDNO("Bill-to Customer No."):
      // Stop PA042806
            BEGIN
              IF CheckValueLedgerEntryPosted2GL(ValueEntryL) THEN
      // Start PA032589
                IF ServMgmtG.CustomerChangeIntExternCheck("Bill-to Customer No.",ValueEntryL."Source No. (Payment)") THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA032589
                  "Dimension Change" := TRUE;
                  EXIT;
                END;
              ValueEntryL.VALIDATE("Source No. (Payment)","Bill-to Customer No.");
            END;
      // Start PA042806
          FIELDNO("Location Code"):
      // Stop PA042806
            BEGIN
              ValueEntryL.TESTFIELD("Location Code","Location Code");
              EXIT;
            END;
        END;
        ValueEntryL.MODIFY;
      UNTIL ValueEntryL.NEXT = 0;
      EXIT(TRUE);
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckServLedgerEntryPosted2GL@57(VAR ServLedgEntryP@1109400000 : Record 5025620) : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      EXIT(
        (ServLedgEntryP."Amt. to Post to G/L" <> 0) OR (ServLedgEntryP."Amt. Posted to G/L" <> 0) OR
        (ServLedgEntryP."Amt. to Recognize" <> 0) OR (ServLedgEntryP."Amt. Recognized" <> 0) OR
        (ServLedgEntryP."Add.-Curr. Amt. to Post to G/L" <> 0) OR (ServLedgEntryP."Add.-Curr. Amt. Posted to G/L" <> 0) OR
        (ServLedgEntryP."Add.-Curr. Amount to Recognize" <> 0) OR (ServLedgEntryP."Add.-Curr. Amount Recognized" <> 0));
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckValueLedgerEntryPosted2GL@60(VAR ValueLedgEntryP@1109400000 : Record 5802) : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      EXIT((ValueLedgEntryP."Cost Posted to G/L" <> 0) OR (ValueLedgEntryP."Cost Posted to G/L (ACY)" <> 0));
    END;

    PROCEDURE InsertCheck@67(PerformTriggerP@1109400000 : Boolean) SuccessfulR : Boolean;
    VAR
      ServLineL@1109400001 : Record 5025625;
      SetToAutomaticL@1109400002 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      ServLineL := Rec;
      ServLineL.LOCKTABLE;
      IF ServLineL.FIND('=') THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      IF PerformTriggerP AND SetProcessTypeAutomatic THEN
        SetToAutomaticL := TRUE;
      IF PerformTriggerP THEN
        INSERT(PerformTriggerP);
      IF SetToAutomaticL THEN
        SetProcessTypeManual(TRUE);
      SuccessfulR := TRUE;
    END;

    PROCEDURE LoadUnitPrice@1109400001();
    BEGIN
      UpdateUnitPrice();
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CheckSplittCalculation@1109400002(FieldNoP@1109400001 : Integer;CheckSplitWithoutErrorP@1109400002 : Boolean) : Boolean;
    VAR
      ServLineCustL@1109400000 : Record 5025639;
      FieldCaptionL@1101175180 : Text[100];
    BEGIN
      ServLineCustL.RESET;
      ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
      ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
      ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Document Line No.","Line No.");
      // Start EU.0107753.108695
      IF ServLineCustL.COUNT = 1 THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      // Stop EU.0107753.108695
      ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Consider Price Calculation",TRUE);
      // Start PA033983
      IF NOT ServLineCustL.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
        ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Consider Price Calculation");
        ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Apply Remaining Cust. Amount", TRUE);
        IF NOT ServLineCustL.FINDFIRST THEN
      // Start PA042806
          EXIT(TRUE);
      // Stop PA042806
        FieldCaptionL := ServLineCustL.FIELDCAPTION("Apply Remaining Cust. Amount");
      END ELSE
        FieldCaptionL := ServLineCustL.FIELDCAPTION("Consider Price Calculation");
      // Start PA042806
      IF NOT CheckSplitWithoutErrorP THEN
        CASE FieldNoP OF
          FIELDNO("Unit Price"):
            ERROR(C_INC054,FIELDCAPTION("Unit Price"),FieldCaptionL);
          FIELDNO("Line Discount %"):
            ERROR(C_INC054,FIELDCAPTION("Line Discount %"),FieldCaptionL);
          FIELDNO("Line Discount Amount"):
            ERROR(C_INC054,FIELDCAPTION("Line Discount Amount"),FieldCaptionL);
          FIELDNO(Amount):
            ERROR(C_INC054,FIELDCAPTION(Amount),FieldCaptionL);
          FIELDNO("Amount Including VAT"):
            ERROR(C_INC054,FIELDCAPTION("Amount Including VAT"),FieldCaptionL);
          FIELDNO(Quantity):
            ERROR(C_INC054,FIELDCAPTION(Quantity),FieldCaptionL);
        END;
      EXIT(FALSE);
      // Stop PA042806
      // Stop PA033983
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckUserRights@1109400003(ActionTypeP@1109400001 : Integer);
    VAR
      ShowErrorL@1109400000 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // Start PA036544
      // Start PA040608
      IF ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::"Function",ExitPointSetupG.Type::Pre,'CheckUserRights') THEN
        EXIT;
      // Stop PA040608
      // Stop PA036544

      // Start PA033019
      IF "Process Type" = "Process Type"::Automatically THEN
        EXIT;
      UserSetupGet();
      CASE Type OF
        Type::" ":
          ShowErrorL := UserSetupG."Service Change Text" = UserSetupG."Service Change Text"::" ";
        Type::"G/L Account":
          ShowErrorL := UserSetupG."Service G/L Account Line" = UserSetupG."Service G/L Account Line"::" ";
        Type::Item:
          ShowErrorL := UserSetupG."Service Item Line" = UserSetupG."Service Item Line"::" ";
        Type::Labor:
          ShowErrorL := UserSetupG."Service Labor Line" = UserSetupG."Service Labor Line"::" ";
        Type::"Ext. Service":
          ShowErrorL := UserSetupG."Service Ext. Service Line" = UserSetupG."Service Ext. Service Line"::" ";
      END;
      IF ShowErrorL THEN
        ERROR(C_INC_YouHaveNoRightsToDoThat,
          SELECTSTR(ActionTypeP + 1, C_INC_InsertModifyDeleteRename),
          TABLECAPTION,
          FIELDCAPTION(Type),
          Type);
      IF (xRec.Type <> Type) AND (ActionTypeP <> ModificationTypeG::Insert) THEN
        CASE xRec.Type OF
          Type::" ":
            ShowErrorL := UserSetupG."Service Change Text" = UserSetupG."Service Change Text"::" ";
          Type::"G/L Account":
            ShowErrorL := UserSetupG."Service G/L Account Line" = UserSetupG."Service G/L Account Line"::" ";
          Type::Item:
            ShowErrorL := UserSetupG."Service Item Line" = UserSetupG."Service Item Line"::" ";
          Type::Labor:
            ShowErrorL := UserSetupG."Service Labor Line" = UserSetupG."Service Labor Line"::" ";
          Type::"Ext. Service":
            ShowErrorL := UserSetupG."Service Ext. Service Line" = UserSetupG."Service Ext. Service Line"::" ";
        END;
      IF ShowErrorL THEN
        ERROR(C_INC_YouHaveNoRightsToDoThat,
          SELECTSTR(ActionTypeP + 1, C_INC_InsertModifyDeleteRename),
          TABLECAPTION,
          FIELDCAPTION(Type),
          xRec.Type);
      // Stop PA033019

      // Start PA036544
      ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::"Function",ExitPointSetupG.Type::Post,'CheckUserRights');
      // Stop PA036544
    END;

    PROCEDURE UserSetupGet@1109400004();
    BEGIN
      IF UserSetupG."User ID" = USERID THEN
        EXIT;
      UserSetupG.GET(USERID);
    END;

      NecessaryR := TRUE;
    END;

      IF DoModifyP THEN
        IF ServLineL.GET("Document Type","Document No.","Line No.") THEN
          MODIFY;
      NecessaryR := TRUE;
    END;

    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckServOptionStatus@1109400009(VAR ServLineP@1109400000 : Record 5025625;CurrFieldNoP@1109400002 : Integer;CalledFromFieldNoP@1109400005 : Integer) IsPostedR : Boolean;
    VAR
      ServLineL@1109400003 : Record 5025625;
      ServOptionL@1109400001 : Record 5025656;
      RecRefL@1109400004 : RecordRef;
      FieldRefL@1109400006 : FieldRef;
    BEGIN
      // Check if Service Option is not already posted.
      ServLineL := ServLineP;
      IF NOT ServLineL.FIND('=') THEN
        ServLineL.INIT;
      IF NOT ServOptionL.GET(
         ServLineL."Document Type",
         ServLineL."Document No.",
         ServLineL."Service Job No.",
         ServLineL."Option Code")
      THEN
        CLEAR(ServOptionL);
      IsPostedR := ServOptionL.Posted;
      IF NOT IsPostedR THEN
        EXIT;
      IF (ServLineP."Option Code" = ServLineL."Option Code") AND
         (ServLineP."Value Increasing Measure" = ServLineL."Value Increasing Measure") AND
         (ServLineP."Service Job No." = ServLineL."Service Job No.") AND
      // Start PA032600
         (ServLineP.Quantity = ServLineL.Quantity) AND
         (ServLineP."Department Code" = ServLineL."Department Code") AND
         (ServLineP."Gen. Bus. Posting Group" = ServLineL."Gen. Bus. Posting Group") AND
         (ServLineP."Unit Price" = ServLineL."Unit Price") AND
         (ServLineP."Service Posting Group" = ServLineL."Service Posting Group") AND
         (ServLineP."Sales Department Code" = ServLineL."Sales Department Code")
      // Stop PA032600
      THEN
        EXIT;
      IF CurrFieldNoP = 0 THEN
        CurrFieldNoP := CalledFromFieldNoP;
      RecRefL.GETTABLE(ServLineP);
      FieldRefL := RecRefL.FIELD(CurrFieldNoP);
      Rec := xRec;
      ERROR(C_INC057,FieldRefL.CAPTION,RecRefL.CAPTION,ServOptionL.TABLECAPTION,ServOptionL."Option Code");
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckServJobStatus@1109400010(VAR ServLineP@1109400000 : Record 5025625) : Boolean;
    VAR
      ServJobLineL@1109400001 : Record 5025627;
      ServOptionL@1109400002 : Record 5025656;
    BEGIN
      IF NOT ServJobLineL.GET(ServLineP."Document Type",ServLineP."Document No.",ServLineP."Service Job No.") THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      IF NOT ServOptionL.GET(
         ServJobLineL."Document Type",
         ServJobLineL."Document No.",
         ServJobLineL."Line No.",ServJobLineL."Option Code")
      THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      EXIT(ServOptionL.Posted);
    END;

    PROCEDURE JobPosOnValidate@31();
    VAR
      ServJobLineL@18555900 : Record 5025627;
      ExCurrFieldNoL@18555901 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0185559
      ExCurrFieldNoL := CurrFieldNo;
      CurrFieldNo := FIELDNO("Service Job No.");
      IF "Job Pos." = 0 THEN
        VALIDATE("Service Job No.", 0)
      ELSE BEGIN
        ServJobLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type", "Document Type");
        ServJobLineL.SETRANGE("Document No.", "Document No.");
        ServJobLineL.SETRANGE("Job Pos.", "Job Pos.");
        IF NOT ServJobLineL.FINDFIRST THEN
          ERROR(C_INC_NotFound, FIELDCAPTION("Job Pos."), "Job Pos.");
        VALIDATE("Service Job No.", ServJobLineL."Line No.");
      END;
      CurrFieldNo := ExCurrFieldNoL;
      // Stop EU.0185559
    END;

    PROCEDURE ServiceJobNoOnValidate@1109450038(ResetLineValuesP@1109400003 : Boolean);
    VAR
      ServLineL@1109400002 : Record 5025625;
      ServLineCustL@1109400001 : Record 5025639;
      InvNoL@1109400000 : Integer;
      AvoidResetL@1109400004 : Boolean;
      TransactionStartedHereL@10430600 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // @ New function to Perform the OnValidate business logic when a Service Jon No is validated.
      // @ Param ResetLineValuesP - indicator if the Quantity field should be validated in order to reset a Job assignment.
      // @                          This is used when a Service Job No. has to be removed from a line.
      // Start PA042806

      // Start EU.0147204.147905
      AvoidResetL := NOT ResetLineValuesP;
      // Stop EU.0147204.147905

      GetServHeader();
      // Start PA043822
      // Start EU.0119070.119481
      IF "Service Job No." <> xRec."Service Job No." THEN
        ServLineCustInvValidation();
      // Stop EU.0119070.119481
      // Start EU.0104306
      TransactionStartedHereL := SetProcessTriggeredFromField(FIELDNO("Service Job No."));
      // Stop EU.0104306
      IF ResetLineValuesP THEN BEGIN
        IF AvoidResetLineValues() THEN BEGIN
          ResetLineValuesP := FALSE;
          AvoidResetL := TRUE;
        END;
      END;
      // Stop PA043822
      IF "Package No." > '' THEN
        CheckPackageLock(FIELDCAPTION("Service Job No."));

      CheckServOptionStatus(Rec,CurrFieldNo,FIELDNO("Service Job No."));

      // Start EU.0052165
      IF ("Service Job No." <> 0) AND GetServiceJob() THEN BEGIN
      // Stop EU.0052165
      // Start PA043750.95994
      // Start EU.0147204.147905
        IF ("Service Job No." <> xRec."Service Job No.") AND (xRec."Service Job No." <> 0) AND (Type <> Type::" ") THEN
      // Stop EU.0147204.147905
      // Stop PA043750.95994
          IF ResetLineValuesP THEN
            VALIDATE(Quantity);
        "Fair Deal" := ServJobG."Fair Deal";

        EPRecRef2G.GETTABLE(ServJobG);
        ServiceLineExitPoint(Rec, ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnValidate,ExitPointSetupG.Type::"Inside 1",FIELDNAME("Service Job No."));

        IF ServJobG."Bill-to Customer No." > '' THEN
          IF ServJobG."Bill-to Customer No." <> "Bill-to Customer No." THEN
            VALIDATE("Bill-to Customer No.",ServJobG."Bill-to Customer No.")
          ELSE
            IF NOT SkipSrvLineCustUpdateG THEN
              SrvCustSplitMgmtG.UpdServLineCust_ServLine(ServHdrG, Rec, FALSE, SkipSrvCustUpdateG, FALSE, TRUE);
        VALIDATE("Service Posting Group",ServJobG."Service Posting Group");
      // Start EU.0044639
        IF ServCustG.GET("Document Type", "Document No.", "Bill-to Customer No.") THEN
          IF "Gen. Bus. Posting Group" <> ServCustG."Default Gen. Bus. Posting Grp." THEN
           VALIDATE("Gen. Bus. Posting Group", ServCustG."Default Gen. Bus. Posting Grp.");
        IF "VAT Bus. Posting Group" <> ServJobG."VAT Bus. Posting Group" THEN
          VALIDATE("VAT Bus. Posting Group", ServJobG."VAT Bus. Posting Group");
      // Stop EU.0044639
        "Post with Book No." := ServJobG."Post with Book No.";
      // Start EU.0152364.153023
        IF "Serv. Contract Type" <> ServJobG."Serv. Contract Type" THEN
          VALIDATE("Serv. Contract Type", ServJobG."Serv. Contract Type");
      // Stop EU.0152364.153023
        // Take over Resource No. from Job Line
        IF (Type <> Type::" ") AND ("Line No." <> 0) THEN
          SetResourceNo_ServJob();
      END ELSE BEGIN
        REPEAT
          InvNoL := SrvCustSplitMgmtG.GetInvNo(xRec);
          SrvCustSplitMgmtG.ReduceInvNo(ServHdrG,InvNoL,"Line No.");
        UNTIL InvNoL = 0;
      // Start PA043822
        IF NOT AvoidResetL THEN
          VALIDATE("Bill-to Customer No.",ServHdrG."Bill-to Customer No.");
        IF (Type <> Type::" ") AND NOT AvoidResetL THEN
      // Stop PA043822
          VALIDATE(Quantity);
      END;
      // Set Option and Service Posting Group
      "Option Code" := '';
      "Service Posting Group" := ServHdrG."Service Posting Group";
      IF "Service Job No." <> 0 THEN
      // Start EU.0052165
        IF GetServiceJob() THEN BEGIN
      // Stop EU.0052165
          "Service Posting Group" := ServJobG."Service Posting Group";
          IF Type <> Type::" " THEN
            "Option Code" := ServJobG."Option Code";
        END;
      IF "Document Type" = "Document Type"::Order THEN
        ServPostGroupGet(ServPostingGroupG,"Service Posting Group",TRUE)
      ELSE
        CLEAR(ServPostingGroupG);
      VALIDATE("Service Posting Group");
      // Start PA045431
      IF "Service Job No." <> 0 THEN
        IF "Sales Department Code" <> ServJobG."Sales Department Code" THEN
          VALIDATE("Sales Department Code", ServJobG."Sales Department Code");
      UpdatePostWithBookNo();
      // Stop PA045431
      UpdateOptionCode(Rec,xRec,FIELDNO("Service Job No."));
      UpdateAssocEntry(FIELDNO("Service Job No."));
      IF "Service Job No." <> 0 THEN
        SrvCustSplitMgmtG.SetInvNo(Rec);
      IF "Line No." <> 0 THEN BEGIN
        ServLineL.RESET;
        ServLineL.SETCURRENTKEY("Document Type","Document No.","Attached to Line No.");
        ServLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
        ServLineL.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
        ServLineL.SETRANGE("Attached to Line No.","Line No.");
        IF ServLineL.FINDSET(TRUE) THEN
          REPEAT
            ServLineL.VALIDATE("Service Job No.","Service Job No.");
            ServLineL.MODIFY(TRUE);
          UNTIL ServLineL.NEXT = 0;
      END;
      // Start EU.0215508.215566
      ServLineCustL.DoUpdateAmountInServiceLine(Rec, CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO(Quantity));
      // Stop EU.0215508.215566
      CALCFIELDS("No. of Bill-to Customers");
      // Stop PA042806
      // Start EU.0169755.170219
      IF CurrFieldNo <> FIELDNO("Service Job No.") THEN
      // Stop  EU.0169755.170219
      // Start EU.0104306
        RunOrderLineRounding(TransactionStartedHereL, xRec);
      // Stop EU.0104306
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetItemLocation@5806() : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      IF (ItemLocationGG."Location Code" = "Location Code") AND (ItemLocationGG."Item No." = "No.") THEN
        EXIT(TRUE);
      // Start PA032651
      EXIT(ItemLocationGG.GET("No.","Location Code"));
      // Stop PA032651
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetUnitCost@5808();
    BEGIN
      TESTFIELD(Type,Type::Item);
      TESTFIELD("No.");
      GetItem();
      "Qty. per Unit of Measure" := UnitOfMeasureMgtG.GetQtyPerUnitOfMeasure(ItemG,"Unit of Measure Code");
      // Start PA032651
      IF GetItemLocation() THEN
        VALIDATE("Unit Cost (LCY)", ItemLocationGG."Unit Cost" * "Qty. per Unit of Measure")
      // Stop PA032651
      ELSE
        VALIDATE("Unit Cost (LCY)",ItemG."Unit Cost" * "Qty. per Unit of Measure");
    END;

    PROCEDURE UpdatePostWithBookNo@1109400013();
    BEGIN
      // Start PA045431
      IF  Type IN [Type::" ",Type::"G/L Account"] THEN
        "Post with Book No." := FALSE
      ELSE BEGIN
        "Post with Book No." := "Value Increasing Measure";
        IF ServPostGroupGet(ServPostingGroupG, "Service Posting Group", FALSE) THEN
          IF CustG.IsInternalCustomer("Bill-to Customer No.") THEN
            "Post with Book No." := (ServPostingGroupG."Post with Book No." OR "Value Increasing Measure");
      END;
      // Stop PA045431
    END;

    PROCEDURE ServHeaderGet@1109400018(VAR ServLineP@1109400000 : Record 5025625);
    BEGIN
      ServLineP.TESTFIELD("Document No.");
      IF (ServLineP."Document Type" = ServHdrG."Document Type") AND
         (ServLineP."Document No." = ServHdrG."No.") AND
         (ServLineP."Document No." > '')
      THEN
        EXIT;
      ServHdrG.GET("Document Type","Document No.");
    END;

    PROCEDURE ServPostGroupGet@1109400017(VAR ServPostGroupP@1109400000 : Record 5025634;ServPostGroupCodeP@1109400001 : Code[10];CheckWithGetP@1109400002 : Boolean) : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      IF (ServPostGroupP.Code = ServPostGroupCodeP) AND (ServPostGroupCodeP > '') THEN
        EXIT(TRUE);
      IF NOT CheckWithGetP THEN
        EXIT(ServPostGroupP.GET(ServPostGroupCodeP));
      ServPostGroupP.GET(ServPostGroupCodeP);
      EXIT(TRUE);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE ServSetupGet@1109400020();
    BEGIN
      IF ServSetupReadG THEN
        EXIT;
      ServSetupG.GET;
      ServSetupReadG := TRUE;
    END;

    PROCEDURE DefaultOptionCodeGet@1109400019() : Code[20];
    BEGIN
      ServSetupGet();
      IF ServSetupG."Default Option Code" = '' THEN
        ERROR(C_INC048, ServSetupG.TABLECAPTION, ServSetupG.FIELDCAPTION("Default Option Code"));
      EXIT(ServSetupG."Default Option Code");
    END;

    PROCEDURE UpdateOptionCode@1109400016(VAR ServLineP@1109400002 : Record 5025625;VAR xServLineP@1109400001 : Record 5025625;FieldNoP@1109400000 : Integer);
    VAR
      UserServPostGroupL@1109400005 : Record 5028690;
      CustIsInternalL@1109400003 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      IF (FieldNoP <> CurrFieldNo) AND (CurrFieldNo <> 0) THEN
        EXIT;
      // Start PA032589
      CustIsInternalL := CustG.IsInternalCustomer(ServLineP."Bill-to Customer No.");
      // Stop PA032589
      IF NOT ServHdrG.ServPostingGroupGet(ServPostingGroupG,ServLineP."Service Posting Group") THEN
        CLEAR(ServPostingGroupG);

      ServLineP."Value Increasing Measure" := CustIsInternalL AND ServPostingGroupG."Value Increasing Measure";

      CASE FieldNoP OF
      // Start PA042806
        FIELDNO(Type):
      // Stop PA042806
          IF ServLineP.Type = xServLineP.Type THEN
            EXIT;
      // Start PA042806
        FIELDNO("No."):
      // Stop PA042806
          IF ServLineP."No." = xServLineP."No." THEN
            EXIT;
      // Start PA042806
        FIELDNO("Bill-to Customer No."):
      // Stop PA042806
          IF ServLineP."Bill-to Customer No." = xServLineP."Bill-to Customer No." THEN
            EXIT;
      // Start PA042806
        FIELDNO("Service Job No."):
      // Stop PA042806
          IF ServLineP."Service Job No." = xServLineP."Service Job No." THEN
            EXIT;
      // Start PA042806
        FIELDNO("Service Posting Group"):
      // Stop PA042806
          BEGIN
      // Start EU.0119070.119481
            ServLineP.ServLineCustInvValidation();
      // Stop EU.0119070.119481
            IF ServLineP."Document Type" = ServLineP."Document Type"::Order THEN
      // Start PA040142
              IF ServLineP."Option Code" > '' THEN
                ServLineP.TESTFIELD("Service Posting Group");
      // Stop PA040142
      // Start PA042806
            IF CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO("Service Posting Group") THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA042806
              // When a line is assigned to a job, then it is not possible to change the Service Posting Group in the line.
              IF (ServLineP."Service Posting Group" <> xServLineP."Service Posting Group") AND
                 (ServLineP."Service Job No." <> 0)
              THEN
      // Start EU.0052165
                ERROR(C_INC_FieldChangeCanBeDoneInTheJobOnly,
                  TABLECAPTION,
                  STRSUBSTNO('%1 %2',Type, "No."),
                  FIELDCAPTION("Service Job No."),
                  "Service Job No.",
                  FIELDCAPTION("Service Posting Group"));
      // Stop EU.0052165

              UserServPostGroupL.ServPostGroupIsValid(ServLineP."Service Posting Group");
            END;

            // Check if Service Option is not already posted.
      // Start PA042806
            CheckServOptionStatus(ServLineP,CurrFieldNo,FIELDNO("Service Posting Group"));
      // Stop PA042806

            IF ServLineP."Service Posting Group" > '' THEN BEGIN
              ServHeaderGet(ServLineP);
              ServPostGroupGet(ServPostingGroupG,ServLineP."Service Posting Group",TRUE);
      // Start PA034249
              ServPostingGroupG.ServiceVehStatusCheck("Document Type", ServHdrG.VIN, "Service Posting Group","Document No.");
      // Stop PA034249
            END;

            IF ServLineP."Service Posting Group" = xServLineP."Service Posting Group" THEN
              EXIT;
          END;
      // Start PA042806
        FIELDNO("Option Code"):
      // Stop PA042806
          BEGIN
            IF ServLineP."Option Code" = xServLineP."Option Code" THEN
              EXIT;

            IF ServLineP.Type = ServLineP.Type::" " THEN
      // Start EU.0129713.131032
              IF (CurrFieldNo <> 0) AND (ServLineP."Option Code" > '') THEN
      // Stop EU.0129713.131032
                ERROR(C_INC058,ServLineP.FIELDCAPTION("Option Code"),ServLineP.FIELDCAPTION(Type),ServLineP.Type);
            // If the service line is assigned to a job is should be not allowed to change the "Option code" in the line.
            IF CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO("Option Code") THEN
              IF (ServLineP."Service Job No." <> 0) AND (ServLineP.Type <> ServLineP.Type::" ") THEN
      // Start EU.0052165
                ERROR(C_INC_FieldChangeCanBeDoneInTheJobOnly,
                  TABLECAPTION,
                  STRSUBSTNO('%1 %2',Type, "No."),
                  FIELDCAPTION("Service Job No."),
                  "Service Job No.",
                  FIELDCAPTION("Option Code"));
      // Stop EU.0052165

            // If the "Option code" was set to "blank", then it must be checked that the "Service Posting Group"
            // is no "Value Increasing Measure".
            IF (ServLineP."Option Code" = '') AND ServLineP."Value Increasing Measure" THEN
              ERROR(C_INC048,ServLineP.TABLECAPTION,ServLineP.FIELDCAPTION("Option Code"));
          END;
        ELSE
          EXIT;
      END;

      CASE ServLineP.Type OF
        ServLineP.Type::" ":
          BEGIN
            ServLineP.VALIDATE("Option Code",'');
            ServLineP.VALIDATE("Post with Book No.",FALSE);
            EXIT;
          END;
      END;

      IF ServLineP."Value Increasing Measure" <> xServLineP."Value Increasing Measure" THEN
        ServLineP.VALIDATE("Value Increasing Measure");

      IF ServLineP."Service Job No." <> 0 THEN
      // Start EU.0052165
        ServJobG.GET(ServLineP."Document Type", ServLineP."Document No.", ServLineP."Service Job No.")
      // Stop EU.0052165
      ELSE
        ServHeaderGet(ServLineP);

      IF ServLineP."Value Increasing Measure" THEN BEGIN
      // Start PA045431
        IF FieldNoP <> FIELDNO("Option Code") THEN
          IF ServLineP."Service Job No." <> 0 THEN
            ServLineP.VALIDATE("Option Code", ServJobG."Option Code")
          ELSE
            IF ServHdrG."Option Code" = '' THEN
              ServLineP.VALIDATE("Option Code", DefaultOptionCodeGet)
            ELSE
              ServLineP.VALIDATE("Option Code", ServHdrG."Option Code");
      END ELSE BEGIN
      // Start PA032651
      // Start PA042806
        IF (FieldNoP <> FIELDNO("Option Code")) OR (FieldNoP = CurrFieldNo) THEN
      // Stop PA042806
      // Stop PA032651
          ServLineP.VALIDATE("Option Code",'');
      END;
      UpdatePostWithBookNo();
      // Stop PA045431
    END;

    PROCEDURE OptionCodeOnLookup@1109400015(VAR TextP@1109400000 : Text[250]) : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      IF NOT ItemG.GET(TextP) THEN
        CLEAR(ItemG);

      GetServHeader;
      IF NOT VehicleG.GET(ServHdrG.VIN) THEN
        CLEAR(VehicleG);
      ItemG.RESET;
      ItemG.SETCURRENTKEY("Item Type","Make Code","No.");
      ItemG.SETRANGE("Item Type",ItemG."Item Type"::"Own Option");
      IF VehicleG."Make Code" > '' THEN
        ItemG.SETFILTER("Make Code",'%1|%2',VehicleG."Make Code",'');
      IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(PAGE::"Own Options List",ItemG) <> ACTION::LookupOK THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      TextP := ItemG."No.";
      EXIT(TRUE);
    END;

    PROCEDURE UpdateQtytoInv@1109400025();
    VAR
      ServOptionL@1109400000 : Record 5025656;
      QtyInvSaveL@1109400001 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      IF ServOptionL.GET("Document Type","Document No.","Service Job No.","Option Code") THEN
        IF ServOptionL.Post THEN BEGIN
          QtyInvSaveL := "Qty. to Invoice";
          InitQtyToInv;
          IF QtyInvSaveL <> "Qty. to Invoice" THEN
            VALIDATE("Qty. to Invoice");
        END ELSE
          IF "Qty. to Invoice" <> 0 THEN
            VALIDATE("Qty. to Invoice",0);
    END;

    PROCEDURE SkipCheckLock@1109400021(SkipCheckLockP@1109400000 : Boolean);
    BEGIN
      SkipCheckLockG := SkipCheckLockP;
    END;

    PROCEDURE ReduceInvNo@1109400023(InvNoP@1109400000 : Integer);
    VAR
      ServLineCustL@1109400001 : Record 5025639;
      CountL@1109400004 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      GetServHeader();
      ServLineCustL.RESET;
      ServLineCustL.SETCURRENTKEY("Document Type","Document No.","Document Line No.","Bill-to Customer No.");
      ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Document Type", ServHdrG."Document Type");
      ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Document No.", ServHdrG."No.");
      ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Invoice No.", InvNoP);
      CountL := ServLineCustL.COUNT;
      ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Document Line No.", "Line No.");
      IF CountL = ServLineCustL.COUNT THEN BEGIN
        ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Invoice No.");
        ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Document Line No.");
        IF ServLineCustL.FINDSET(TRUE) THEN
          REPEAT
            IF ServLineCustL."Invoice No." > InvNoP THEN BEGIN
              ServLineCustL."Invoice No." := ServLineCustL."Invoice No." - 1;
              ServLineCustL.MODIFY;
            END;
          UNTIL ServLineCustL.NEXT = 0;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetInvNo@1109400022(ServLineP@1109400000 : Record 5025625) InvNoR : Integer;

    END;

    PROCEDURE Divide@1109400032(NumeratorP@1109400000 : Decimal;DenominatorP@1109400001 : Decimal) : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      IF (NumeratorP = 0) OR (DenominatorP = 0) THEN
        EXIT(0);
      EXIT(NumeratorP / DenominatorP);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CheckServiceInvoiceExists@21055406();
    VAR
      ErrorTextL@21055400 : Text;
      ServiceLineCustL@21055401 : Record 5025639;
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0210554.211581
      IF NOT ISTEMPORARY THEN BEGIN
        TESTFIELD("Quantity Invoiced", 0);
        SalesLineG.RESET;
        SalesLineG.SETCURRENTKEY("Service Order No.");
        SalesLineG.SETRANGE("Document Type", SalesLineG."Document Type"::Invoice);
        SalesLineG.SETRANGE("Service Order No.", "Document No.");
        SalesLineG.SETRANGE("Service Order Line No.", "Line No.");
        IF SalesLineG.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
          IF NOT CustG.GET(SalesLineG."Sell-to Customer No.") THEN
            CustG.INIT;
          IF SalesLineG.COUNT = 1 THEN
      // Start EU.0215508.215623
            ERROR(C_INC_OneUnpostedServiceInvoiceExists, "Line No.", Type, "No.", Description, SalesLineG."Sell-to Customer No.", CustG.Name, SalesLineG."Document No.");
      // Stop EU.0215508.215623
          REPEAT
            IF NOT CustG.GET(SalesLineG."Sell-to Customer No.") THEN
              CustG.INIT;
            ErrorTextL := ErrorTextL + STRSUBSTNO(', %1 (%2, %3)', SalesLineG."Document No.", SalesLineG."Sell-to Customer No.", CustG.Name);
          UNTIL SalesLineG.NEXT = 0;
      // Start EU.0215508.215623
          ERROR(C_INC_ManyUnpostedServiceInvoicesExist, "Line No.", Type, "No.", Description, COPYSTR(ErrorTextL, 3));
      // Stop EU.0215508.215623
        END;
        ServiceLineCustL.RESET;
        ServiceLineCustL.SETRANGE("Document Type", "Document Type");
        ServiceLineCustL.SETRANGE("Document No.", "Document No.");
        ServiceLineCustL.SETRANGE("Document Line No.", "Line No.");
        ServiceLineCustL.SETFILTER("Quantity Invoiced", '>0');
        IF ServiceLineCustL.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
          IF NOT CustG.GET(ServiceLineCustL."Bill-to Customer No.") THEN
            CustG.INIT;
          IF ServiceLineCustL.COUNT = 1 THEN
      // Start EU.0215508.215623
            ERROR(C_INC_OnePostedServiceInvoiceExists, "Line No.", Type, "No.", Description, ServiceLineCustL."Bill-to Customer No.", CustG.Name);
      // Stop EU.0215508.215623
          REPEAT
            IF NOT CustG.GET(ServiceLineCustL."Bill-to Customer No.") THEN
              CustG.INIT;
            ErrorTextL := ErrorTextL + STRSUBSTNO(', %1, %2', ServiceLineCustL."Bill-to Customer No.", CustG.Name);
          UNTIL ServiceLineCustL.NEXT = 0;
      // Start EU.0215508.215623
          ERROR(C_INC_ManyPostedServiceInvoicesExist, "Line No.", Type, "No.", Description, COPYSTR(ErrorTextL, 3));
      // Stop EU.0215508.215623
        END;
      END;
      // Stop EU.0210554.211581
    END;

    PROCEDURE ServLineCustInvValidation@1000000005();
    VAR
      ServLineCustL@1001 : Record 5025639;
      InvoicedOverQtyL@1000 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      // @ Check if the line was fully or partially invoices. Check must include single line split customer invoices.
      // Start EU.0119070.119481
      IF Type <> Type::" " THEN BEGIN
      // Start EU.0128664.129214
        IF CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO(Quantity) THEN
          InvoicedOverQtyL := Quantity;
      // Start EU.0137593.138279
      // Start EU.0136500.136489
      // Stop EU.0136500.136489
      // Stop EU.0137593.138279
        ServLineCustL.RESET;
        ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Document Type", "Document Type");
        ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Document No.", "Document No.");
        ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Document Line No.", "Line No.");
      // Start EU.0137593.138279
      // Start EU.0136500.136489
        IF InvoicedOverQtyL < 0 THEN
          ServLineCustL.SETFILTER("Quantity Invoiced", '<%1', InvoicedOverQtyL)
        ELSE
          ServLineCustL.SETFILTER("Quantity Invoiced", '>%1', InvoicedOverQtyL);
      // Stop EU.0136500.136489
      // Stop EU.0137593.138279
        IF ServLineCustL.FINDFIRST THEN
          ERROR(C_INC_LineSplitInvocePosedAlready, "Line No.",
            STRSUBSTNO('%1 %2', ServLineCustL."Bill-to Customer No.", ServLineCustL."Bill-to Name"),
            STRSUBSTNO('%1=%2', ServLineCustL.FIELDCAPTION("Quantity Invoiced"), ServLineCustL."Quantity Invoiced"));
      // Stop EU.0128664.129214
      END;
      // Stop EU.0119070.119481
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalcItemAvailQty@1119432003(VAR InvAvailableQtyP@1119432001 : Decimal;VAR InvExpectedQtyP@1119432000 : Decimal) InvIsComplAvailableR : Boolean;
    VAR
      ServLineL@1119432002 : Record 5025625;
      SkipL@72000 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // @ The function should calculate the available quantity of an item depending of the given Location Code and
      // @ should return that the outstanding quantity of an item is completely available.
      // @ param InvAvailableQtyP : Available qty. of an item depending of date filter 0d to eternal and of curr. location.
      // @ param InvExpectedQtyP :  Expected qty. of an item depending of date filter 0d to eternal and of curr. location.
      // @ retval InvIsComplAvailableR : Returns yes if the available quantity is bigger than outstanding qty.
      // Start PA032450
      InvIsComplAvailableR := FALSE;
      InvAvailableQtyP := 0;
      InvExpectedQtyP := 0;
      IF Type <> Type::Item THEN
        EXIT;
      IF "No." = '' THEN
        EXIT;
      IF NOT ItemG.GET("No.") THEN
        EXIT;
      // Start PA033011.5989972
      IF ServLineL.GET("Document Type","Document No.","Line No.") THEN BEGIN
      // Start EU.0078549
        OnCalcItemAvailQtyEvent(Rec, xRec, SkipL);
        IF NOT SkipL THEN
      // Stop EU.0078549
          MODIFY;
        ServLineL := Rec;
      END ELSE
        ServLineL.INIT;
      // Stop PA033011.5989972
      ItemG.RESET;
      ItemG.SETFILTER("Date Filter",'..%1',12319999D);
      ItemG.SETRANGE("Location Filter","Location Code");
      ItemG.SETRANGE("Bin Filter","Bin Code");
      InvExpectedQtyP := AvailabilityMgtG.ExpectedQtyOnHand(ItemG,TRUE,TRUE,0,InvAvailableQtyP,12319999D);
      // Start PA033011.5989972
      // Stop PA033011.5989972
      InvIsComplAvailableR := InvAvailableQtyP + ServLineL."Outstanding Qty. (Base)" >= "Outstanding Qty. (Base)";
      // Stop PA032450
    END;

    PROCEDURE InitReqWorksheetName@1119432011();
    BEGIN
      // @ The function should initialize the field "Req. Worksheet Name" based on "Requisition Wksh. Name" from Service Header
      // Start PA032450
      IF (Type = Type::Item) AND ("No." > '') THEN
      // Start PA041510
      // Start EU.0000369
          IF ("Req. Worksheet Name" = '') OR (xRec."Location Code" <> "Location Code") OR
             (xRec."Data Make Code" <> "Data Make Code")
          THEN BEGIN
            GetServHeader();
            IF (ServHdrG."Requisition Wksh. Name" = '') OR (xRec."Location Code" <> "Location Code") OR
               (xRec."Data Make Code" <> "Data Make Code")
            THEN BEGIN
              VALIDATE("Req. Worksheet Name", ReqWorksheetFunctionsG.GetDefReqWorksheetName(
                ServHdrG."Req. Wksh. Template Name", "Location Code", '', "Data Make Code", FALSE));
      // Stop EU.0000369
            END ELSE BEGIN
              VALIDATE("Req. Worksheet Name", ServHdrG."Requisition Wksh. Name");
            END;
          END;
      // Stop PA041510
      // Stop PA032450
    END;

    PROCEDURE SelectReqWorksheetName@1119432001(VAR ReqWorksheetNameP@1119432001 : Text[30]) : Boolean;
    VAR
      ReqWorksheetNameL@1119432002 : Code[10];
    BEGIN
      // @ Here a filtered lookup for field "Req. Worksheet Name" is provided by calling a function in codeunit
      // @ "Req. Worksheet Functions".
      // @ param ReqWorksheetNameP : Contains the current or the selected new value of field "Req. Worksheet Name".
      // @ retval : Returns true if the user has selected a new value.
      // Start PA032450
      TESTFIELD(Type,Type::Item);
      ReqWorksheetNameL := ReqWorksheetNameP;

      // Start PA032651
      IF NOT ReqWorksheetFunctionsG.SelectReqWorksheetName(
      // Stop PA032651
         ReqWorksheetNameL,
         ServHdrG."Req. Wksh. Template Name",
         "Location Code",
      // Start EU.0000369
         "Data Make Code",
      // Stop EU.0000369
         "No.")
      THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      ReqWorksheetNameP := ReqWorksheetNameL;
      EXIT(TRUE);
      // Stop PA032450
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckNegativeStock@1119432002();
    VAR
      ReservationEntryL@1119432003 : Record 337;
      ItemJnlCheckLineL@1119432000 : Codeunit 21;
      ReservedQtyOnInvL@1119432001 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      // @ The function has to prepare some data to call the real function in codeunit 21.
      // Start PA032800
      IF CurrFieldNo <> FIELDNO("Qty. to Ship") THEN
        EXIT;
      IF (Type <> Type::Item) OR ("Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::Quote]) OR ("Qty. to Ship" = 0) THEN
        EXIT;
      IF "Reserved Qty. (Base)" <> 0 THEN
        ReservedQtyOnInvL := ReservMgtG.CalcReservQtyOnInventory(
          ReservationEntryL."For Type"::Service,
          "Document Type",
          "Document No.",
          "Line No.",
          '',
          "No.",
          "Location Code",
          "Bin Code");
      IF ItemJnlCheckLineL.CheckNegItemStockAllowed(
         "No.",
         "Location Code",
         "Bin Code",
         USERID,
         "Qty. to Ship (Base)",
         ReservedQtyOnInvL,
         GETPOSITION(TRUE))
      THEN
        EXIT;
      "Qty. to Ship" := xRec."Qty. to Ship";
      // Stop PA032800
    END;

    PROCEDURE UpdateExtServLedgerEntry@1115000001();
    VAR
      ServLedgEntryL@1115000000 : Record 5025620;
    BEGIN
      // @ Update fields "Total Price" and "Unit Price" in table Service Ledger Entry
      // Start PA033019.8918595
      GetServHeader();
      // Stop PA033019.8918595
      ServLedgEntryL.RESET;
      ServLedgEntryL.SETCURRENTKEY("Order No.","Order Line No.","Entry Type");
      ServLedgEntryL.SETRANGE("Order No.","Document No.");
      ServLedgEntryL.SETRANGE("Order Line No.","Line No.");
      ServLedgEntryL.SETRANGE("Entry Type",ServLedgEntryL."Entry Type"::Usage);
      ServLedgEntryL.SETRANGE(Type,ServLedgEntryL.Type::"Ext. Service");
      IF ServLedgEntryL.FINDSET(TRUE) THEN
        REPEAT
          ServLedgEntryL."Unit Price" := "Unit Price";
          ServLedgEntryL."Total Price" := ROUND("Unit Price" * ServLedgEntryL.Quantity);
      // Start PA033019.8918595
          IF ServHdrG."Currency Code" > '' THEN BEGIN
            ServLedgEntryL."Total Price" := "Unit Price" * ServLedgEntryL.Quantity;
            ServLedgEntryL."Total Price" := CurrencyExchRateG.ExchangeAmtFCYToLCY(
              TODAY,
              ServHdrG."Currency Code",
              ServLedgEntryL."Total Price",
              ServHdrG."Currency Factor");
            ServLedgEntryL."Total Price" := ROUND(ServLedgEntryL."Total Price");
            ServLedgEntryL."Unit Price" := ROUND((ServLedgEntryL."Total Price" / Quantity),0.00001);
          END;
      // Stop PA033019.8918595
          ServLedgEntryL.MODIFY;
        UNTIL ServLedgEntryL.NEXT = 0;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckReplacement1toN@1100409000() : Boolean;
    VAR
      CurrentItemReplacementsL@1100409000 : Record 5028701;
    BEGIN
      // @ checks if for this added Item No. an 1 to N Replacement was stored into Current Item Replacements Table.
      // Start PA033958
      CurrentItemReplacementsL.RESET;
      CurrentItemReplacementsL.SETRANGE("Old Item No.","No.");
      CurrentItemReplacementsL.SETRANGE("1:N Replacement",TRUE);

    PROCEDURE Fill1toNReplIntoServiceLines@1100409002() : Code[20];
    VAR
      CurrentItemReplacementsL@1100409000 : Record 5028701;
      ServiceLineL@1100409001 : Record 5025625;
      NewLineNoL@1100409002 : Integer;
      ReplacedItemNoL@1100409003 : Code[20];
      RetItemNoL@1100409004 : Code[20];
    BEGIN
      // @ Fill 1 to N Repl Into Service Lines
      // Start PA033958
      CurrentItemReplacementsL.RESET;
      CurrentItemReplacementsL.SETRANGE("Old Item No.","No.");
      CurrentItemReplacementsL.SETRANGE("1:N Replacement",TRUE);
      IF CurrentItemReplacementsL.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
        ReplacedItemNoL := "No.";
        "No." := CurrentItemReplacementsL."New Item No.";
        RetItemNoL := "No.";
        NewLineNoL := 0;
        CurrentItemReplacementsL.NEXT;
        REPEAT
          ServiceLineL.RESET;
          ServiceLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
          ServiceLineL.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
          IF ServiceLineL.FINDLAST THEN
            NewLineNoL := ServiceLineL."Line No." + 10000
          ELSE
            NewLineNoL := 10000;
          ServiceLineL.INIT;
          ServiceLineL := Rec;
          ServiceLineL."Line No." := NewLineNoL;
          ServiceLineL.VALIDATE("No.",CurrentItemReplacementsL."New Item No.");
          ServiceLineL.VALIDATE(Quantity,1);
          ServiceLineL.INSERT;
        UNTIL CurrentItemReplacementsL.NEXT = 0;
        CurrentItemReplacementsL.RESET;
        CurrentItemReplacementsL.SETRANGE("Old Item No.",ReplacedItemNoL);
        CurrentItemReplacementsL.SETRANGE("1:N Replacement",TRUE);
        IF NOT CurrentItemReplacementsL.ISEMPTY THEN
          CurrentItemReplacementsL.DELETEALL;
      END ELSE
        RetItemNoL := "No.";
      EXIT(RetItemNoL);
      // Stop PA033958
    END;

    PROCEDURE AdditionalItemQtyConfirmation@1101368192() : Boolean;

    PROCEDURE UpdateSplittCalculation@1101175189();
    BEGIN
      // @ Wrapper function to call the new UpdateLineSplittCalculation with FALSE
      // Start EU.0104306

      // Stop EU.0104306
    END;

    PROCEDURE UpdateLineSplittCalculation@99(CalledFromAmountRoundingP@1000 : Boolean);
    VAR
      ServLineCustL@1109400000 : Record 5025639;
      SkipLineDiscountL@1001 : Boolean;
      AmountRoundingCorrectionL@1002 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      // @ Updates the Service Line Customer records with the current record.
      // @ param CalledFromAmountRoundingP : When active then any detected Amount difference is added to the highest customer split line
      // @                                   which doese not have any own price calculation activated.
      // Start PA033983
      ServLineCustL.RESET;
      ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
      ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
      ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Document Line No.","Line No.");
      // Start EU.0104306
      SkipLineDiscountL := CalledFromAmountRoundingP;
      ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Consider Price Calculation", TRUE);
      IF SkipLineDiscountL THEN
        SkipLineDiscountL := NOT ServLineCustL.ISEMPTY;
      ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Consider Price Calculation", FALSE);
      // Stop EU.0104306
      IF ServLineCustL.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
      // Start EU.0104306
          ServLineCustL.UpdateServLineLineCustomersWithServLine(Rec, SkipLineDiscountL);
      // Stop EU.0104306
      // Start PA044791
          ServLineCustL.MODIFY;
      // Stop PA044791
        UNTIL ServLineCustL.NEXT = 0;
      // Stop PA033983
      // Start EU.0015329
      ServLineCustL.RESET;
      ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
      ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
      ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Document Line No.","Line No.");
      IF ServLineCustL.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        ServLineCustL.RoundingRestCorrectionAfterCustmerLineSplit(ServLineCustL);
        ServLineCustL.CALCSUMS(Amount);
        ServLineCustL.Amount := ROUND(ServLineCustL.Amount, CurrencyG."Amount Rounding Precision");
      // Start EU.0019677
      // Start EU.0104306
        IF Amount <> ServLineCustL.Amount THEN
          IF CalledFromAmountRoundingP THEN BEGIN
            AmountRoundingCorrectionL := Amount - ServLineCustL.Amount;
            ServLineCustL.RESET;
            ServLineCustL.SETCURRENTKEY(Amount);
            ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
            ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
            ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Document Line No.","Line No.");
            ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Consider Price Calculation", FALSE);
            ServLineCustL.FINDLAST;
            ServLineCustL.SETRANGE(Amount, ServLineCustL.Amount);
            IF ServLineCustL.COUNT > 1 THEN
              ServLineCustL.NEXT(- RANDOM(ServLineCustL.COUNT));
            ServLineCustL.Amount := ServLineCustL.Amount + AmountRoundingCorrectionL;
            ServLineCustL.MODIFY;
          END ELSE BEGIN
      // Stop EU.0104306
            GetServHeader();
            SrvCustSplitMgmtG.UpdServLineCust_ServLine(ServHdrG, Rec, FALSE, SkipSrvCustUpdateG, FALSE, FALSE);
          END;
      // Stop EU.0019677
      END;
      // Stop EU.0015329
    END;

    PROCEDURE SetDefaultResourceNo@1100769811();
    BEGIN
      // @ Function sets the Resource No. for a new Service Line - only if Split Type is 'Automatic'
      // @ Service Resource Assignment table will be updated

      // Start PA034057
      IF "Document Type" <> "Document Type"::Order THEN
        EXIT;

      GetServHeader();
      IF ServHdrG."Resource Time Split Type" = ServHdrG."Resource Time Split Type"::Manual THEN
        EXIT;
      // Start PA041187.87916
      // Stop PA041187.87916

      "Resource No." := GetDefaultResourceNo();
      IF "Resource No." = '' THEN
        EXIT;


      // Start PA036950
      IF UserSessionUnitG.TimeManLicensePermissionCheck(FALSE) AND ("Resource No." <> '') THEN BEGIN
        IF ServResourceMgntG.ManualAssExists4ServLine(Rec) THEN
          EXIT;

      // Update Service Resource Assignment
        ServResourceMgntG.CreateServResAssign_DocLine(
          "Document Type",
          "Document No.",
          "Line No.",
          "Resource No.",
          FALSE,
          FALSE);

      // Stop PA034057
      END;
      // Stop PA036950
      // Start PA042629
      VALIDATE("Resource No.");
      // Stop PA042629
    END;

    PROCEDURE SetResourceNo_ServJob@1100769812();
    BEGIN
      // @ Function takes over the Resource No. from Service Job to Service Line
      // @ Service Resource Assignment table will be updated

      // Start PA034057
      IF (Type = Type::" ") OR ("Line No." = 0) OR ("Service Job No." = 0) THEN
        EXIT;

      // Start PA034057.I002090
      GetServHeader();
      IF ServHdrG."Resource Time Split Type" = ServHdrG."Resource Time Split Type"::Manual THEN
        EXIT;
      // Stop PA034057.I002090

      // Stop EU.0052165
      IF NOT GetServiceJob() THEN
        EXIT;
      IF ServJobG."Assign. Resource No." = '' THEN
        EXIT;
      IF "Resource No." = ServJobG."Assign. Resource No." THEN
      // Stop EU.0052165
        EXIT;


      // Start PA036950
      // Start PA040415
      IF UserSessionUnitG.TimeManLicensePermissionCheck(FALSE) THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA040415
        IF ServResourceMgntG.ManualAssExists4ServLine(Rec) THEN
          EXIT;
        IF "Resource No." <> '' THEN
          IF CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO("Service Job No.") THEN
      // Start EU.0052165
            IF NOT CONFIRM(C_INC_ChangeResNoByJob,FALSE,"Resource No.",ServJobG."Assign. Resource No.") THEN
              EXIT;
      // Start PA040829
        VALIDATE("Resource No.", ServJobG."Assign. Resource No.");
      // Stop EU.0052165
      // Stop PA040829
        // Update Service Resource Assignment
        ServResourceMgntG.CreateServResAssign_DocLine(
          "Document Type",
          "Document No.",
          "Line No.",
          "Resource No.",
          FALSE,
          FALSE);
      // Stop PA034057
      END;
      // Stop PA036950
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetDefaultResourceNo@1100769813() ResourceNoR : Code[20];
    VAR
      TimeClockEntryL@1100769813 : Record 5208401;
      TimeClockEntry2L@1109400000 : Record 5208401;
      ServiceResAssignmentL@1109400001 : Record 5208431;
    BEGIN
      // @ Function searches the default Resource No for the current Service Line
      // @ Checks Service Job Line and Clocking Data
      // @ retval: Default Resource No (if found)

      // Start PA034057
      ResourceNoR := '';

      IF (Type = Type::" ") AND ("Line No." = 0) THEN
        EXIT;

      // Start PA041187.87916
      // Rule 8, Prio 1 - Manually assigned Resource No's shouldn't be changed
      // Start PA041187.89142
      IF "Resource No." <> '' THEN BEGIN
      // Start EU.0104306
        ServiceResAssignmentL.SETRANGE("Document Type", "Document Type");
      // Stop EU.0104306
        ServiceResAssignmentL.SETRANGE("Document No.", "Document No.");
        ServiceResAssignmentL.SETRANGE("Line No.", "Line No.");
        IF ServiceResAssignmentL.FINDFIRST AND ServiceResAssignmentL.Manual THEN
          EXIT("Resource No.");
      END;
      // Stop PA041187.89142

      // Start PA036950
      // Start PA040415
      IF UserSessionUnitG.TimeManLicensePermissionCheck(FALSE) AND (Type = Type::Labor) THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA040415
        TimeClockEntryL.RESET;
        TimeClockEntryL.SETCURRENTKEY("Service Order No.",Date,Time);
        TimeClockEntryL.SETRANGE("Service Order No.","Document No.");
        TimeClockEntryL.SETRANGE(Type, TimeClockEntryL.Type::"Begin");

        // Rule 6, Prio 3 - if clocking on service line no. exists,
        TimeClockEntryL.SETRANGE("Service Line No.", "Line No.");
        IF TimeClockEntryL.FINDLAST THEN
          EXIT(TimeClockEntryL."Resource No.");

        // Rule 5, Prio 4 / Rule 4, Prio 5 - If clocking on Job level exists. Open Clockings have Prio
        TimeClockEntryL.SETRANGE("Service Line No.");
        IF "Service Job No." <> 0 THEN BEGIN
          TimeClockEntryL.SETRANGE("Service Job No.", "Service Job No.");
          IF TimeClockEntryL.FINDLAST THEN BEGIN
            ResourceNoR := TimeClockEntryL."Resource No.";
            REPEAT
              TimeClockEntry2L.SETCURRENTKEY("Linked to Entry No.");
              TimeClockEntry2L.SETRANGE("Linked to Entry No.",TimeClockEntryL."Entry No.");
              IF TimeClockEntry2L.ISEMPTY THEN
                EXIT(TimeClockEntryL."Resource No.");
            UNTIL TimeClockEntryL.NEXT(-1) = 0;
            EXIT(ResourceNoR);
          END;
        END;

        // Rule 3, Prio 6 / Rule 2, Prio 7 - If clocking on Order level exists. Open clockings have Prio
        TimeClockEntryL.SETRANGE("Service Job No.");
        IF TimeClockEntryL.FINDLAST THEN BEGIN
          ResourceNoR := TimeClockEntryL."Resource No.";
          REPEAT
            TimeClockEntry2L.SETCURRENTKEY("Linked to Entry No.");
            TimeClockEntry2L.SETRANGE("Linked to Entry No.",TimeClockEntryL."Entry No.");
            IF TimeClockEntry2L.ISEMPTY THEN
              EXIT(TimeClockEntryL."Resource No.");
          UNTIL TimeClockEntryL.NEXT(-1) = 0;
          EXIT(ResourceNoR);
        END;
      END;

      // Rule 1, Prio 8 - Default Resource No. from Service Job Line
      // Start EU.0052165
      IF "Service Job No." <> 0 THEN
        IF GetServiceJob() THEN
          ResourceNoR := ServJobG."Assign. Resource No.";
      // Start EU.0052165
      // Stop PA041187.87916
    END;
