    PROCEDURE CreateDim@1109400034(TypeP@1109400005 : Integer;NoP@1109400004 : Code[20];MakeCodeP@1109400012 : Code[20];Type2P@1109400003 : Integer;No2P@1109400002 : Code[20];MakeCode2P@1109400010 : Code[20];Type3P@1109400007 : Integer;No3P@1109400008 : Code[20];MakeCode3P@1109400011 : Code[20]);
    VAR
      SourceCodeSetupL@1109400006 : Record 242;
      TableIDL@1109400001 : ARRAY [10] OF Integer;
      NoL@1109400000 : ARRAY [10] OF Code[20];
      MakeCodeL@1109400009 : ARRAY [10] OF Code[20];
    BEGIN
      // @ param TypeP - of type Integer
      // @ param NoP - of type Code length 20
      // @ param MakeCodeP of type Code length 20 - relevant only for Labor.
      // @ param Type2P - of type Integer
      // @ param No2P - of type Code length 20
      // @ param MakeCode2P of type Code length 20 - relevant only for Labor.
      // @ param Type3P - of type Integer
      // @ param No3P - of type Code length 20
      // @ param MakeCode3P of type Code length 20 - relevant only for Labor.

      // Start PA036002.26542
      SourceCodeSetupL.GET;
      TableIDL[1] := TypeP;
      NoL[1] := NoP;
      // Start PA036002.27221
      MakeCodeL[1] := MakeCodeP;
      // Stop PA036002.27221
      TableIDL[2] := Type2P;
      NoL[2] := No2P;
      // Start PA036002.27221
      MakeCodeL[2] := MakeCode2P;
      // Stop PA036002.27221
      // Start PA036002.26594
      // Start PA036002.27288
      GetServHeader;
      IF (ServHdrG."Bill-to Customer No." <> "Bill-to Customer No.") THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA036002.27288
        TableIDL[3] := Type3P;
        NoL[3] := No3P;
      // Stop PA036002.26594
      // Start PA036002.27221
        MakeCodeL[3] := MakeCode3P;
      // Stop PA036002.27221
      // Start PA036002.27288
      END;
      // Stop PA036002.27288
      // Start PA036002.26254
      DimMgtG.SetLineParam(DimMgtG.TypeToTableIDMyEngine3(Type),TRUE);
      // Stop PA036002.26254
      // Start PA036002.27153
      "Dimension Set ID" := DimMgtG.GetDefaultDimID(TableIDL,NoL,MakeCodeL,SourceCodeSetupL.Service,"Department Code","Make Code",ServHdrG."Dimension Set ID",DATABASE::Customer);
      // Stop PA036002.27153
      DimMgtG.UpdateGlobalDimFromDimSetID("Dimension Set ID","Department Code","Make Code");
      // Stop PA036002.26542
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE UpdateAppointmentDataInServiceLines@11776600(UpdateFieldNoP@11776600 : Integer);
    VAR
      RecL@11776601 : Record 5025625;
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0117766
      IF "Vehicle Appointment Code" = '' THEN
        EXIT;
      IF CurrFieldNo = 0 THEN
        EXIT;
      GetServHeader();
      IF "Line No." <> 0 THEN BEGIN
        RecL.SETRANGE("Document Type", "Document Type");
        RecL.SETRANGE("Document No.", "Document No.");
        RecL.SETFILTER("Line No.", '<>%1', "Line No.");
        RecL.SETRANGE(Type, Type);
        RecL.SETRANGE("Vehicle Appointment Code", "Vehicle Appointment Code");
        CASE UpdateFieldNoP OF
          FIELDNO("Next Appointment on"):
            BEGIN
              RecL.SETFILTER("Next Appointment on", '<>%1', "Next Appointment on");
              IF NOT RecL.ISEMPTY THEN
                RecL.MODIFYALL("Next Appointment on", "Next Appointment on");
            END;
          FIELDNO("Next Appointment at Mileage"):
            BEGIN
              RecL.SETFILTER("Next Appointment at Mileage", '<>%1', "Next Appointment at Mileage");
              IF NOT RecL.ISEMPTY THEN
                RecL.MODIFYALL("Next Appointment at Mileage", "Next Appointment at Mileage");
            END;
          FIELDNO("Next Appoint. at Running Time"):
            BEGIN
              RecL.SETFILTER("Next Appoint. at Running Time", '<>%1', "Next Appoint. at Running Time");
              IF NOT RecL.ISEMPTY THEN
                RecL.MODIFYALL("Next Appoint. at Running Time", "Next Appoint. at Running Time");
            END;
        END;
      END;
      // Stop EU.0117766
    END;

    PROCEDURE SetAppointmentLine@1101422632(VAR RecP@11776600 : Record 5025625;ExRecP@11776601 : Record 5025625;ActionP@1101422631 : 'Insert,Delete,Modify');
    VAR
      ServLineL@1101422630 : Record 5025625;
    BEGIN
      // @ function to check if record is default line
      // Start PA036188
      // Start EU.0117766
      IF NOT (RecP.Type IN [ServLineL.Type::Labor, ServLineL.Type::"Ext. Service"]) THEN
        EXIT;
      IF ActionP = ActionP::Modify THEN
        IF "Vehicle Appointment Code" <> ExRecP."Vehicle Appointment Code" THEN
          IF ExRecP."Vehicle Appointment Code" > '' THEN
            SetAppointmentLine(ExRecP, ExRecP, ActionG::Delete);
      ServLineL.RESET;
      ServLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type", RecP."Document Type");
      ServLineL.SETRANGE("Document No.", RecP."Document No.");
      ServLineL.SETFILTER("Line No.", '<>%1', RecP."Line No.");
      ServLineL.SETRANGE(Type, RecP.Type);
      ServLineL.SETRANGE("Vehicle Appointment Code", RecP."Vehicle Appointment Code");
      CASE ActionP OF
        ActionP::Insert, ActionP::Modify:
          RecP."Appointment Line" := ServLineL.ISEMPTY;
        ActionP::Delete:
          IF RecP."Appointment Line" THEN
            IF ServLineL.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
              ServLineL."Appointment Line" := TRUE;
              ServLineL.MODIFY;
            END;
      // Stop EU.0117766
      END;
      // Stop PA036188
    END;

    PROCEDURE UpdateVehicleAppointment@1101422630();
    VAR
      VehApptL@1101422631 : Record 5025450;
      VehAppTypeL@1101422630 : Record 5025449;
    BEGIN
      // @ function to create/Update Vehicle Appointment
      // Start EU.0117766
      IF "Appointment Line" THEN
      // Stop EU.0117766
      // Start PA036188
        IF ("Vehicle Appointment Code" > '') AND ((Type = Type::Labor) OR (Type = Type::"Ext. Service")) THEN BEGIN
          IF ("Next Appointment on" <> 0D) OR ("Next Appointment at Mileage" <> 0) OR ("Next Appoint. at Running Time" <> 0) THEN BEGIN
            IF "Quantity Shipped" <> 0 THEN BEGIN
              ServHdrG.GET("Document Type","Document No.");
      // Start EU.0117766
      // Start PA036188.31748
              IF VehAppTypeL.GET("Vehicle Appointment Code") THEN BEGIN
                VehAppTypeL.TESTFIELD(Type, VehAppTypeL.Type::Recurring);
                VehApptL.RESET;
                VehApptL.SETRANGE(VIN, ServHdrG.VIN);
                VehApptL.SETRANGE("Appointment Type", "Vehicle Appointment Code");
      // Start EU.0126935.127403
      // Start EU.0191766
                IF GetServiceJob() AND (ServJobG."Appointment Line No." <> 0) THEN BEGIN
      // Stop EU.0126935.127403
                  VehApptL.SETRANGE("Document Type", "Document Type");
                  VehApptL.SETRANGE("Document No.", "Document No.");
                  VehApptL.SETRANGE("Line No.", ServJobG."Appointment Line No.");
                END;
                VehApptL.SETFILTER(Status, '<>%1', VehApptL.Status::Cancelled);
                IF NOT VehApptL.FINDFIRST THEN
      // Start EU.0191766
                  VehApptL.CreateApptFromServHdr(ServHdrG, VehApptL.Status::Recurring, VehAppTypeL, "Next Appointment on");
      // Stop EU.0191766
                IF "Service Job No." > 0 THEN
                  VehApptL."Job Cart No." := ShoppingCartMgtG.CreateNewAppointmentShoppingCartHdr(ServJobG, ServJobG."Bill-to Customer No.", ServHdrG.VIN, FALSE);
      // Stop EU.0117766
      // Start EU.0135165.135425
                VehApptL."Document Type" := "Document Type";
                VehApptL."Document No." := "Document No.";
      // Stop EU.0191766
      // Stop EU.0135165.135425
                VehApptL."Next Appointment Date" := "Next Appointment on";
                VehApptL."Next Appointment at Mileage" := "Next Appointment at Mileage";
                VehApptL."Next Appoint. at Running Time" := "Next Appoint. at Running Time";
      // Start EU.0117766
                VehApptL.MODIFY(TRUE);
      // Stop EU.0117766
              END;
      // Stop PA036188.31748
            END;
          END;
        END;
      // Stop PA036188
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckForLineDuplicates@1109400035();
    VAR
      ServLineL@1109400000 : Record 5025625;
      AdditionalItemL@1109400005 : Record 5028716;
      AddItemDuplicateWarningBufferL@1055602 : Text;
      CounterL@1055600 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      // @ Function checks for duplicated lines on documents with type Order.
      // Start PA037942
      UserSetupGet;
      CASE UserSetupG."Check For Lines Duplicate No." OF
        UserSetupG."Check For Lines Duplicate No."::" ":
          EXIT;
        UserSetupG."Check For Lines Duplicate No."::Warning,
        UserSetupG."Check For Lines Duplicate No."::Error:
          BEGIN
            ServLineL.RESET;
            ServLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
            ServLineL.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
            ServLineL.SETFILTER("Line No.",'<>%1',"Line No.");
            ServLineL.SETRANGE(Type,Type);
            ServLineL.SETRANGE("No.","No.");
            IF NOT ServLineL.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
      // Start PA044975
              IF UserSetupG."Check For Lines Duplicate No." = UserSetupG."Check For Lines Duplicate No."::Error THEN
                ERROR(C_INC_DuplicateError, Type, "No.");
              IF NOT CONFIRM(C_INC_DuplicateWarning, FALSE, Type, "No.") THEN
                ERROR('');
            END;
      // Start EU.0123449.123868
      // Start PA037942.48468
            IF Type = Type::Item THEN BEGIN
      // Stop EU.0123449.123868
              AdditionalItemL.RESET;
              AdditionalItemL.SETRANGE("Additional Item No.","No.");
              AdditionalItemL.SETRANGE("Consider in Service Sales", TRUE);
      // Start EU.0053218
              IF AdditionalItemL.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
                IF UserSetupG."Check For Lines Duplicate No." = UserSetupG."Check For Lines Duplicate No."::Error THEN
                  ERROR(C_INC_DuplicateErrorAddItem, Type, "No.");
                REPEAT
                  CounterL += 1;
                  AdditionalItemL.CALCFIELDS("Item Description");
                  AddItemDuplicateWarningBufferL := AddItemDuplicateWarningBufferL + '\' +
                    STRSUBSTNO('%1. %2 %3', CounterL, AdditionalItemL."Item No.", AdditionalItemL."Item Description");
                UNTIL AdditionalItemL.NEXT = 0;
                IF NOT CONFIRM(STRSUBSTNO(C_INC_DuplicateWarningAddItem, Type, "No.", AddItemDuplicateWarningBufferL,'\\'),FALSE) THEN
                  ERROR('');
              END;
      // Start EU.0123449.123868
            END;
      // Stop EU.0053218
      // Stop PA044975
      // Stop PA037942.48468
      // Stop EU.0123449.123868
          END;
      END;
      // Stop PA037942
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE AvoidResetLineValues@1109400043() AvoidResetR : Boolean;
    VAR
      ServCustSplitUpL@21055400 : Record 5045370;
    BEGIN
      // @ This is a support function to check some conditions to skip the update of line figures in case of "Service Job No." update
      // @ This function is used by ServiceJobNoOnValidate() and "Service Job No." OnValidate trigger
      // @ retval Boolean TRUE the conditions are fulfilled and line figures should be skipped, FALSE otherwise

      // Start EU.0082249
      IF SkipResetLineValuesG THEN
        EXIT(TRUE);
      // Stop EU.0082249
      // Start EU.0169755.170219
      CALCFIELDS("No. of Bill-to Customers");
      // When there are several splits then reset the values
      IF "No. of Bill-to Customers" <> 1 THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      // Stop EU.0169755.170219
      // Start PA043822
      // Start EU.0095702.100876
      // Start EU.0161230.160507
      // When there is a package then keep the discounts only in case it is a fixed price package. If not the Job change should force fresh values
      IF "Package No." > '' THEN
        IF ServPkgLineG.GET("Document Type", "Document No.", "Package No.", "Package Version No.") THEN
          IF ServPkgLineG."Unit Price" <> 0 THEN
            EXIT(TRUE);
      // Stop EU.0095702.100876
      // Start EU.0169755.170219
      // Stop EU.0169755.170219
      // Start EU.0210554.171367
      IF ("Service Job No." <> 0) AND GetServiceJob() THEN BEGIN
        AvoidResetR := "Bill-to Customer No." = ServJobG."Bill-to Customer No.";
        IF AvoidResetR THEN BEGIN
          ServCustSplitUpL.SETRANGE("Document Type", "Document Type");
          ServCustSplitUpL.SETRANGE("Document No.", "Document No.");
          ServCustSplitUpL.SETRANGE("Service Job No.", "Service Job No.");
          ServCustSplitUpL.SETFILTER("Bill-to Customer No.", '<>%1', ServJobG."Bill-to Customer No.");
          AvoidResetR := ServCustSplitUpL.ISEMPTY;
        END;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        GetServHeader();
        AvoidResetR := "Bill-to Customer No." = ServHdrG."Bill-to Customer No.";
      END;
      // Start EU.0203951.208158
      // Stop EU.0203951.208158
      // Stop EU.0161230.160507
      // Stop PA043822
      OnPostAvoidResetLineValuesEvent(Rec, ServJobG, AvoidResetR);
      // Stop EU.0210554.171367
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalculateReserveQtyOnStock@36900(VAR FirstReservationDateP@1737400 : Date) QuantityR : Decimal;
    VAR
      ResEntryL@36902 : Record 337;
      ReservMgtL@36901 : Codeunit 99000845;
    BEGIN
      // @ This is a support function to calculate the sum of Quantity on Reservation Entries from stock (From Type = Item Ledger Entry) linked to the line
      // @ param FirstReservationDateP : "Creation Date" of the first reservation related to the line
      // @ retval : Decimal with the calculated Quantity
      // Start EU.0000369
      // Start EU.0017374
      FirstReservationDateP := 0D;
      // Stop EU.0017374
      IF "Reserved Quantity" = 0 THEN
        EXIT(0);
      ReservMgtL.InitFilterAndSortingLookupFor(ResEntryL, TRUE);
      ReservMgtL.ServFilterReservFor(ResEntryL, Rec);
      // Start EU.0017374
      // Note "From Type" is empty in case of reservation on no inventory tracking item
      ResEntryL.SETFILTER("From Type", '%1|%2', ResEntryL."From Type"::" ", ResEntryL."From Type"::"Item Ledger Entry");
      ResEntryL.CALCSUMS(Quantity);
      QuantityR := ResEntryL.Quantity;
      IF QuantityR > 0 THEN
        IF ResEntryL.FINDFIRST THEN
          FirstReservationDateP := ResEntryL."Creation Date";
      // Stop EU.0017374
      // Stop EU.0000369
    END;

    PROCEDURE CreateTempReplChain@1055604(ItemNoP@1055600 : Code[20];ChainNoP@1055601 : Integer);
    BEGIN
      // @ This function creates records in a temporary Replacement Chain Record to display replacements
      // @ that have not yet been completed.
      // @ param ItemNoP - Code 20
      // @ param ChainNoP - Integer

      // Start PA044817
      ReplcmtChainTempG.INIT;
      ReplcmtChainTempG."Item No." := ItemNoP;
      ReplcmtChainTempG."Chain No." := ChainNoP;
      IF ReplcmtChainTempG.INSERT THEN
        ;
      // Stop PA044817
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckItemReplcmnt@1055608();
    VAR
      CurrItemReplL@1055600 : Record 5028701;
      CurrItemRepl2L@1055603 : Record 5028701;
      ReplChainL@1055601 : Record 5028707;
      ReplChain2L@1055602 : Record 5028707;
    BEGIN
      // @ This function searches, according to Item Replacement Status, for uncomplete replacements in
      // @ Current Item Replacement table.

      // Start PA044817
      IF ItemG."Replacement Status" = ItemG."Replacement Status"::"Will be replaced" THEN BEGIN
        CurrItemReplL.RESET;
        CurrItemReplL.SETRANGE("Old Item No.", "No.");
        IF CurrItemReplL.FINDSET THEN
          // Handle N to 1 future replacements
          IF CurrItemReplL."N:1 Replacement" THEN BEGIN
            // Found the first of the line
            IF CurrItemReplL."Attached to Replacement No." = 0 THEN BEGIN
              CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemReplL."Old Item No.",1);
              CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemReplL."New Item No.",1);
              // Search for the attached
              CurrItemRepl2L.RESET;
              CurrItemRepl2L.SETCURRENTKEY("Attached to Replacement No.");
              CurrItemRepl2L.SETRANGE("Attached to Replacement No.", CurrItemReplL."Replacement No.");
              IF CurrItemRepl2L.FINDSET THEN
                REPEAT
                  CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemRepl2L."Old Item No.",1);
                UNTIL CurrItemRepl2L.NEXT = 0;
            END ELSE BEGIN
              // Found an attached replacement, so find the first in line
              CurrItemRepl2L.RESET;
              CurrItemRepl2L.SETRANGE("Replacement No.", CurrItemReplL."Attached to Replacement No.");
              IF CurrItemRepl2L.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemRepl2L."Old Item No.",1);
                CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemRepl2L."New Item No.",1);
              END;
              // Search for the attached
              CurrItemRepl2L.RESET;
              CurrItemRepl2L.SETRANGE("Attached to Replacement No.", CurrItemReplL."Attached to Replacement No.");
              IF CurrItemRepl2L.FINDSET THEN
                REPEAT
                  CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemRepl2L."Old Item No.",1);
                UNTIL CurrItemRepl2L.NEXT = 0;
            END;

          END ELSE BEGIN
            // This may handle both 1:1 or 1:N current replacements
            REPEAT
              CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemReplL."Old Item No.",1);
              CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemReplL."New Item No.",1);
            UNTIL CurrItemReplL.NEXT = 0;
          END;
      END ELSE
        IF ItemG."Replacement Status" = ItemG."Replacement Status"::"Replacement Item" THEN BEGIN
          CurrItemReplL.RESET;
          CurrItemReplL.SETRANGE("New Item No.", "No.");
          IF CurrItemReplL.FINDSET THEN
            // Handle 1 to N future replacements
            IF CurrItemReplL."1:N Replacement" THEN BEGIN
              // Found the first of the line
              IF CurrItemReplL."Attached to Replacement No." = 0 THEN BEGIN
                CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemReplL."Old Item No.",1);
                CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemReplL."New Item No.",1);
                // Search for the attached
                CurrItemRepl2L.RESET;
                CurrItemRepl2L.SETCURRENTKEY("Attached to Replacement No.");
                CurrItemRepl2L.SETRANGE("Attached to Replacement No.", CurrItemReplL."Replacement No.");
                IF CurrItemRepl2L.FINDSET THEN
                  REPEAT
                    CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemRepl2L."New Item No.",1);
                  UNTIL CurrItemRepl2L.NEXT = 0;
              END ELSE BEGIN
                // Found an attached replacement, so find the first in line
                CurrItemRepl2L.RESET;
                CurrItemRepl2L.SETRANGE("Replacement No.", CurrItemReplL."Attached to Replacement No.");
                IF CurrItemRepl2L.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                  CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemRepl2L."Old Item No.",1);
                  CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemRepl2L."New Item No.",1);
                END;
                // Search for the attached
                CurrItemRepl2L.RESET;
                CurrItemRepl2L.SETRANGE("Attached to Replacement No.", CurrItemReplL."Attached to Replacement No.");
                IF CurrItemRepl2L.FINDSET THEN
                  REPEAT
                    CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemRepl2L."New Item No.",1);
                  UNTIL CurrItemRepl2L.NEXT = 0;
              END;
            END ELSE BEGIN
              // This may handle both 1:1 or N:1 current replacements
              REPEAT
                CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemReplL."Old Item No.",1);
                CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemReplL."New Item No.",1);
              UNTIL CurrItemReplL.NEXT = 0;
            END;
        END;
      // Stop PA044817
    END;

    PROCEDURE SetCurrFieldNo@1109400046(CurrFieldNoP@1109400000 : Integer);
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0024419
      CurrFieldNo := CurrFieldNoP;
      // Stop EU.0024419
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE ConfirmItemReplacement@4729400();
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0047294
      IF NOT WithoutReplcmtWindowG THEN
        IF ItemG.GET("No.") THEN
          CASE ItemG."Replacement Status" OF
            ItemG."Replacement Status"::"Has been replaced":
              ShowReplcmtG := CONFIRM(C_INC020, TRUE, ItemG.TABLECAPTION, "No.");
            ItemG."Replacement Status"::"Replacement Item":
              ShowReplcmtG := CONFIRM(C_INC024, TRUE, ItemG.TABLECAPTION, "No.");
            ItemG."Replacement Status"::"Will be replaced":
              BEGIN
                ShowReplcmtG := CONFIRM(C_INC027, TRUE, ItemG.TABLECAPTION, "No.");
                FutureReplG := TRUE;
              END;
          END;
      // Stop EU.0047294
    END;

    PROCEDURE CanModifyCustSplit@72002(CustNoP@72000 : Code[20]) : Boolean;
    VAR
      ServLineCustL@72001 : Record 5025639;
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0051613
      ServLineCustL.RESET;
      ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Document Type", "Document Type");
      ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Document No.", "Document No.");
      ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Document Line No.", "Line No.");
      ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Bill-to Customer No.", CustNoP);
      IF NOT ServLineCustL.ISEMPTY THEN
        EXIT(TRUE);

      ServLineCustL.SETRANGE("Bill-to Customer No.");
      EXIT(ServLineCustL.COUNT = 1);
      // Stop EU.0051613
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CheckReValidateItemNoField@11(DirectAssignP@1001 : Boolean;VAR ReplcmtChainP@1000 : Record 5028707) : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0114873.116335
      // Start EU.0121768.123540
      IF (NOT DirectAssignP) THEN BEGIN
      // Stop EU.0121768.123540
        ConfirmItemReplacement();
        IF NOT ShowReplcmtG THEN
          EXIT(FALSE);
      // Start EU.0122714.123771
        COMMIT;
      // Stop EU.0122714.123771
        IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(PAGE::"Replacement Item by Location", ReplcmtChainP) <> ACTION::LookupOK THEN
          EXIT(FALSE);
      END;
      IF "No." = ReplcmtChainP."Item No." THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      // Start EU.0120358.121710
      IF ReplcmtChainP."Item No." = '' THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      // Stop EU.0120358.121710
      Item2G.GET(ReplcmtChainP."Item No.");
      WithoutReplcmtWindowG := TRUE;
      VALIDATE("No.", ReplcmtChainP."Item No.");
      WithoutReplcmtWindowG := FALSE;
      EXIT(TRUE);
      // Stop EU.0114873.116335
    END;

    PROCEDURE SetReplcmtWindow@10690900(ValueP@10690900 : Boolean);
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0106909.114669
      WithoutReplcmtWindowG := ValueP;
      // Stop EU.0106909.114669
    END;

      EU.0104321 12.08.20 MS Modification to properly calculate "VAT %" in case of 'Sales Tax' VAT calculation type
      EU.0104306 17.09.20 DR New option field "VAT Calculation Logic" used to skip the "Amount Including VAT" rounding adjustment.
                             Amount Rounding process restructured. With help of the new RunOrderLineRounding and UpdateVATAmountRounding functions the Amount Rounding process
                             is called only in the end of the first Amount influencing code trigger. Before it was called several times even from other triggers.
                             This avoids a double execution which caused problems and it also has a performance win.
                             Now functions AdjustRoundingRestOneVAT and TempTableUpdateLineVATAmountRounding can also put adjust VAT rounding differences on the Amount field.
                             - Allow the flexible manual modification of the "Amount", "Amount inclusive VAT" and Quantity field even for lines with Job numbers.
                             - Use SrvCustSplitMgmtG.UpdServLineCusFromServLine instead of SrvCustSplitMgmtG.UpdServLineCust_ServLine to inform the function about the current used field.
                             - New functions CalcOriginalAmount, UpdateLineSplittCalculation added.
                             - New fields adopted from IT solution: "VAT Difference Amount", "Manual VAT Amount", "VAT Amount", "Calculated VAT Amount", "Original Amount" and "Original Amount Incl. VAT"
                             - Function AdjustRoundingRestOneVAT redeveloped to consider new parameters from the General Ledger Setup.
                             - Consider new "Service VAT Rounding Adj." = "Directly when modify a Line" parameter to run the direct line adjustment or not.
                             - New FlowFields "Labors incl. Taxes", "Items incl. Taxes", "Ext. Services incl. Taxes", "G/L Accounts incl. Taxes"
                             - When an "Amount" or "Amount including VAT" is filled then a Quantity and Unit Price is mandatory.
